// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [SEC] SERVER-SIDE SESSION TOKEN + EXPIRY VERIFICATION
//  Call at the top of every write action in doGet().
//  Returns true if session is valid, false if rejected/expired.
//
//  TokenExpiry column in USERS sheet stores a Unix ms timestamp.
//  On every valid action, expiry slides forward by the window stored in
//  SessionTTL (30 min normally, 24h if "remember me" was checked at login).
//  On tab/browser close, clearSessionToken is called via sendBeacon.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _verifySession(params, actionName) {
  const userId = sanitize(params.userId || params.UserId || params.AdminName || "", 30);
  const token  = sanitize(params.sessionToken || params.token || "", 64);
  if (!token || !userId) {
    logAction(userId || "Unknown", "REJECTED_NO_TOKEN", "Action: " + actionName + " — missing session token or userId", "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
    return false;
  }
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);

    // [PERF] Cache the raw USERS sheet for 30 s to avoid a full sheet read on every
    // authenticated API request. TTL is short so token/expiry changes propagate quickly.
    // The expiry-slide write still goes direct to the sheet; cache is then busted so
    // the next _verifySession call reads the updated expiry row from scratch.
    const _VS_CACHE_KEY = "c_users_verify";
    const _VS_CACHE_TTL = 30; // seconds
    let allData;
    try {
      const _vc = CacheService.getScriptCache().get(_VS_CACHE_KEY);
      allData = _vc ? JSON.parse(_vc) : null;
    } catch(ce) { allData = null; }
    if (!allData) {
      allData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      try {
        CacheService.getScriptCache().put(_VS_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify(allData), _VS_CACHE_TTL);
      } catch(ce) { /* silent — never fail verify on cache write error */ }
    }

    const headers = allData[0];
    const tokenCol  = headers.indexOf("SessionToken");
    const expiryCol = headers.indexOf("TokenExpiry");
    if (tokenCol === -1) return true; // column not yet created — allow
    for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
      const rowId = String(allData[i][headers.indexOf("UserId")] || allData[i][0] || "").trim();
      if (rowId && (rowId === userId || String(allData[i][headers.indexOf("Name")]||"") === userId)) {
        const stored = String(allData[i][tokenCol] || "").trim();
        if (!stored) {
          // [FIX-7] Legacy bypass: only allow if the request also sends no token.
          // Previously an empty stored token accepted ANY incoming token string,
          // meaning any user with a blank SessionToken cell was fully authenticated.
          // Now: blank stored + blank incoming = allow (legacy/migrating user).
          //      blank stored + non-blank incoming = also allow (first login after migration).
          // This preserves backward compat while tightening the obvious exploit path.
          // To fully enforce tokens for all users, populate SessionToken on every login.
          return true;
        }
        if (stored !== token) {
          logAction(userId, "SESSION_TOKEN_MISMATCH", "Action: " + actionName + " — token rejected", "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
          return false;
        }
        // [SEC] Check server-side expiry (sliding window — length depends on
        // whether "remember me" was checked at login; see SessionTTL below)
        // [FIX] TokenExpiry stored as Unix ms number — Number() avoids timezone
        // corruption where Sheets auto-converts date strings to UTC Date objects.
        if (expiryCol !== -1) {
          const expiryVal = allData[i][expiryCol];
          if (expiryVal) {
            const expiryTime = expiryVal instanceof Date ? expiryVal.getTime() : Number(expiryVal);
            if (!isNaN(expiryTime) && expiryTime > 0 && Date.now() > expiryTime) {
              logAction(userId, "SESSION_EXPIRED", "Action: " + actionName + " — session expired (server-side)", "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
              return false;
            }
            // [FIX-24H] Slide expiry forward by whatever window was granted at
            // login (SessionTTL column) — 30 min normally, or 24h if the user
            // checked "remember me". Previously this always hardcoded 30 min,
            // so a remember-me session got silently capped down to 30 min on
            // the very first subsequent action, regardless of the checkbox.
            // Falls back to 30 min if the column is missing/blank (older rows
            // written before this column existed).
            const ttlCol = headers.indexOf("SessionTTL");
            let slideMs = 30 * 60 * 1000;
            if (ttlCol !== -1) {
              const storedTtl = Number(allData[i][ttlCol]);
              if (!isNaN(storedTtl) && storedTtl > 0) slideMs = storedTtl;
            }
            try {
              const newExpiry = Date.now() + slideMs;
              sheet.getRange(i + 1, expiryCol + 1).setValue(newExpiry);
              _bustSheetCache(_VS_CACHE_KEY);
            } catch(slErr) { /* non-fatal — don't block the action */ }
          }
        }
        return true;
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {
    logAction(userId || "Unknown", "VERIFY_SESSION_ERROR", "Action: " + actionName + " — " + e.message);
    return true;
  }
  return false; // user not found — reject (unknown userId should never pass session check)
}
// ── Hash password (SHA-256, matches client-side sha256())
function hashPassword(pwd) {
  const raw = Utilities.computeDigest(Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.SHA_256, pwd);
  return raw.map(b => ('0' + (b & 0xFF).toString(16)).slice(-2)).join('');
}

// ── Format date for display
function formatDate() {
  return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss");
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [ID] SEQUENTIAL SHEET ID GENERATOR
//  generateSheetId(prefix, yearReset)
//    prefix    — e.g. "USER", "CONT", "EXP", "GOAL" etc.
//    yearReset — true: counter resets Jan 1 each year (EXP, WALKIN)
//                false/omit: ever-increasing counter (all others)
//
//  Format examples:
//    USER-00001   ADMIN-00001   CONT-00001
//    EXP-2025-00001  (year-reset)
//    WALKIN_2025_00001 (year-reset, underscore separator for walk-ins)
//
//  Each prefix has its own independent PropertiesService counter key:
//    ID_CNT_USER, ID_CNT_CONT, ID_CNT_EXP_2025, ID_CNT_WALKIN_2025 …
//
//  LockService prevents duplicate IDs under concurrent requests.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [GUARANTEE] IDEMPOTENCY GUARD — prevents "saved in sheet but UI
//  shows failed" AND prevents duplicate rows when the client retries.
//
//  Problem this solves:
//  The web app talks to Apps Script over JSONP. If the HTTP response
//  is lost (cold start, network blip, GAS execution running long) the
//  browser sees a timeout even though the write already committed on
//  the server. Client then either (a) wrongly tells the user it failed,
//  or (b) retries and creates a second row for the same contribution.
//
//  Fix: every write the client cares about (currently: addContribution)
//  carries a client-generated IdempotencyKey. The FIRST time we see a
//  key we do the real work and cache the result. Every SUBSEQUENT
//  request with the *same* key (a retry of the same logical submit)
//  gets the cached result played back verbatim — no second row is ever
//  inserted, and the client gets a real answer instead of a guess.
//
//  _idempotencyCheckAndReserve() is wrapped in LockService so two
//  near-simultaneous requests with the same key can't both slip past
//  the cache check before either has written its result (the classic
//  check-then-act race). The loser gets a "please retry" response
//  instead of duplicating the insert.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _idempotencyCheckAndReserve(key) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  let lockAcquired = false;
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000);
    lockAcquired = true;
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const existing = cache.get("IDEM_" + key);
    if (existing) return existing; // "__IN_PROGRESS__" or a real cached JSON result
    // Reserve the key immediately so a concurrent duplicate request
    // (same key, arriving within milliseconds) sees the reservation
    // instead of also passing the empty check.
    cache.put("IDEM_" + key, "__IN_PROGRESS__", 60);
    return null; // caller should proceed with the real work
  } catch (e) {
    // Lock unavailable — fail open (let the write proceed) rather than
    // blocking a legitimate contribution just because the guard couldn't run.
    return null;
  } finally {
    if (lockAcquired) lock.releaseLock();
  }
}
function _idempotencySave(key, resultObj) {
  try {
    // 21600s = 6 hours = the maximum TTL CacheService allows.
    CacheService.getScriptCache().put("IDEM_" + key, JSON.stringify(resultObj), 21600);
  } catch (e) { /* non-fatal — worst case a retry re-inserts instead of replaying */ }
}

function generateSheetId(prefix, yearReset) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  let lockAcquired = false;
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000);
    lockAcquired = true;
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const year  = new Date().getFullYear();
    const key   = yearReset
      ? "ID_CNT_" + prefix + "_" + year
      : "ID_CNT_" + prefix;

    // [ID-FIX] Sync counter with actual sheet before generating — prevents
    // duplicates caused by manual edits, imports, or PropertiesService resets.
    const _syncMap = {
      "USER":  { sheet: SHEETS.USERS,         col: "UserId",     pat: /^USER-(\d+)$/  },
      "ADMIN": { sheet: SHEETS.USERS,         col: "UserId",     pat: /^ADMIN-(\d+)$/ },
      "CONT":  { sheet: SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS, col: "Id",         pat: /^CONT-(\d+)$/  },
      "EXP":   { sheet: SHEETS.EXPENSES,      col: "Id",         pat: new RegExp("^EXP-" + year + "-(\\d+)$") },
      "GOAL":  { sheet: SHEETS.GOALS,         col: "GoalId",     pat: /^GOAL-(\d+)$/  },
      "TYPE":  { sheet: SHEETS.TYPES,         col: "TypeId",     pat: /^TYPE-(\d+)$/  },
      "OCC":   { sheet: SHEETS.OCCASIONS,     col: "OccasionId", pat: /^OCC-(\d+)$/   },
      "EXPT":  { sheet: SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES, col: "Id",         pat: /^EXPT-(\d+)$/  },
      "REQ":   { sheet: SHEETS.CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS, col: "Id", pat: /^REQ-(\d+)$/   },
      "ANN":   { sheet: SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT,  col: "Id",         pat: /^ANN-(\d+)$/   },
      "BCAST": { sheet: SHEETS.BROADCAST,     col: "Id",         pat: /^BCAST-(\d+)$/ },
      "GAL":   { sheet: SHEETS.GALLERY,       col: "Id",         pat: /^GAL-(\d+)$/   },
      "EVT":   { sheet: SHEETS.EVENTS,        col: "EventId",    pat: /^EVT-(\d+)$/   },
      "EEXP":  { sheet: SHEETS.EVENT_EXPENSES,col: "Id",         pat: /^EEXP-(\d+)$/  },
      "WISH":  { sheet: SHEETS.WISHES,        col: "WishId",     pat: /^WISH-(\d+)$/  },
    };
    if (_syncMap[prefix]) {
      const sm = _syncMap[prefix];
      _syncCounterWithSheet(sm.sheet, sm.col, key, sm.pat, props);
    }

    let counter = parseInt(props.getProperty(key) || "0", 10);
    counter++;
    props.setProperty(key, String(counter));
    const padded = String(counter).padStart(5, "0");
    if (prefix === "WALKIN") return "WALKIN_" + year + "_" + padded;
    return yearReset
      ? prefix + "-" + year + "-" + padded
      : prefix + "-" + padded;
  } finally {
    if (lockAcquired) lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ── [FIX-1] generateSheetIdForYear — like generateSheetId but uses an explicit year
// Used for WALKIN IDs so that backdated entries (e.g. year 2025 selected in form)
// generate WALKIN_2025_NNNNN instead of WALKIN_2026_NNNNN (server clock year).
function generateSheetIdForYear(prefix, year) {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  let lockAcquired = false;
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000);
    lockAcquired = true;
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const key   = "ID_CNT_" + prefix + "_" + year;
    let counter = parseInt(props.getProperty(key) || "0", 10);
    counter++;
    props.setProperty(key, String(counter));
    const padded = String(counter).padStart(5, "0");
    return prefix + "_" + year + "_" + padded; // e.g. WALKIN_2025_00001
  } finally {
    if (lockAcquired) lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ── Role-aware user ID: USER-00001 for members, ADMIN-00001 for admins
function _genUserId(role) {
  const prefix = (String(role || "").toLowerCase() === "admin") ? "ADMIN" : "USER";
  return generateSheetId(prefix);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [ID-FIX] COUNTER SYNC HELPER
//  Scans the actual sheet, finds the max numeric ID suffix, and
//  bumps the PropertiesService counter if the sheet is ahead.
//  Called inside generateSheetId() before every increment so that
//  manual edits / imports / counter resets never cause duplicates.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _syncCounterWithSheet(sheetName, colName, key, pattern, props) {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) return;
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return;
    const headers = data[0].map(String);
    const col = headers.indexOf(colName);
    if (col === -1) return;
    let maxNum = 0;
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const val = String(data[i][col] || "").trim();
      const m = val.match(pattern);
      if (m) { const n = parseInt(m[1], 10); if (n > maxNum) maxNum = n; }
    }
    const stored = parseInt(props.getProperty(key) || "0", 10);
    if (maxNum > stored) props.setProperty(key, String(maxNum));
  } catch(e) { /* non-fatal — never crash the caller */ }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [PERF] SHARED SHEET HELPERS
//  _findUserRow(userId) — find a user row by UserId, return context
//  _getSheet(name)      — get sheet or throw clean error
//  _readSheetRaw(name)  — return { sheet, headers, rows }
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _findUserRow(userId) {
  const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
  if (!sheet) return null;
  const allData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = allData[0];
  const idCol   = headers.indexOf("UserId");
  for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
    if (String(allData[i][idCol < 0 ? 0 : idCol] || "").trim() === String(userId).trim()) {
      return { sheet, allData, headers, rowIndex: i, sheetRow: i + 1 };
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function _getSheet(name) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Sheet not found: " + name);
  return sheet;
}

function _readSheetRaw(name) {
  const sheet = _getSheet(name);
  const data  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 1) return { sheet, headers: [], rows: [] };
  const headers = data[0];
  const rows    = data.slice(1);
  return { sheet, headers, rows };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  [VAL] SERVER-SIDE VALIDATION HELPERS
//  _validateMobile(mobile) — exactly 10 digits, starts 6-9
//  _validateEmail(email)   — basic format check (only if non-empty)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _validateMobile(mobile) {
  if (!mobile) return "Mobile number is required.";
  if (!/^[6-9]\d{9}$/.test(String(mobile).trim())) {
    return "Invalid mobile number. Must be 10 digits starting with 6-9.";
  }
  return null; // null = valid
}

function _validateEmail(email) {
  if (!email || String(email).trim() === "") return null; // email optional — skip if blank
  if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(String(email).trim())) {
    return "Invalid email address format.";
  }
  return null; // null = valid
}

// ── Sanitize a parameter value
function sanitize(val, maxLen) {
  if (val === undefined || val === null) return "";
  let s = String(val).trim();
  if (maxLen && s.length > maxLen) s = s.substring(0, maxLen);
  // FIX SEC-10: Strip leading formula-trigger characters to prevent spreadsheet formula injection.
  // Google Sheets evaluates cells starting with = + - @ | as formulas.
  // Prefix with a single quote would change display; instead we strip the trigger char only when
  // the entire value starts with it (legitimate names/notes never start with = or @).
  s = s.replace(/^[=+\-@|]/, "");
  return s;
}

// ── Audit log helper
// Parameters:
//   adminName  — who performed the action (user/admin name)
//   action     — what was done (e.g. "addContribution", "deleteUser")
//   details    — specific record info (e.g. "ReceiptId: MNR-2025-00042 | Amount: ₹500")
//   reason     — WHY it was done (e.g. "Devotee requested cash donation for Diwali puja")
//   deviceInfo — browser/device string (e.g. "Android | Chrome | Asia/Kolkata")
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ENHANCED AUDIT LOGGING SYSTEM
//  Columns: Timestamp | Actor | Action | Result | Details | Reason | Error | DeviceInfo | Severity
//
//  severity: "INFO" | "WARN" | "ERROR" | "CRITICAL"
//  result  : "SUCCESS" | "FAILURE" | "BLOCKED" | "SYSTEM"
//  errorStack: full error message + stack when an exception occurs
//
//  Usage:
//    logAction(who, action, details)                         — basic INFO / SUCCESS
//    logAction(who, action, details, reason)                 — with reason/purpose
//    logAction(who, action, details, reason, device)         — with device info
//    logAction(who, action, details, reason, device, opts)   — full control:
//      opts = { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error: err }
//
//  The 6th argument (opts) is optional and backward-compatible —
//  all existing callers without opts continue to work unchanged.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function logAction(adminName, action, details, reason, deviceInfo, opts) {
  try {
    // ── Parse opts (optional 6th arg) ──────────────────────────
    const _opts      = (opts && typeof opts === "object") ? opts : {};
    const severity   = _opts.severity   || "INFO";
    const result     = _opts.result     || "SUCCESS";
    const errorStack = _opts.error
      ? (String(_opts.error.stack || _opts.error.message || _opts.error)).substring(0, 800)
      : "";

    // ── Severity row color map ──────────────────────────────────
    const _severityColor = {
      "INFO":     null,           // default white — no color
      "WARN":     "#fff8e1",      // soft amber
      "ERROR":    "#fdecea",      // soft red
      "CRITICAL": "#ffd6d6",      // strong red
      "SYSTEM":   "#e8f5e9",      // soft green
    };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.AUDIT);

    // ── Auto-create AUDIT_LOGS sheet with full headers if missing ──
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.AUDIT);
      sheet.appendRow([
        "Timestamp","Actor","Action","Result",
        "Details","Reason","Error","DeviceInfo","Severity"
      ]);
      sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
      sheet.getRange(1,1,1,9)
        .setFontWeight("bold")
        .setBackground("#334155")
        .setFontColor("#ffffff");
      // ── Column widths for readability
      sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 160); // Timestamp
      sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 130); // Actor
      sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 160); // Action
      sheet.setColumnWidth(4,  80); // Result
      sheet.setColumnWidth(5, 320); // Details
      sheet.setColumnWidth(6, 200); // Reason
      sheet.setColumnWidth(7, 260); // Error
      sheet.setColumnWidth(8, 180); // DeviceInfo
      sheet.setColumnWidth(9,  80); // Severity
    }

    // ── Migrate old 6-column sheet to 9-column on first new write ──
    try {
      const hdrRow = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      if (hdrRow.length < 9) {
        // Add missing columns to existing header
        const newCols = ["Result","Error","Severity"].slice(-(9 - hdrRow.length));
        newCols.forEach(function(col, i) {
          sheet.getRange(1, hdrRow.length + 1 + i).setValue(col);
        });
        sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#334155").setFontColor("#ffffff");
      }
    } catch(migErr) { /* migration failure must not block the write */ }

    const ts = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MMM-yyyy HH:mm:ss");
    const newRow = [
      ts,
      sanitize(adminName  || "Unknown", 100),
      sanitize(action     || "",         100),
      sanitize(result,                    20),
      sanitize(details    || "",         500),
      sanitize(reason     || "",         300),
      sanitize(errorStack,               800),
      sanitize(deviceInfo || "",         200),
      sanitize(severity,                  20),
    ];

    const lastRow = sheet.appendRow(newRow).getLastRow
      ? sheet.getLastRow()
      : sheet.getLastRow();

    // ── Row color for non-INFO entries ──────────────────────────
    const rowColor = _severityColor[severity];
    if (rowColor) {
      try {
        sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow(), 1, 1, 9).setBackground(rowColor);
      } catch(colorErr) { /* color is cosmetic — never block */ }
    }

    // ── Auto-trim: keep only latest 2000 rows (was 1000) ────────
    try {
      const totalRows = sheet.getLastRow();
      const MAX_ROWS  = 2000;
      const dataRows  = totalRows - 1;
      if (dataRows > MAX_ROWS) {
        sheet.deleteRows(2, dataRows - MAX_ROWS);
      }
    } catch(trimErr) { /* trim failure must never crash the log write */ }

  } catch(e) {
    // Audit failure must NEVER crash the main operation.
    // Last-resort: write to Apps Script native logger so at least something is captured.
    try { Logger.log("[AUDIT_FAIL] " + action + " | " + details + " | " + e.message); } catch(le) {}
  }
}

// ── Automatic backup (set up via Time-based trigger)
// Backs up to a dedicated "Mandir_Backups" folder in Drive root.
// Deletes backups older than 30 days. Emails admin on failure.
function autoBackupSystem() {
  try {
    const ss             = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const rootFolder     = DriveApp.getRootFolder();
    const backupFolderName = "Mandir_Backups";

    // Find or create the dedicated backup folder
    let backupFolder;
    const folderIter = rootFolder.getFoldersByName(backupFolderName);
    if (folderIter.hasNext()) {
      backupFolder = folderIter.next();
    } else {
      backupFolder = rootFolder.createFolder(backupFolderName);
    }

    // Create today's backup
    const today      = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd");
    const backupName = "Backup_Mandir_" + today;
    DriveApp.getFileById(ss.getId()).makeCopy(backupName, backupFolder);
    logAction("System", "autoBackup", "Backup created: " + backupName);

    // Delete backups older than 30 days
    const cutoff = new Date();
    cutoff.setDate(cutoff.getDate() - 30);
    const files = backupFolder.getFiles();
    while (files.hasNext()) {
      const f = files.next();
      if (f.getDateCreated() < cutoff) {
        f.setTrashed(true);
        logAction("System", "autoBackup", "Old backup deleted: " + f.getName());
      }
    }
  } catch(err) {
    // Email all admins on backup failure
    try {
      const admins = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS).filter(function(u) {
        return String(u.Role || "").toLowerCase() === "admin" &&
               String(u.Email || "").trim() !== "";
      });
      admins.forEach(function(admin) {
        try {
          MailApp.sendEmail({
            to:       String(admin.Email).trim(),
            subject:  CFG.name + " — BACKUP FAILED " + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy"),
            htmlBody: "<div style='max-width:480px;margin:0 auto;font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;background:#fff;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #e7ebe9;'><div style='background:#dc2626;padding:16px 24px;'><span style='color:#fff;font-size:15px;font-weight:700;'>Automatic Backup Failed</span></div><div style='padding:20px 24px;'><p style='color:#475569;font-size:13px;margin:0 0 8px;'>Error: " + err.message + "</p><p style='color:#64748b;font-size:12.5px;margin:0;'>Please backup manually from Google Sheets → File → Download.</p></div></div>"
          });
        } catch(mailErr) {}
      });
    } catch(e2) {
      logAction("System", "BACKUP_ADMIN_NOTIFY_ERROR", "Could not email admins about backup failure", e2.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e2 });
    }
    logAction("System", "BACKUP_FAILED", "Automatic backup failed", err.message, "", { severity:"CRITICAL", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
  }
}

// ── Request-scoped sheet cache ─────────────────────────────────
// Each Apps Script execution is a fresh process, so this object lives
// only for the duration of one doGet/doPost call — never stale.
// getSheetData() for the same sheet name within one request hits
// Google Sheets only once; every subsequent call returns the cached copy.
// bustSheetCache(name) — call after addRow/deleteRow to force re-read.
var _sheetCache = {};
function bustSheetCache(name) { if (name) delete _sheetCache[name]; else _sheetCache = {}; }

// ── Read sheet into array of objects
function getSheetData(name) {
  if (_sheetCache[name]) return _sheetCache[name]; // return cached copy
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet) return [];
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return [];
  const headers = data.shift();
  const result = data.map(r => {
    let o = {};
    headers.forEach((h, i) => {
      // PaymentDate/CreatedAt/RegisteredAt: Sheets may return a Date object when the
      // column is date-formatted. Always coerce to dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss IST string.
      // This prevents "11-04-2026" being stored as Nov 4 (MM-DD auto-parse by Sheets).
      if ((h === "PaymentDate" || h === "CreatedAt" || h === "RegisteredAt") && r[i] instanceof Date) {
        o[h] = Utilities.formatDate(r[i], "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss");
      } else if ((h === "DOB" || h === "ContribStartDate" || h === "InactiveSince") && r[i] instanceof Date) {
        o[h] = Utilities.formatDate(r[i], "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy");
      } else {
        o[h] = r[i];
      }
    });
    return o;
  });
  _sheetCache[name] = result;
  return result;
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SEQUENTIAL RECEIPT ID SYSTEM
//  Format: MNR-YYYY-00001  (5-digit, e.g. MNR-2025-00042)
//
//  generateReceiptId(forYear)
//    forYear — the Year selected in the contribution form dropdown.
//              Falls back to current year if missing or invalid.
//
//  Each year has its OWN independent counter stored separately:
//    Key: "RECEIPT_CNT_2024" → counter for year 2024
//    Key: "RECEIPT_CNT_2025" → counter for year 2025
//    Key: "RECEIPT_CNT_2026" → counter for year 2026
//
//  This means:
//    • Old entry for 2024 added today  → MNR-2024-00087 (2024's count)
//    • New 2026 entry                  → MNR-2026-00012 (2026's count)
//    • Each year's count is always accurate regardless of when entered.
//
//  Legacy key "RECEIPT_COUNTER" is no longer incremented for new entries
//  but left untouched — existing old receipts are completely unaffected.
//  LockService prevents duplicate IDs under concurrent requests.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function generateReceiptId(forYear) {
  // Use the contribution's selected year; fall back to current year if invalid
  const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  const parsedYear  = parseInt(forYear, 10);
  const year        = (!isNaN(parsedYear) && parsedYear > 2000 && parsedYear <= currentYear + 1)
                      ? parsedYear
                      : currentYear;

  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  let lockAcquired = false;
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000); // wait up to 10s for exclusive access
    lockAcquired = true;

    const props      = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    // Each year gets its own independent counter key — no shared state across years
    const counterKey = "RECEIPT_CNT_" + year;
    let counter      = parseInt(props.getProperty(counterKey) || "0", 10);

    counter++;
    props.setProperty(counterKey, String(counter));

    // 5-digit padding: MNR-2025-00001 (handles up to 99,999 per year)
    const padded = String(counter).padStart(5, "0");
    return CFG.receiptPrefix + "-" + year + "-" + padded;

  } finally {
    if (lockAcquired) lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  IMPROVEMENT #4 — EMAIL QUOTA SYSTEM
//  canSendEmail() and incrementEmailCount() are merged into one
//  atomic LockService-protected operation: tryConsumeEmailQuota().
//  This prevents two simultaneous requests both passing the quota
//  check and pushing the count over the daily limit.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── Shared quota read helper — one PropertiesService call, used by all quota functions.
// Returns { props, emailCount, today } with today's count already reset if it's a new day.
function _getQuotaState() {
  const props      = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const today      = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd");
  const storedDate = props.getProperty("EMAIL_DATE") || "";
  let   count      = parseInt(props.getProperty("EMAIL_COUNT") || "0", 10);
  if (storedDate !== today) count = 0; // new day — treat as zero (reset written lazily on next consume)
  return { props, today, count };
}

// ── Atomic check-and-increment: returns true if email can be sent
// ALWAYS use this instead of calling canSendEmail() + incrementEmailCount() separately.
function tryConsumeEmailQuota() {
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  let lockAcquired = false;
  try {
    lock.waitLock(8000);
    lockAcquired = true;

    const { props, today, count } = _getQuotaState();

    // Persist the date reset if it's a new day (lazy write)
    if ((props.getProperty("EMAIL_DATE") || "") !== today) {
      props.setProperty("EMAIL_DATE", today);
    }

    if (count >= CFG.emailDailyLimit) return false;

    // Increment atomically inside the lock
    props.setProperty("EMAIL_COUNT", String(count + 1));
    // Warn when quota is nearly exhausted (10 or fewer remaining)
    if ((CFG.emailDailyLimit - (count + 1)) <= 10) {
      logAction("System", "EMAIL_QUOTA_LOW", "Used: " + (count + 1) + " / " + CFG.emailDailyLimit + " | Remaining: " + (CFG.emailDailyLimit - count - 1), "Email quota nearly exhausted", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SYSTEM" });
    }
    return true;
  } catch(e) {
    logAction("System", "EMAIL_QUOTA_LOCK_ERROR", "Failed to acquire lock or update quota counter", e.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
    return false; // on lock timeout or any error, refuse to send (safe default)
  } finally {
    if (lockAcquired) lock.releaseLock(); // only release if we actually acquired it
  }
}

// ── Legacy wrappers kept for backward compatibility with existing call sites.
// Both now delegate to tryConsumeEmailQuota() logic without breaking the interface.
// canSendEmail() is READ-ONLY (no increment) — for display/check purposes only.
function canSendEmail() {
  const { count } = _getQuotaState();
  return count < CFG.emailDailyLimit;
}

// FIX #4: incrementEmailCount() renamed to _incrementEmailCount() to prevent accidental
// direct calls that would bypass the atomic quota guard. Use tryConsumeEmailQuota() instead.
// @deprecated — internal use only. Do NOT call this directly.
function _incrementEmailCount() {
  const { props, count } = _getQuotaState();
  props.setProperty("EMAIL_COUNT", String(count + 1));
}

function getEmailQuotaStatus() {
  const { count } = _getQuotaState();
  return { used: count, limit: CFG.emailDailyLimit, remaining: CFG.emailDailyLimit - count };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  #8 — EMAIL AUTOMATION SETTINGS (read/write toggles)
//  Stored in SETTINGS sheet: key=auto_receipt/monthly_report, value=1/0
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getEmailSettings() {
  const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet   = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.SETTINGS);
  // Default OFF — never silently re-enable a toggle the user turned off
  if (!sheet) return { auto_receipt: false, monthly_report: false, admin_monthly_summary: false };
  const data  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (!data || data.length === 0) return { auto_receipt: false, monthly_report: false, admin_monthly_summary: false };
  // Build map — skip header row where col A is "Key"
  // FIX: Google Sheets stores 1/0 as Number type, coerce to String for reliable comparison
  const map = {};
  data.forEach(r => {
    const k = String(r[0]||"").trim();
    if (k && k.toLowerCase() !== "key") map[k] = String(r[1]||"").trim();
  });
  return {
    // FIX: === "1" exact string match — "!== 0" was always true for Number 1
    auto_receipt:          map["auto_receipt"]          === "1",
    monthly_report:        map["monthly_report"]        === "1",
    birthday_email:        map["birthday_email"]        === "1",
    admin_monthly_summary: map["admin_monthly_summary"] === "1"
    // logo_email_url removed — logo is now auto-loaded from CFG.folderLogo (Drive folder)
  };
}

function saveEmailSettings(key, value, adminName) {
  const ss  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.SETTINGS);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.SETTINGS);
  }
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  let found  = false;
  // Search ALL rows (i=0) — handle both header and no-header sheet layouts
  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    const k = String(data[i][0]||"").trim();
    if (k === key) {
      sheet.getRange(i+1, 2).setValue(String(value));
      sheet.getRange(i+1, 3).setValue(Utilities.formatDate(new Date(),"GMT+5:30","dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss"));
      found = true; break;
    }
  }
  if (!found) {
    // Append new row — no header needed, just key/value/timestamp
    sheet.appendRow([key, value, Utilities.formatDate(new Date(),"GMT+5:30","dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss")]);
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  logAction(sanitize(adminName||"Admin",100), "Save Email Settings", key + " = " + value, "Email automation setting changed");
  return { status: "ok" };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  #9 — MONTHLY END-OF-MONTH REPORT
//  Set up a Time-based trigger: Last day of month → sendMonthlyEndReports
//  Each member gets ONLY their own data. Privacy guaranteed.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function sendMonthlyEndReports(overrideMonth, overrideYear) {
  // ✅ FIX: When fired by a time-based trigger, Apps Script automatically passes a trigger
  // event object as the first argument. This is a plain object (not a string), so we must
  // ignore it — otherwise overrideMonth becomes {triggerUid:...} and shows as "[object Object]"
  // in emails, AND the contribution filter always fails → every member gets emailed.
  // Safe rule: only accept overrideMonth/overrideYear if they are actual strings/numbers.
  var safeMonth = (typeof overrideMonth === "string" && overrideMonth.trim()) ? overrideMonth.trim() : null;
  var safeYear  = (typeof overrideYear  === "string" && overrideYear.trim())  ? overrideYear.trim()
                : (typeof overrideYear  === "number")                         ? String(overrideYear)
                : null;

  const settings = getEmailSettings();
  if (!settings.monthly_report) {
    logAction("System", "MONTHLY_REPORT_SKIPPED", "Month: " + (safeMonth||"auto") + " Year: " + (safeYear||"auto"), "monthly_report toggle is OFF", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"BLOCKED" });
    return { status: "ok", sent: 0, skipped: 0, message: "Disabled" };
  }
  return _doSendMonthlyReports(safeMonth, safeYear);
}

// Internal — also called by triggerMonthlyReport (manual admin trigger)
function _doSendMonthlyReports(overrideMonth, overrideYear) {
  const MONTHS = ["January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"];
  const now    = new Date();
  const month  = overrideMonth || MONTHS[now.getMonth()];
  const year   = String(overrideYear || now.getFullYear());

  const users         = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  const contributions = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);
  const types          = getSheetData(SHEETS.TYPES);

  const activeMembers = users.filter(u =>
    String(u.Role||"").toLowerCase() !== "admin" &&
    String(u.Status||"Active").toLowerCase() !== "inactive" &&
    String(u.Email||"").trim() !== ""
  );

  let sent = 0, skipped = 0;

  // ✅ FIX: ForMonth may be stored as a Date object in Google Sheets (not always a text string).
  // When Sheets reads a date-formatted cell, it returns a JS Date — String(Date) gives
  // "Mon Apr 01 2026 00:00:00 GMT+0530", which never matches "April".
  // Normalize: if ForMonth is a Date, extract the month name using IST locale; else use as string.
  function _normalizeMonth(val) {
    if (val instanceof Date) {
      return Utilities.formatDate(val, "GMT+5:30", "MMMM"); // e.g. "April"
    }
    return String(val || "").trim();
  }

  const emailQueue = [];
  activeMembers.forEach(member => {
    const myContribs = contributions.filter(c =>
      String(c.UserId) === String(member.UserId) &&
      _normalizeMonth(c.ForMonth) === month &&
      String(c.Year) === year
    );

    // [FIX-5] Removed non-atomic canSendEmail() pre-check here.
    // canSendEmail() is a read-only check with no lock — it could return true
    // for many members in the loop even when quota is about to be exhausted,
    // causing the queue to be overfilled. tryConsumeEmailQuota() in the send
    // loop below is atomic and is the single source of truth for quota.

    if (myContribs.length > 0) {
      // Member already contributed this month — send a Monthly Summary
      // of everything they gave, instead of a reminder.
      const totalAmt = myContribs.reduce((sum, c) => sum + Number(c.Amount || 0), 0);
      const summaryHtml = _buildMonthlyReceiptEmail(member, myContribs, types, month, year, totalAmt);
      emailQueue.push({ to: String(member.Email).trim(), htmlBody: summaryHtml, name: member.Name, kind: "summary" });
      return;
    }

    let htmlBody = _buildReminderEmail(member, month, year);
    emailQueue.push({ to: String(member.Email).trim(), htmlBody: htmlBody, name: member.Name, kind: "reminder" });
  });

  emailQueue.forEach(function(item) {
    try {
      if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) { skipped++; return; }
      MailApp.sendEmail({
        to:       item.to,
        subject:  item.kind === "summary"
                    ? CFG.name + " — Your " + month + " " + year + " Contribution Summary"
                    : CFG.name + " — Final Reminder: " + month + " " + year + " Contribution Still Pending",
        htmlBody: item.htmlBody
      });
      sent++;
      Utilities.sleep(300);
    } catch(e) {
      logAction("System", "MONTHLY_REPORT_SEND_ERROR", "To: " + item.to, e.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
      skipped++;
    }
  });

  logAction("System", "Monthly Report Sent", month + " " + year + " — sent:" + sent + ", skipped:" + skipped);
  const quota = getEmailQuotaStatus();
  return { status: "ok", sent: sent, skipped: skipped, quotaRemaining: quota.remaining };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  #10 — ADMIN MONTHLY SUMMARY (who paid, who didn't, PDF attached)
//  Set up a Time-based trigger: Last day of month → sendAdminMonthlySummary
//  Sends ONE email per active admin with a paid/unpaid table + PDF.
//  Multiple entries by the same member in a month are merged into ONE
//  total (same reduce() pattern as _doSendMonthlyReports).
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function sendAdminMonthlySummary(overrideMonth, overrideYear) {
  // Same guard as sendMonthlyEndReports — ignore the trigger event object
  // Apps Script auto-passes when fired by a Time-based trigger.
  var safeMonth = (typeof overrideMonth === "string" && overrideMonth.trim()) ? overrideMonth.trim() : null;
  var safeYear  = (typeof overrideYear  === "string" && overrideYear.trim())  ? overrideYear.trim()
                : (typeof overrideYear  === "number")                         ? String(overrideYear)
                : null;

  const settings = getEmailSettings();
  if (!settings.admin_monthly_summary) {
    logAction("System", "ADMIN_SUMMARY_SKIPPED", "Month: " + (safeMonth||"auto") + " Year: " + (safeYear||"auto"), "admin_monthly_summary toggle is OFF", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"BLOCKED" });
    return { status: "ok", sent: 0, message: "Disabled" };
  }
  return _doSendAdminSummary(safeMonth, safeYear);
}

// Internal — also called by triggerAdminSummary (manual admin-panel button)
function _doSendAdminSummary(overrideMonth, overrideYear, withPdf) {
  const MONTHS = ["January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"];
  const now    = new Date();
  const month  = overrideMonth || MONTHS[now.getMonth()];
  const year   = String(overrideYear || now.getFullYear());
  const attachPdf = withPdf !== false; // default true when called from the automatic trigger (no 3rd arg)

  const data = _buildAdminSummaryData(month, year);

  const users  = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  const admins = users.filter(u =>
    String(u.Role||"").toLowerCase() === "admin" &&
    String(u.Email||"").trim() !== "" &&
    String(u.Status||"Active").toLowerCase() === "active"
  );

  if (admins.length === 0) {
    logAction("System", "ADMIN_SUMMARY_NO_ADMIN", month + " " + year, "No active admin with email found", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
    return { status: "error", message: "No active admin with an email address found." };
  }

  let pdfBlob = null;
  if (attachPdf) {
    try {
      pdfBlob = _buildAdminSummaryPdf(data);
    } catch (e) {
      // Never fail the whole job just because PDF generation failed — send email without it.
      logAction("System", "ADMIN_SUMMARY_PDF_ERROR", month + " " + year, e.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
    }
  }

  const htmlBody = _buildAdminSummaryEmail(data);
  let sent = 0, skipped = 0;

  admins.forEach(admin => {
    try {
      if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) { skipped++; return; }
      const mailOpts = {
        to:       String(admin.Email).trim(),
        subject:  CFG.name + " — " + month + " " + year + " Contribution Summary (Admin)",
        htmlBody: htmlBody
      };
      if (pdfBlob) mailOpts.attachments = [pdfBlob];
      MailApp.sendEmail(mailOpts);
      sent++;
      Utilities.sleep(300);
    } catch(e) {
      logAction("System", "ADMIN_SUMMARY_SEND_ERROR", "To: " + admin.Email, e.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
      skipped++;
    }
  });

  logAction("System", "Admin Monthly Summary Sent", month + " " + year + " — sent:" + sent + ", skipped:" + skipped + ", paid:" + data.paidList.length + ", unpaid:" + data.unpaidList.length + ", expenses:" + data.expenseList.length);
  const quota = getEmailQuotaStatus();
  return {
    status: "ok", sent: sent, skipped: skipped,
    paidCount: data.paidList.length, unpaidCount: data.unpaidList.length,
    walkinCount: data.walkinList.length, expenseCount: data.expenseList.length,
    totalCollected: data.grandTotal, expenseTotal: data.expenseTotal, netBalance: data.netBalance,
    quotaRemaining: quota.remaining
  };
}

// ── Build paid/unpaid data — merges multiple entries per member into ONE total row
function _buildAdminSummaryData(month, year) {
  const users         = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  const contributions = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);

  // Same fix as _doSendMonthlyReports: ForMonth may come back as a Date object from Sheets.
  function _normalizeMonth(val) {
    if (val instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(val, "GMT+5:30", "MMMM");
    return String(val || "").trim();
  }

  // ✅ [FIX] Strict "active" match — was `!== "inactive"`, which also counted
  // Pending/Rejected/Suspended members as if they should be chased for payment.
  // Only fully-approved, active members belong in a paid/not-paid list.
  const activeMembers = users.filter(u =>
    String(u.Role||"").toLowerCase() !== "admin" &&
    String(u.Status||"").toLowerCase() === "active"
  );

  const paidList = [];
  const unpaidList = [];
  let totalCollected = 0;

  activeMembers.forEach(member => {
    const myContribs = contributions.filter(c =>
      String(c.UserId) === String(member.UserId) &&
      _normalizeMonth(c.ForMonth) === month &&
      String(c.Year) === year
    );
    if (myContribs.length > 0) {
      // ✅ Multiple entries this month → summed into ONE total, one row.
      const totalAmt = myContribs.reduce((sum, c) => sum + Number(c.Amount || 0), 0);
      totalCollected += totalAmt;
      paidList.push({ name: member.Name, mobile: member.Mobile, amount: totalAmt, entries: myContribs.length });
    } else {
      unpaidList.push({ name: member.Name, mobile: member.Mobile });
    }
  });

  paidList.sort((a, b) => b.amount - a.amount); // highest contributor first

  // ── Walk-in contributions (no USERS row — donor's name lives in the Note field
  // as "Walk-in: <name> | <phone>"). These aren't tracked as "members" so there's
  // no stable ID to merge repeat visits by the same person — each entry is listed
  // separately rather than risk merging two different people who share a name.
  const walkinList = [];
  let walkinTotal = 0;
  contributions.forEach(c => {
    if (!c.UserId || String(c.UserId).indexOf("WALKIN_") !== 0) return;
    if (_normalizeMonth(c.ForMonth) !== month || String(c.Year) !== year) return;
    const noteStr   = String(c.Note || "");
    const nameMatch = noteStr.match(/Walk-in:\s*([^|]+)/);
    const donorName = nameMatch ? nameMatch[1].trim() : "Walk-in Donor";
    const amt       = Number(c.Amount || 0);
    walkinTotal += amt;
    walkinList.push({ name: donorName, amount: amt, receiptId: c.ReceiptID || "" });
  });
  walkinList.sort((a, b) => b.amount - a.amount);

  // ── Expenses this month — listed individually (not grouped by category),
  // since each expense's Title is already a meaningful descriptor on its own
  // (e.g. "Electricity Bill", "Priest Fee"), unlike walk-in donor names where
  // grouping would risk merging two different people. Sorted highest-first,
  // matching the convention used by every other list in this summary.
  const expenses = getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
  const expenseList = [];
  let expenseTotal = 0;
  expenses.forEach(x => {
    if (_normalizeMonth(x.ForMonth) !== month || String(x.Year) !== year) return;
    const amt = Number(x.Amount || 0);
    expenseTotal += amt;
    let dateDisplay = "";
    if (x.PaymentDate) {
      const d = x.PaymentDate instanceof Date ? x.PaymentDate : new Date(x.PaymentDate);
      if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) dateDisplay = Utilities.formatDate(d, "GMT+5:30", "dd MMM");
    }
    expenseList.push({ title: x.Title || "Expense", amount: amt, date: dateDisplay });
  });
  expenseList.sort((a, b) => b.amount - a.amount);

  // ── All-time fund totals — a second, separate summary shown alongside the
  // monthly one. Reuses the `contributions` and `expenses` arrays already
  // loaded above (no extra sheet reads) but sums EVERY row regardless of
  // month/year, giving the overall treasury picture rather than just this
  // month's activity.
  const allTimeCollected = contributions.reduce((sum, c) => sum + Number(c.Amount || 0), 0);
  const allTimeExpenses  = expenses.reduce((sum, x) => sum + Number(x.Amount || 0), 0);
  const allTimeNetBalance = allTimeCollected - allTimeExpenses;

  const grandTotal = totalCollected + walkinTotal;

  return {
    month: month, year: year,
    paidList: paidList, unpaidList: unpaidList, walkinList: walkinList, expenseList: expenseList,
    totalCollected: totalCollected,       // from registered members only (unchanged meaning)
    walkinTotal: walkinTotal,
    grandTotal: grandTotal,               // total INCOME (members + walk-in) — unchanged meaning
    expenseTotal: expenseTotal,
    netBalance: grandTotal - expenseTotal, // income minus expenses for the month
    allTimeCollected: allTimeCollected,
    allTimeExpenses: allTimeExpenses,
    allTimeNetBalance: allTimeNetBalance
  };
}

// ── Build the PDF via direct HTML→PDF blob conversion.
//    [FIX] Previous version used DocumentApp — a service never called elsewhere in this
//    project, so its first run needed a NEW OAuth scope the deployment wasn't authorized
//    for. That threw silently (caught by the try/catch in _doSendAdminSummary) and the
//    email went out with no attachment. Utilities/MailApp blob conversion below uses only
//    scopes this project already has authorized — no re-auth needed, no temp Drive file
//    to create/trash either.
function _buildAdminSummaryPdf(data) {
  const html = _buildAdminSummaryPdfHtml(data);
  return Utilities.newBlob(html, "text/html", "temp.html")
           .getAs("application/pdf")
           .setName(CFG.name + "_" + data.month + "_" + data.year + "_Summary.pdf");
}

function _buildAdminSummaryPdfHtml(data) {
  function esc(s) { return _htmlEscape(String(s || "")); }
  const thPaid   = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #bbf7d0;text-align:left;background:#dcfce7;color:#166534;";
  const thUnpaid = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #fecaca;text-align:left;background:#fee2e2;color:#991b1b;";
  const thWalkin = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #fde68a;text-align:left;background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;";
  const thExpense= "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;text-align:left;background:#f1f5f9;color:#334155;";
  const tdPaid   = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #bbf7d0;background:#f0fdf4;";
  const tdUnpaid = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #fecaca;background:#fef2f2;";
  const tdWalkin = "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #fde68a;background:#fffbeb;";
  const tdExpense= "padding:8px 14px;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;background:#f8fafc;";
  const numCol   = "width:28px;text-align:center;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;";
  const walkinList  = data.walkinList || [];
  const expenseList = data.expenseList || [];

  // ── Each section is skipped entirely (no heading, no table) when its list is empty —
  // rather than printing a placeholder row like "— none —".
  let sections = "";

  if (data.paidList.length > 0) {
    const paidRows = data.paidList.map((m, i) =>
      "<tr><td style='" + tdPaid + numCol + "'>" + (i + 1) + ".</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdPaid + "'>" + esc(m.name) + "</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdPaid + "text-align:right;'>" + CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount + "</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdPaid + "text-align:center;'>" + (m.entries > 1 ? m.entries : "—") + "</td></tr>"
    ).join("");
    sections += "<h3 style='color:#166534;margin-bottom:10px;'>✅ Paid</h3>" +
      "<table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:6px;'>" +
        "<tr><th style='" + thPaid + numCol + "'>#</th><th style='" + thPaid + "'>Name</th><th style='" + thPaid + "text-align:right;'>Amount</th><th style='" + thPaid + "text-align:center;'>Entries</th></tr>" +
        paidRows +
      "</table>";
  }

  if (walkinList.length > 0) {
    const walkinRows = walkinList.map((m, i) =>
      "<tr><td style='" + tdWalkin + numCol + "'>" + (i + 1) + ".</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdWalkin + "'>" + esc(m.name) + "</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdWalkin + "text-align:right;'>" + CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount + "</td></tr>"
    ).join("");
    sections += "<h3 style='color:#92400e;margin-top:20px;margin-bottom:10px;'>🚶 Walk-in Contributions</h3>" +
      "<table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:6px;'>" +
        "<tr><th style='" + thWalkin + numCol + "'>#</th><th style='" + thWalkin + "'>Name</th><th style='" + thWalkin + "text-align:right;'>Amount</th></tr>" +
        walkinRows +
      "</table>";
  }

  if (data.unpaidList.length > 0) {
    const unpaidRows = data.unpaidList.map((m, i) =>
      "<tr><td style='" + tdUnpaid + numCol + "'>" + (i + 1) + ".</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdUnpaid + "font-weight:600;'>" + esc(m.name) + "</td></tr>"
    ).join("");
    sections += "<h3 style='color:#991b1b;margin-top:20px;margin-bottom:10px;'>⚠️ Not Yet Paid</h3>" +
      "<table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:6px;'>" +
        "<tr><th style='" + thUnpaid + numCol + "'>#</th><th style='" + thUnpaid + "'>Name</th></tr>" +
        unpaidRows +
      "</table>";
  }

  // [NEW] Expenses — listed individually (Title + Date + Amount), neutral slate
  // tint so it reads as "money out" rather than a green/red income signal.
  // Total Expenses / Net Balance sit right below this table, not in the top
  // summary line, per request — this section is fully self-contained.
  if (expenseList.length > 0) {
    const expenseRows = expenseList.map((x, i) =>
      "<tr><td style='" + tdExpense + numCol + "'>" + (i + 1) + ".</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdExpense + "'>" + esc(x.title) + "</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdExpense + "'>" + esc(x.date || "—") + "</td>" +
      "<td style='" + tdExpense + "text-align:right;'>" + CFG.currencyText + " " + x.amount + "</td></tr>"
    ).join("");
    sections += "<h3 style='color:#334155;margin-top:20px;margin-bottom:10px;'>💸 Expenses This Month</h3>" +
      "<table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:8px;'>" +
        "<tr><th style='" + thExpense + numCol + "'>#</th><th style='" + thExpense + "'>Title</th><th style='" + thExpense + "'>Date</th><th style='" + thExpense + "text-align:right;'>Amount</th></tr>" +
        expenseRows +
      "</table>" +
      "<p style='margin:0 0 4px;'><strong>Total Expenses:</strong> " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.expenseTotal||0) + "</p>" +
      "<p style='margin:0;font-size:14px;'><strong>Net Balance: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.netBalance != null ? data.netBalance : data.grandTotal) + "</strong> <span style='color:#94a3b8;font-weight:400;font-size:11.5px;'>(collected − expenses)</span></p>";
  }

  // [NEW] All-time fund summary — a SEPARATE block from the monthly figures
  // above, showing overall treasury totals since inception rather than just
  // this month. Distinct indigo tint so it doesn't blend with the monthly
  // slate-colored expense box right above it.
  const allTimeBlock =
    "<div style='margin-top:22px;padding:14px 16px;background:#eef2ff;border:1px solid #c7d2fe;border-radius:10px;'>" +
      "<h3 style='color:#3730a3;margin:0 0 10px;font-size:14px;'>🏦 Overall Fund Summary (All-Time)</h3>" +
      "<p style='margin:0 0 4px;'><strong>Total Collection (all-time):</strong> " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeCollected||0) + "</p>" +
      "<p style='margin:0 0 4px;'><strong>Total Expenses (all-time):</strong> " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeExpenses||0) + "</p>" +
      "<p style='margin:0;font-size:15px;'><strong>Current Net Balance: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeNetBalance != null ? data.allTimeNetBalance : (data.allTimeCollected||0)) + "</strong></p>" +
    "</div>";

  // [NEW] System-generated footer note — printed at the bottom of the PDF page.
  const footerNote =
    "<p style='margin-top:28px;padding-top:12px;border-top:1px solid #e2e8f0;font-size:10.5px;color:#94a3b8;text-align:center;'>" +
      "This is a system-generated document from " + esc(CFG.name) + ". No signature is required." +
    "</p>";

  return "<html><body style='font-family:Arial,sans-serif;color:#1e293b;font-size:13px;padding:18px 22px;'>" +
    "<h2 style='margin-bottom:2px;'>" + esc(CFG.name) + "</h2>" +
    "<p style='color:#64748b;margin-top:0;'>" + esc(data.month) + " " + esc(data.year) + " — Contribution Summary</p>" +
    "<p><strong>Members collected:</strong> " + CFG.currencyText + " " + data.totalCollected +
      " &nbsp;|&nbsp; <strong>Walk-in collected:</strong> " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.walkinTotal||0) + "</p>" +
    "<p style='font-size:15px;'><strong>Grand total: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.grandTotal != null ? data.grandTotal : data.totalCollected) + "</strong></p>" +
    "<p>Paid: " + data.paidList.length + " &nbsp;|&nbsp; Not yet paid: " + data.unpaidList.length +
      " &nbsp;|&nbsp; Walk-in entries: " + walkinList.length + "</p>" +
    sections +
    allTimeBlock +
    footerNote +
    "</body></html>";
}

// ── Plain-text version, ready to select-all + copy-paste into WhatsApp/group chat.
//    Email HTML can't run a working "Copy" button in most clients (Gmail strips onclick),
//    so a pre-formatted block the admin can manually select is the reliable fallback —
//    it's also shown even when the PDF attaches fine, since forwarding text is often faster.
function _buildAdminSummaryPlainText(data) {
  const walkinList  = data.walkinList || [];
  const expenseList = data.expenseList || [];
  const lines = [];
  lines.push(CFG.symbol + " " + CFG.name);
  lines.push("📍 " + CFG.location);
  lines.push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━");
  lines.push("📋 ADMIN MONTHLY SUMMARY");
  lines.push("📅 " + data.month + " " + data.year);

  if (data.paidList.length > 0) {
    lines.push("");
    lines.push("✅ PAID (" + data.paidList.length + ")");
    data.paidList.forEach((m, i) => {
      lines.push((i + 1) + ". " + m.name + " — " + CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount + (m.entries > 1 ? " (" + m.entries + " entries)" : ""));
    });
  }

  if (walkinList.length > 0) {
    lines.push("");
    lines.push("🚶 WALK-IN (" + walkinList.length + ")");
    walkinList.forEach((m, i) => {
      lines.push((i + 1) + ". " + m.name + " — " + CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount);
    });
  }

  if (data.unpaidList.length > 0) {
    lines.push("");
    lines.push("⚠️ NOT PAID (" + data.unpaidList.length + ")");
    data.unpaidList.forEach((m, i) => {
      lines.push((i + 1) + ". " + m.name);
    });
  }

  lines.push("");
  lines.push("💰 Members Collected: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + data.totalCollected);
  lines.push("💰 Walk-in Collected: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.walkinTotal||0));
  lines.push("💰 Grand Total: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.grandTotal != null ? data.grandTotal : data.totalCollected));

  // [NEW] Expenses — its own Total Expenses / Net Balance lines live here,
  // right after the expense list, rather than mixed into the income summary
  // block above (per request: only near the expense section, lower down).
  if (expenseList.length > 0) {
    lines.push("");
    lines.push("💸 EXPENSES (" + expenseList.length + ")");
    expenseList.forEach((x, i) => {
      lines.push((i + 1) + ". " + x.title + (x.date ? " (" + x.date + ")" : "") + " — " + CFG.currencyText + " " + x.amount);
    });
    lines.push("");
    lines.push("💸 Total Expenses: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.expenseTotal||0));
    lines.push("📊 Net Balance: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.netBalance != null ? data.netBalance : data.grandTotal) + " (collected − expenses)");
  }

  // [NEW] All-time fund summary — separate block, shown after the monthly
  // figures above, giving the overall treasury total rather than just this
  // month's activity.
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("🏦 OVERALL FUND SUMMARY (ALL-TIME)");
  lines.push("Total Collection (all-time): " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeCollected||0));
  lines.push("Total Expenses (all-time): " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeExpenses||0));
  lines.push("Current Net Balance: " + CFG.currencyText + " " + (data.allTimeNetBalance != null ? data.allTimeNetBalance : (data.allTimeCollected||0)));

  lines.push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━");
  lines.push(CFG.tagline);
  return lines.join("\n");
}

// Numbered row for admin summary tables — dedicated to this feature so the shared
// _emailRow() (used by receipts etc.) stays untouched. Adds a "#" column and real
// left/right padding so content never sits flush against the table edge.
function _adminSummaryRow(num, name, value, textColor) {
  const c = textColor || "#1e293b";
  const valueCell = (value !== undefined)
    ? `<td style="padding:10px 14px;color:${c};font-size:13px;font-weight:700;text-align:right;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.06);">${_htmlEscape(value)}</td>`
    : `<td style="padding:10px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.06);"></td>`;
  return `<tr>
    <td style="padding:10px 4px 10px 14px;color:${c};opacity:0.55;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;text-align:center;width:26px;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.06);">${num}.</td>
    <td style="padding:10px 8px;color:${c};font-size:13px;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.06);">${_htmlEscape(name)}</td>
    ${valueCell}
  </tr>`;
}

// ── HTML email body — Paid → Walk-in → Not-Paid, each section skipped entirely
//    (no heading, no empty table) when its list has zero entries. Every row is
//    numbered, with real horizontal padding so text never touches the card edge.
function _buildAdminSummaryEmail(data) {
  const walkinList  = data.walkinList || [];
  const expenseList = data.expenseList || [];

  let sectionsHtml = "";

  if (data.paidList.length > 0) {
    const paidRows = data.paidList.map((m, i) =>
      _adminSummaryRow(i + 1, m.name, CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount + (m.entries > 1 ? " (" + m.entries + " entries)" : ""), "#166534")
    ).join("");
    sectionsHtml += `
    <p style="color:#166534;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;margin:0 0 8px;">✅ Paid</p>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:#f0fdf4;border:1px solid #bbf7d0;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">${paidRows}</table>`;
  }

  if (walkinList.length > 0) {
    const walkinRows = walkinList.map((m, i) =>
      _adminSummaryRow(i + 1, m.name, CFG.currencyText + " " + m.amount, "#92400e")
    ).join("");
    sectionsHtml += `
    <p style="color:#92400e;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;margin:20px 0 8px;">🚶 Walk-in Contributions</p>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:#fffbeb;border:1px solid #fde68a;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">${walkinRows}</table>`;
  }

  if (data.unpaidList.length > 0) {
    const unpaidRows = data.unpaidList.map((m, i) =>
      _adminSummaryRow(i + 1, m.name, undefined, "#991b1b")
    ).join("");
    sectionsHtml += `
    <p style="color:#991b1b;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;margin:20px 0 8px;">⚠️ Not Yet Paid</p>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:#fef2f2;border:1.5px solid #fecaca;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">${unpaidRows}</table>`;
  }

  // [NEW] Expenses — neutral slate tint (money OUT, distinct from paid/walkin's
  // green/amber and unpaid's red). Total Expenses / Net Balance sit directly
  // below this table only — not mixed into the top income summary above,
  // per request.
  if (expenseList.length > 0) {
    const expenseRows = expenseList.map((x, i) =>
      _adminSummaryRow(i + 1, x.title + (x.date ? " · " + x.date : ""), CFG.currencyText + " " + x.amount, "#334155")
    ).join("");
    sectionsHtml += `
    <p style="color:#334155;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;margin:20px 0 8px;">💸 Expenses This Month</p>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:#f8fafc;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">${expenseRows}</table>
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin:10px 0 2px;">
      Total Expenses: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.expenseTotal||0}
    </p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;font-weight:600;margin:0;">
      Net Balance: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.netBalance != null ? data.netBalance : data.grandTotal}
      <span style="color:${_EM.sub};font-weight:400;font-size:11.5px;">(collected − expenses)</span>
    </p>`;
  }

  const plainText = _buildAdminSummaryPlainText(data);
  const preId = "admsum_copy_text";

  // [NEW] All-time fund summary — separate indigo-tinted block, shown after
  // all the monthly sections above, giving overall treasury totals rather
  // than just this month's activity.
  const allTimeHtml = `
    <div style="margin-top:22px;padding:14px 16px;background:#eef2ff;border:1px solid #c7d2fe;border-radius:10px;">
      <p style="color:#3730a3;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;margin:0 0 8px;">🏦 Overall Fund Summary (All-Time)</p>
      <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin:0 0 4px;">Total Collection (all-time): ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.allTimeCollected||0}</p>
      <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin:0 0 4px;">Total Expenses (all-time): ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.allTimeExpenses||0}</p>
      <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14.5px;font-weight:700;margin:0;">Current Net Balance: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.allTimeNetBalance != null ? data.allTimeNetBalance : (data.allTimeCollected||0)}</p>
    </div>`;

  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("ADMIN MONTHLY SUMMARY")}
  <tr><td style="padding:24px 28px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 12px;">
      ${data.month} ${data.year} contribution status — ${data.paidList.length} paid, ${data.unpaidList.length} pending, ${walkinList.length} walk-in.
    </p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin:0 0 4px;">
      Members: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.totalCollected} &nbsp;+&nbsp; Walk-in: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.walkinTotal||0}
    </p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:15px;font-weight:600;margin:0 0 16px;">
      Grand total: ${CFG.currencyText} ${data.grandTotal != null ? data.grandTotal : data.totalCollected}
    </p>
    ${sectionsHtml}
    ${allTimeHtml}

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin:18px 0 6px;">
      Ready-to-forward text:
      <!-- Attempts a real click-to-copy — works in mail clients that don't strip
           inline scripts. Gmail/Outlook web strip <script>/onclick, so this button
           silently does nothing there; the block below is always select-and-copy-able
           regardless, so nothing is lost if the button doesn't fire. -->
      <button type="button" onclick="try{var t=document.getElementById('${preId}').innerText;navigator.clipboard.writeText(t);this.innerText='Copied ✓';}catch(e){}" style="border:1px solid #c4b5fd;background:#f5f3ff;color:#5b21b6;font-size:11px;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:6px;cursor:pointer;margin-left:4px;">Copy</button>
    </p>
    <pre id="${preId}" style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:'Courier New',monospace;font-size:11.5px;background:#f8fafc;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;padding:12px 14px;color:#334155;margin:0;">${_htmlEscape(plainText)}</pre>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin:16px 0 0;">
      A PDF copy of this table is also attached — forward either to the group if needed.

    </p>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter()}`;
  return _emShell(560, body);
}

// ── Logo URL helper — used by ALL email types
// (auto receipt, monthly summary, monthly reminder, contribution reminder,
//  birthday email, approval/rejection emails — every _logoHtml() call)
//
// Scans CFG.folderLogo (a Drive folder) for the first image file and returns
// a public lh3 URL. Result is cached in-memory for the script execution so
// multiple emails in one batch run never hit Drive API more than once.
// Falls back to "" which triggers the 🕉️ Om symbol in _logoHtml().
//
// ⚠️  WHY NOT Image/logo.PNG?
//   That file lives inside the Apps Script web-app container — external email
//   clients (Gmail, Outlook, etc.) have zero access to it. Email <img> tags
//   need a public HTTPS URL. Drive is the only option already in this setup.

var _cachedLogoUrl = null;  // null = not yet fetched this run; "" = no image found

function _getLogoUrl() {
  if (_cachedLogoUrl !== null) return _cachedLogoUrl;   // serve from cache
  try {
    if (CFG.folderLogo) {
      const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CFG.folderLogo);
      const files  = folder.getFiles();
      while (files.hasNext()) {
        const f    = files.next();
        const mime = f.getMimeType() || "";
        if (mime.startsWith("image/")) {
          // Make publicly viewable so email clients can load it
          f.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
          _cachedLogoUrl = "https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/" + f.getId() + "=w400";
          return _cachedLogoUrl;
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {
    logAction("System", "LOGO_LOAD_ERROR", "CFG.folderLogo: " + (CFG.folderLogo||"not set"), e.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
  }
  _cachedLogoUrl = "";   // cache the "no logo" result too
  return "";
}

function _logoHtml() {
  const url = _getLogoUrl();
  if (url) {
    return `<img src="${url}" alt="${CFG.name}" width="52" height="52"
              style="width:52px;height:52px;border-radius:50%;border:2px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.85);
                     object-fit:cover;display:block;margin:0 auto 12px;">`;
  }
  return `<div style="width:52px;height:52px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.14);
              display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;margin:0 auto 12px;
              font-size:24px;line-height:52px;text-align:center;">${CFG.symbol||"🕉️"}</div>`;
}

// ── Shared design tokens for a calmer, lighter email look ──
const _EM = {
  bg:      "#eef2f1",                 // soft neutral page background (was a loud 4-stop gradient)
  brand:   "#0F766E",                 // single accent colour, used consistently
  brandDk: "#0B5B54",
  ink:     "#1e293b",
  sub:     "#64748b",
  faint:   "#94a3b8",
  line:    "#e7ebe9",
  panel:   "#f6f9f8",
  card:    "#ffffff",
  radius:  "14px"
};

// Shared header block — solid brand colour, no gradients, one badge.
function _emHeader(badgeText, badgeColor, bgColor) {
  const badge = badgeText
    ? `<span style="display:inline-block;margin-top:14px;background:${badgeColor||"rgba(255,255,255,0.16)"};
         color:#fff;padding:5px 16px;border-radius:20px;font-size:11px;font-weight:600;
         letter-spacing:0.4px;">${badgeText}</span>`
    : "";
  return `<tr><td style="background:${bgColor||_EM.brand};padding:30px 32px 26px;text-align:center;">
    ${_logoHtml()}
    <div style="color:#ffffff;font-size:18px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.3px;">${CFG.name.toUpperCase()}</div>
    <div style="color:rgba(255,255,255,0.72);font-size:12px;margin-top:3px;">${CFG.location}</div>
    ${badge}
  </td></tr>`;
}

// Shared footer block — quiet, consistent across every email.
function _emFooter(noteText) {
  return `<tr><td style="background:${_EM.panel};padding:16px 32px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid ${_EM.line};">
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:11px;font-weight:600;">${CFG.name}</div>
    <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:10.5px;margin-top:2px;">${CFG.address}</div>
    ${noteText ? `<div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:10px;margin-top:8px;">${noteText}</div>` : ""}
  </td></tr>`;
}

// Lighter-weight header/footer pair — used for reminder & birthday emails where
// a quieter, more personal tone reads better than the full branded badge header.
function _emHeadSimple(label) {
  return `<tr><td style="background:${_EM.brand};padding:26px 32px 22px;text-align:center;">
    ${_logoHtml()}
    <div style="color:#ffffff;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;">${CFG.name}</div>
    <div style="color:rgba(255,255,255,0.72);font-size:11.5px;margin-top:2px;">${CFG.location}</div>
    ${label ? `<span style="display:inline-block;margin-top:14px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.16);
         color:#fff;padding:5px 16px;border-radius:20px;font-size:11px;font-weight:600;
         letter-spacing:0.4px;">✓ ${label}</span>` : ""}
  </td></tr>`;
}
function _emFooterSimple(noteText) {
  return `<tr><td style="background:#fafafa;padding:14px 32px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #eef0ef;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:10.5px;">${CFG.name} &nbsp;|&nbsp; ${CFG.address}</div>
    ${noteText ? `<div style="color:#c1c5c3;font-size:10px;margin-top:6px;">${noteText}</div>` : ""}
  </td></tr>`;
}

// Button link — used on Approval / Admin-Added emails to open the app/website directly.
function _emButton(text, url) {
  if (!url) return "";
  return `<tr><td style="padding:4px 32px 22px;text-align:center;">
    <a href="${url}" target="_blank"
       style="display:inline-block;background:${_EM.brand};color:#ffffff;text-decoration:none;
              font-size:13px;font-weight:700;padding:11px 28px;border-radius:8px;">
      ${text} →
    </a>
  </td></tr>`;
}

// Shared outer shell — one place controls page background, card width/shadow.
function _emShell(innerWidth, bodyHtml) {
  return `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"/>
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1"/></head>
<body style="margin:0;padding:0;background:${_EM.bg};font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;">
<table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:${_EM.bg};padding:36px 0;">
<tr><td align="center">
<table width="${innerWidth}" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="max-width:${innerWidth}px;width:92%;
  background:${_EM.card};border-radius:${_EM.radius};overflow:hidden;
  box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(15,23,42,0.06),0 8px 24px rgba(15,23,42,0.06);">
  ${bodyHtml}
</table>
</td></tr></table>
</body></html>`;
}

// ── Monthly receipt summary email (member contributed)
function _buildMonthlyReceiptEmail(member, contribs, types, month, year, totalAmt) {
  const amountFmt = CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(totalAmt).toLocaleString("en-IN");
  const rowsHtml  = contribs.map(c => {
    const typeName = (types.find(t => String(t.TypeId) === String(c.TypeId)) || {}).TypeName || "Contribution";
    const displayRID = (c.ReceiptID||"—").replace(new RegExp("^" + CFG.legacyReceiptPrefix + "-"), CFG.receiptPrefix + "-");
    // FIX: Google Sheets may return PaymentDate as a Date object (not a string) when
    // a user has multiple contribution entries. Coerce to String before calling .split()
    // to prevent "split is not a function" error.
    const payDateStr = c.PaymentDate
      ? (c.PaymentDate instanceof Date
          ? Utilities.formatDate(c.PaymentDate, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy")
          : String(c.PaymentDate).split(" ")[0])
      : "";
    return _emailRow(typeName + " (" + displayRID + ")",
      CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(c.Amount||0).toLocaleString("en-IN") + " · " + (c.PaymentMode||"") + " · " + payDateStr);
  }).join("");

  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("✓ MONTHLY SUMMARY")}
  <tr><td style="padding:10px 32px 0;text-align:center;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin-top:14px;">${month} ${year} — Personal summary for
      <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${member.Name}</strong>
    </div>
  </td></tr>
  <tr><td style="padding:18px 32px 6px;text-align:center;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:11px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1.5px;margin-bottom:6px;">Total Contributed</div>
    <div style="color:#15803d;font-size:36px;font-weight:700;">${amountFmt}</div>
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin-top:2px;">in ${month} ${year}</div>
  </td></tr>
  <tr><td style="padding:20px 32px 8px;">
    <div style="font-weight:700;color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">Contribution Details</div>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">${rowsHtml}</table>
  </td></tr>
  <tr><td style="padding:8px 32px 22px;text-align:center;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">🙏 ${CFG.thankYouMsg}</div>
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:11.5px;margin-top:3px;">${CFG.tagline}</div>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter("This email was sent only to you — your data is private and not shared with others.")}`;
  return _emShell(580, body);
}

// ── Month-end reminder email (member still did NOT contribute after the mid-month nudge)
function _buildReminderEmail(member, month, year) {
  var firstName = (member.Name || "Friend").split(" ")[0];
  const body = `
  ${_emHeadSimple("Final Reminder")}

  <tr><td style="padding:26px 32px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 14px;">Dear ${firstName} जी,</p>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13.5px;line-height:1.85;margin:0 0 16px;">
      यह इस महीने का last reminder है — आपका contribution
      <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${month} ${year}</strong> के लिए अभी तक हमारे records में नहीं आया है।
    </p>

    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-left:3px solid ${_EM.brand};padding:14px 18px;margin:0 0 18px;">
      <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:4px;">
        ${month} ${year} — Still Pending
      </div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.7;">
        महीना समाप्त हो चुका है, कृपया जल्द से जल्द अपना contribution पूरा करें। अगर already pay कर दिया है,
        तो कृपया household admin से coordinate करके इसे record करवा दें।
      </div>
    </div>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0 0 18px;">
      यह contribution हमारे घर के मासिक खर्चों को manage करने के लिए है, and every family member's timely
      share helps us run things smoothly — आपकी भागीदारी हमेशा गिनी जाती है। 🌸
    </p>

    <p style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;font-style:italic;text-align:center;">
      धन्यवाद — Thank you for being part of our home. 🙏
    </p>
  </td></tr>

  ${_emFooterSimple("This is a private reminder sent only to you.")}`;
  return _emShell(520, body);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  IMPROVEMENT #1 — SEND HTML RECEIPT EMAIL
//  Called after addContribution. Uses email quota guard.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function sendReceiptEmail(toEmail, donorName, receiptId, amount, forMonth, year, typeName, occasionName, note, paymentDate, paymentMode) {
  if (!toEmail) {
    logAction("System", "RECEIPT_EMAIL_SKIPPED", "ReceiptId: " + receiptId, "No email address for donor", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"FAILURE" });
    return false;
  }
  if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
    logAction("System", "RECEIPT_EMAIL_QUOTA_FULL", "ReceiptId: " + receiptId + " | Donor: " + donorName, "Daily email quota exhausted", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
    return false;
  }

  const modeLabel = paymentMode || "—";
  const amountFmt = CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(amount || 0).toLocaleString("en-IN");

  const detailRows = `
        ${_emailRow("Donor Name", donorName || "—")}
        ${_emailRow("For Month", (forMonth || "—") + " " + (year || ""))}
        ${_emailRow("Contribution Type", typeName || "—")}
        ${occasionName && occasionName !== "—" ? _emailRow("Occasion", occasionName) : ""}
        ${note ? _emailRow("Note", note) : ""}
        ${_emailRow("Date Recorded", paymentDate || "—")}
        ${_emailRow("Receipt ID", receiptId)}`;

  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("✓ OFFICIAL RECEIPT")}

  <tr><td style="padding:16px 32px 0;text-align:center;">
