    <span style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;">Receipt No.</span>
    <span style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:14px;font-weight:700;font-family:monospace;letter-spacing:0.5px;"> ${receiptId}</span>
  </td></tr>

  <tr><td style="padding:20px 32px 8px;text-align:center;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:11px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1.5px;margin-bottom:4px;">Amount Received</div>
    <div style="color:#16a34a;font-size:34px;font-weight:700;">${amountFmt}</div>
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin-top:2px;">Payment Mode: <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${modeLabel}</strong></div>
  </td></tr>

  <tr><td style="padding:20px 32px 4px;">
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">${detailRows}</table>
  </td></tr>

  <tr><td style="padding:16px 32px 22px;">
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr>
      <td style="text-align:left;padding-top:16px;border-top:1px solid ${_EM.line};">
        <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:12px;font-weight:700;">${CFG.signatory}</div>
        <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:11px;">${CFG.designation}</div>
        <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:11px;">${CFG.name}</div>
      </td>
      <td style="text-align:right;padding-top:16px;border-top:1px solid ${_EM.line};">
        <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:11px;">System-generated receipt.</div>
        <div style="color:${_EM.faint};font-size:11px;">No signature required.</div>
      </td>
    </tr></table>
  </td></tr>

  <tr><td style="padding:0 32px 22px;text-align:center;">
    <div style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">🙏 ${CFG.thankYouMsg}</div>
    <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:11.5px;margin-top:3px;">${CFG.tagline}</div>
  </td></tr>

  ${_emFooter("System-generated receipt — sent only to you. Please do not reply to this email.")}`;

  const htmlBody = _emShell(580, body);

  try {
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to:       toEmail,
      subject:  CFG.receiptPrefix + " Receipt " + receiptId + " — " + CFG.name,
      htmlBody: htmlBody
    });
    return true; // quota already consumed atomically in tryConsumeEmailQuota()
  } catch(err) {
    logAction("System", "RECEIPT_EMAIL_SEND_ERROR", "ReceiptId: " + receiptId + " | To: " + toEmail + " | Donor: " + donorName, err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
    return false;
  }
}

// Helper: escape HTML special chars to prevent layout injection in emails
function _htmlEscape(str) {
  return String(str || "")
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
    .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
    .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
}

// Helper: one row in the receipt email table
function _emailRow(label, value) {
  return `<tr>
    <td style="padding:9px 0;color:#64748b;font-size:12px;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;width:45%;">${_htmlEscape(label)}</td>
    <td style="padding:9px 0;color:#1e293b;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;text-align:right;">${_htmlEscape(value)}</td>
  </tr>`;
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MAIN GET HANDLER
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function doGet(e) {
  const action   = sanitize(e.parameter.action, 50);
  // FIX SEC-3: Whitelist callback to alphanumeric+underscore only — prevents JSONP injection
  const _rawCb   = String(e.parameter.callback || "cb");
  const callback = /^[a-zA-Z0-9_$]{1,80}$/.test(_rawCb) ? _rawCb : "cb";
  let result = {};

  _trackRequest(action);   // ── TRAFFIC COUNTER: fires before auth, counts every hit

  // ── MUST #7: Verify session token for all write, mutating, and sensitive read actions
  // FIX SEC-1 (complete): Every action that modifies data OR exposes private data requires auth
  const _WRITE_ACTIONS = [
    // Contributions & Expenses
    "addContribution","updateContribution","deleteContribution",
    "addExpense","updateExpense","deleteExpense",
    "removeExpenseReceipt","removeOneExpenseReceipt","removeAllExpenseReceipts",
    // Users
    "addUser","deleteUser","updateUser","approveUser","rejectUser","changePassword",
    // Master data
    "addType","deleteType","updateType",
    "addOccasion","deleteOccasion","updateOccasion",
    "addExpenseType","deleteExpenseType","updateExpenseType","updateSortOrder",
    // Goals / Events / Gallery
    "addGoal","updateGoal","deleteGoal",
    "addEvent","updateEvent","deleteEvent","addEventExpense",
    "deleteGalleryPhoto",
    // Settings & comms
    "saveEmailSettings","saveAnnouncement","clearAnnouncement",
    "saveBroadcast","deleteBroadcast","saveChatbotConfig",
    // Feedback & contribution requests
    "updateFeedbackStatus","deleteFeedback",
    "submitContributionRequest","resolveContributionRequest",
    "editContributionRequest","deleteContributionRequest",
    // Email blast actions — must require auth to prevent spam abuse
    "triggerMonthlyReport","triggerMonthlyReminder","sendMonthlyReminders","sendBirthdayEmails",
    "sendContribReceiptEmail",
    "triggerAdminSummary","getAdminSummaryStatus",
    // Mobile number change — requires active session
    "sendMobileChangeOTP","verifyMobileChangeOTP",
    // Audit log write — prevent unauthenticated fake entries
    "logAudit",
    // Photo proxy — prevent unauthenticated Drive file access
    "getPhotoBase64",
    // Email logo preview — reads CFG.folderLogo, requires active admin session
    "getEmailLogoPreview",
    // Sensitive reads — private user/financial/system data
    "getAllData","getContributions","getExpenses","getEventData","getYearConfig",
    "getUsers","getUsersByStatus","getPendingUsers","getPendingCount",
    "getFeedback","getContributionRequests","getUserContributionRequests",
    "getAuditLog","getAnnouncementHistory","getHealthCheck",
    "getTrafficStats","resetTrafficStats",  // ── TRAFFIC: admin-only
    "getEmailSettings","getEmailQuota","getYearlySummary",
    "getPaymentDetails",  // SEC: bank/UPI details — never public, requires valid session
    "getMonthlyReportStatus",
    // Birthday wish bell — reads other members' names/photos, writes wish records
    "getTodayBirthdays","sendBirthdayWish","getMyBirthdayWishes",
  ];
  if (_WRITE_ACTIONS.indexOf(action) !== -1 && !_verifySession(e.parameter, action)) {
    return ContentService
      .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify({status:"error",message:"Session expired. Please login again."}) + ")")
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
  }

  // ── LOGIN
  if (action === "login") {
    let users   = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
    let mobile  = sanitize(e.parameter.mobile, 15);
    let pwdHash = sanitize(e.parameter.password, 128);
    const _rl = _checkLoginRate(mobile);
    if (_rl.blocked) {
      // Log brute-force block as CRITICAL
      logAction(mobile || "Unknown", "LOGIN_BLOCKED", "Mobile: " + mobile, "Rate limit exceeded — too many failed attempts", "", { severity: "CRITICAL", result: "BLOCKED" });
      result = { status: "error", message: _rl.message, errorCode: "rate_limited" };
    } else {
      // Step 1: check if mobile exists (regardless of password)
      let userByMobile = users.find(u => String(u.Mobile) === mobile);
      if (!userByMobile) {
        // Mobile not registered at all
        _recordLoginFail(mobile);
        logAction(mobile, "LOGIN_FAILED", "Mobile not registered: " + mobile, "mobile_not_found", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Mobile number not registered. Please check your number or register.", errorCode: "mobile_not_found" };
      } else if (String(userByMobile.Status||"").toLowerCase() === "pending") {
        logAction(mobile, "LOGIN_DENIED", "Account pending approval | Mobile: " + mobile, "account_pending", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"INFO", result:"BLOCKED" });
        result = { status: "pending", message: "Your registration is pending admin approval. You will receive an email once approved." };
      } else if (String(userByMobile.Status||"").toLowerCase() === "rejected") {
        logAction(mobile, "LOGIN_DENIED", "Account rejected | Mobile: " + mobile, "account_rejected", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Your registration was not approved. Please contact the temple admin.", errorCode: "account_rejected" };
      } else if (String(userByMobile.Status||"").toLowerCase() === "inactive") {
        logAction(mobile, "LOGIN_DENIED", "Account inactive | Mobile: " + mobile, "account_inactive", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Your account is deactivated. Please contact admin.", errorCode: "account_inactive" };
      } else if (String(userByMobile.Status||"").toLowerCase() !== "active") {
        _recordLoginFail(mobile);
        logAction(mobile, "LOGIN_FAILED", "Invalid account status: " + userByMobile.Status + " | Mobile: " + mobile, "account_invalid", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Account status invalid. Please contact admin.", errorCode: "account_invalid" };
      } else {
        // Step 2: mobile found and Active — now check password
        if (String(userByMobile.Password) !== pwdHash) {
          _recordLoginFail(mobile);
          logAction(userByMobile.Name || mobile, "LOGIN_FAILED", "Wrong password | Mobile: " + mobile + " | UserId: " + userByMobile.UserId, "wrong_password", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
          result = { status: "error", message: "Incorrect password. Please try again.", errorCode: "wrong_password" };
        } else {
          // Login success
          _clearLoginFail(mobile);
          let safeUser = Object.assign({}, userByMobile);
          delete safeUser.Password;
          const deviceInfo = sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo || "", 200);
          const loginTime  = formatDate();
          // Write LastLogin timestamp back to USERS sheet
          try {
            const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
            const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
            const headers = data[0];
            let llCol = headers.indexOf("LastLogin");
            if (llCol === -1) {
              // Column doesn't exist yet — create it
              llCol = headers.length;
              sheet.getRange(1, llCol + 1).setValue("LastLogin");
            }
            // [FIX-8] Use header-based UserId column lookup — not hardcoded col 0.
            // If sheet columns are ever reordered, col 0 may not be UserId.
            const _uidCol = headers.indexOf("UserId");
            for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
              const _rowId = _uidCol !== -1 ? String(data[i][_uidCol] || "") : String(data[i][0] || "");
              if (_rowId === String(safeUser.UserId)) {
                sheet.getRange(i + 1, llCol + 1).setValue(loginTime);
                SpreadsheetApp.flush();
                break;
              }
            }
          } catch(llErr) { /* non-fatal — never block login on this */ }
          logAction(
            safeUser.Name || "User",
            "Login",
            "Mobile: " + mobile + " | Role: " + (safeUser.Role || "User") + " | UserId: " + (safeUser.UserId || ""),
            "User initiated login",
            deviceInfo
          );
          result = { status: "success", user: safeUser, lastLogin: safeUser.LastLogin || "" };
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // ── SET SESSION TOKEN — writes token + TokenExpiry to USERS sheet
  // [SEC] TokenExpiry is server-enforced. Every subsequent write action checks
  // this column and slides it forward (see _verifySession) by whatever window
  // was granted here — 30 min normally, or 24h if rememberMe was checked at
  // login. The granted window itself is stored in the SessionTTL column so
  // _verifySession's sliding renewal uses the SAME duration every time, rather
  // than silently capping a "remember me" session back down to 30 min.
  else if (action === "setSessionToken") {
    const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    const token  = sanitize(e.parameter.token,  64);
    // [FIX-24H] rememberMe wasn't previously read at all — every login got a
    // 30-min server session regardless of the "Remember me for 24 hours"
    // checkbox, so audit logs showed SESSION_EXPIRED at 30 min even when the
    // box was checked.
    const rememberMe = sanitize(e.parameter.rememberMe, 5) === "1";
    if (!userId || !token) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Missing userId or token" };
    } else {
      const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
      const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const headers = data[0];
      // Ensure SessionToken column exists
      let tokenCol = headers.indexOf("SessionToken");
      if (tokenCol === -1) { tokenCol = headers.length; sheet.getRange(1, tokenCol + 1).setValue("SessionToken"); }
      // Ensure TokenExpiry column exists
      let expiryCol = headers.indexOf("TokenExpiry");
      if (expiryCol === -1) { expiryCol = headers.length + (tokenCol === headers.length ? 1 : 0); sheet.getRange(1, expiryCol + 1).setValue("TokenExpiry"); }
      // Ensure SessionTTL column exists — stores the granted sliding-window
      // length (ms) so _verifySession renews by the same amount each time.
      let ttlCol = headers.indexOf("SessionTTL");
      if (ttlCol === -1) {
        ttlCol = Math.max(tokenCol, expiryCol) + 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, ttlCol + 1).setValue("SessionTTL");
      }
      let found = false;
      // [FIX] Store TokenExpiry as Unix ms number — NOT a formatted date string.
      // Sheets auto-converts date strings to UTC Date objects on read-back,
      // making IST tokens appear 5.5h expired instantly.
      const sessionTtlMs  = rememberMe ? 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 : 30 * 60 * 1000;
      const expiryTime    = Date.now() + sessionTtlMs;
      const expiryDisplay = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(expiryTime), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss"); // audit log only
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]) === userId) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, tokenCol + 1).setValue(token);
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, expiryCol + 1).setValue(expiryTime); // plain number
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, ttlCol + 1).setValue(sessionTtlMs);  // plain number, ms
          SpreadsheetApp.flush();
          found = true; break;
        }
      }
      if (found) {
        logAction(userId, "SESSION_TOKEN_SET", "UserId: " + userId + " | Expiry: " + expiryDisplay + " | RememberMe: " + (rememberMe ? "24h" : "30min"), "Session token + expiry stored after login", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
      } else {
        logAction(userId, "SESSION_TOKEN_SET_FAILED", "UserId: " + userId + " — user not found", "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
      }
      // Bust verify cache so the new token is visible to _verifySession immediately
      if (found) _bustSheetCache("c_users_verify");
      result = found ? { status: "ok" } : { status: "error", message: "User not found" };
    }
  }


  // ── CHECK SESSION TOKEN + EXPIRY
  else if (action === "checkSession") {
    const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    const token  = sanitize(e.parameter.token,  64);
    if (!userId || !token) { result = { valid: true }; }
    else {
      try {
        const sheet    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
        const allData  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers  = allData[0];
        const tokenCol  = headers.indexOf("SessionToken");
        const expiryCol = headers.indexOf("TokenExpiry");
        const nameCol   = headers.indexOf("Name");  // [FIX-C] match by Name too
        if (tokenCol === -1) { result = { valid: true }; }
        else {
          let isValid = true;
          let expiredReason = "";
          let foundRow = -1;
          for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
            // [FIX-C] Match by UserId (col 0) OR Name — same as _verifySession
            const rowUserId = String(allData[i][0] || "").trim();
            const rowName   = nameCol !== -1 ? String(allData[i][nameCol] || "").trim() : "";
            if (!((rowUserId && rowUserId === userId) || (rowName && rowName === userId))) continue;
            foundRow = i;
            const stored = String(allData[i][tokenCol] || "").trim();
            if (stored === "") { isValid = true; break; }           // legacy session, allow
            if (stored !== token) { isValid = false; expiredReason = "token_mismatch"; break; }
            // Check TokenExpiry
            if (expiryCol !== -1) {
              const expiryVal = allData[i][expiryCol];
              if (expiryVal) {
                // [FIX] Unix ms number — use Number(), not new Date()
                const expiryTime = expiryVal instanceof Date ? expiryVal.getTime() : Number(expiryVal);
                if (!isNaN(expiryTime) && expiryTime > 0 && Date.now() > expiryTime) {
                  isValid = false; expiredReason = "expired";
                  // [FIX-C] Auto-clear stale token + expiry so sheet stays clean
                  // Previously checkSession only returned { valid:false } but never
                  // cleaned up — expired token sat in sheet until next manual logout.
                  try {
                    sheet.getRange(i + 1, tokenCol  + 1).setValue("");
                    sheet.getRange(i + 1, expiryCol + 1).setValue("");
                    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
                    logAction(userId, "SESSION_EXPIRED_AUTO_CLEARED",
                      "checkSession detected expiry — token auto-cleared from sheet", "", "",
                      { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
                  } catch(clrErr) { /* non-fatal */ }
                  break;
                }
              }
            }
            isValid = true; break;
          }
          result = { valid: isValid, reason: expiredReason || undefined };
        }
      } catch(err) { result = { valid: true }; }
    }
  }

  // ── CLEAR SESSION TOKEN + EXPIRY (called on logout, tab close via sendBeacon)
  else if (action === "clearSessionToken") {
    const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    if (userId) {
      try {
        const sheet    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
        const allData  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers  = allData[0];
        const tokenCol  = headers.indexOf("SessionToken");
        const expiryCol = headers.indexOf("TokenExpiry");
        const nameCol   = headers.indexOf("Name");
        // FIX: Clear each column independently — do NOT nest expiryCol inside tokenCol check.
        // If TokenExpiry column exists but SessionToken does not (edge case), expiry must still clear.
        // [FIX-2] Match by UserId (col 0) OR Name — mirrors _verifySession so logout always finds the row
        // even when localStorage stores the user's display name instead of UserId.
        for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
          const rowUserId = String(allData[i][0] || "").trim();
          const rowName   = nameCol !== -1 ? String(allData[i][nameCol] || "").trim() : "";
          if ((rowUserId && rowUserId === userId) || (rowName && rowName === userId)) {
            if (tokenCol  !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, tokenCol  + 1).setValue("");
            if (expiryCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, expiryCol + 1).setValue("");
            _bustSheetCache("c_users_verify"); // token cleared — invalidate verify cache
            SpreadsheetApp.flush(); break;
          }
        }
      } catch(e) { /* silent */ }
      logAction(userId, "SESSION_TOKEN_CLEARED", "UserId: " + userId, sanitize(e.parameter.reason||"Session cleared",200), sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
    }
    result = { status: "ok" };
  }

  // ── READ DATA
  // FIX SEC-6: Strip password hashes before returning — getAllData already does this, now getUsers does too
  else if (action === "getUsers")         result = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS).map(u => { const s = Object.assign({}, u); delete s.Password; return s; });
  else if (action === "getTypes")         result = _cachedSheet(SHEETS.TYPES,         "c_types",    600).slice().sort(function(a,b){return(Number(a.SortOrder)||0)-(Number(b.SortOrder)||0);});
  else if (action === "getExpenseTypes")  result = _cachedSheet(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES, "c_exptypes", 600).slice().sort(function(a,b){return(Number(a.SortOrder)||0)-(Number(b.SortOrder)||0);});
  else if (action === "getOccasions")     result = _cachedSheet(SHEETS.OCCASIONS,     "c_occasions",600).slice().sort(function(a,b){return(Number(a.SortOrder)||0)-(Number(b.SortOrder)||0);});
  else if (action === "getContributions") result = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);
  else if (action === "getExpenses")      result = getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
  else if (action === "getEventData")     { result = { events: getSheetData(SHEETS.EVENTS), eventExpenses: getSheetData(SHEETS.EVENT_EXPENSES) }; }
  else if (action === "addEvent")         { result = _addEvent(e.parameter); }
  else if (action === "updateEvent")      { result = _updateEvent(e.parameter); }
  else if (action === "deleteEvent")      { result = _deleteEvent(e.parameter); }
  else if (action === "addEventExpense")  { result = _addEventExpense(e.parameter); }
  else if (action === "getYearConfig")    result = getSheetData("YEAR_CONFIG");

  // ── IMPROVEMENT #1: SEND RECEIPT EMAIL ON DEMAND (from admin Email button)
  else if (action === "sendContribReceiptEmail") {
    // donorUserId — identifies the DONOR for email lookup (may differ from logged-in admin)
    // userId      — identifies the logged-in ADMIN, used by _verifySession above for auth
    const donorUserId  = sanitize(e.parameter.donorUserId || e.parameter.userId, 30);
    const receiptId   = sanitize(e.parameter.receiptId,    30);
    const userName    = sanitize(e.parameter.userName,    100);
    const amount      = sanitize(e.parameter.amount,       20);
    const forMonth    = sanitize(e.parameter.forMonth,     20);
    const year        = sanitize(e.parameter.year,         10);
    const typeName    = sanitize(e.parameter.typeName,    100);
    const occasionName= sanitize(e.parameter.occasionName,100);
    const note        = sanitize(e.parameter.note,        500);
    const paymentDate = sanitize(e.parameter.paymentDate,  50);
    const paymentMode = sanitize(e.parameter.paymentMode,  30);

    // Look up email from USERS sheet using DONOR's id, not admin's
    const users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
    const donor = users.find(u => String(u.UserId) === donorUserId);
    const toEmail = donor ? String(donor.Email||"").trim() : "";

    if (!toEmail) {
      result = { status: "no_email" };
    } else {
      // FIX SEC-A: Do NOT call tryConsumeEmailQuota() here — sendReceiptEmail() already
      // calls it atomically at its top. Calling it here too caused double-consumption
      // (2 quota slots burned per on-demand email instead of 1).
      const sent = sendReceiptEmail(toEmail, userName, receiptId, amount, forMonth, year, typeName, occasionName, note, paymentDate, paymentMode);
      if (sent === false && !canSendEmail()) {
        result = { status: "quota" };
      } else {
        result = { status: sent ? "sent" : "error" };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── IMPROVEMENT #4: GET EMAIL QUOTA STATUS (for admin sidebar badge)
  else if (action === "getEmailQuota") {
    result = getEmailQuotaStatus();
  }

  // ── PUBLIC PAYMENT DETAILS — no session required, open to all visitors
  // Bank receive-details are intentionally public — a donor needs them to pay.
  // Knowing an account number for *receiving* donations is not a security risk.
  // NOT in _WRITE_ACTIONS — open so the donate modal works for every visitor.
  else if (action === "getPublicPaymentDetails") {
    result = {
      status:      "ok",
      upiId:       CFG.upiId       || "",
      accountName: CFG.accountName || "",
      accountNo:   CFG.accountNo   || "",
      ifscCode:    CFG.ifscCode    || "",
      bankName:    CFG.bankName    || "",
      bankBranch:  CFG.bankBranch  || "",
      accountType: CFG.accountType || "",
    };
  }

  // ── PRIVATE PAYMENT DETAILS — session-gated (kept for future use)
  // Same data as above, but only returns to authenticated sessions.
  // Use if you ever add extra sensitive fields only logged-in users should see.
  else if (action === "getPaymentDetails") {
    result = {
      status:      "ok",
      upiId:       CFG.upiId       || "",
      accountName: CFG.accountName || "",
      accountNo:   CFG.accountNo   || "",
      ifscCode:    CFG.ifscCode    || "",
      bankName:    CFG.bankName    || "",
      bankBranch:  CFG.bankBranch  || "",
      accountType: CFG.accountType || "",
    };
  }

  // ── #8: EMAIL AUTOMATION SETTINGS
  else if (action === "getEmailSettings") {
    result = getEmailSettings();
  }
  else if (action === "saveEmailSettings") {
    // Admin passes: action=saveEmailSettings&key=auto_receipt&value=1
    const key      = sanitize(e.parameter.key || "", 30);
    const value    = sanitize(e.parameter.value || "0", 2);   // toggles only: "0" or "1"
    const allowed  = ["auto_receipt", "monthly_report", "birthday_email", "admin_monthly_summary"];
    // logo_email_url removed — logo is now auto-loaded from CFG.folderLogo (Drive folder)
    if (allowed.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
      result = saveEmailSettings(key, value, sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100));
    } else {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Unknown setting key: " + key };
    }
  }

  // ── #9: MANUAL TRIGGER — Monthly Report (fire-and-store pattern)
  // WHY: Google's CDN cuts JSONP responses after ~30s for long-running doGet calls.
  // FIX: Store result in PropertiesService keyed by jobKey, return immediately.
  //      Client polls getMonthlyReportStatus every 5s to read the result.
  else if (action === "triggerMonthlyReport") {
    const month  = sanitize(e.parameter.month,  20);
    const year   = sanitize(e.parameter.year,   10);
    const jobKey = sanitize(e.parameter.jobKey, 50) || ("job_" + Date.now());
    // Cooldown: prevent re-sending the same month+year report within 1 hour
    const throttleKey = "MREPORT_SENT_" + (month || "") + "_" + (year || "");
    let _throttled = false;
    try {
      const lastSent = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(throttleKey);
      if (lastSent && (Date.now() - Number(lastSent)) < 3600000) { _throttled = true; }
      else { PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(throttleKey, String(Date.now())); }
    } catch(e) {}
    if (_throttled) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Monthly report for this period was already sent recently. Please wait 1 hour before re-sending." };
    } else {
    // Mark job as pending immediately so client knows it started
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "MREPORT_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify({ status: "pending" })
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    // Run the report synchronously (GAS executes doGet fully before returning)
    // The JSONP response may be cut off by CDN, but the job WILL complete.
    // Result is also stored so the poll endpoint can return it.
    let jobResult;
    try {
      jobResult = _doSendMonthlyReports(month || null, year || null);
    } catch(err) {
      logAction("System", "MONTHLY_REPORT_ERROR", "Month: " + (month||"auto") + " | Year: " + (year||"auto"), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      jobResult = { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
    // Store final result for polling
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "MREPORT_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify(jobResult)
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    result = jobResult;
    } // end cooldown else
  }

  // ── #9b: POLL for monthly report result
  else if (action === "getMonthlyReportStatus") {
    const jobKey = sanitize(e.parameter.jobKey, 50);
    if (!jobKey) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Missing jobKey" };
    } else {
      try {
        const raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("MREPORT_" + jobKey);
        if (!raw) {
          result = { status: "pending" }; // job not started yet or key expired
        } else {
          result = JSON.parse(raw);
          // Clean up once read successfully (only if done)
          if (result.status !== "pending") {
            try { PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty("MREPORT_" + jobKey); } catch(e) {}
          }
        }
      } catch(e) {
        result = { status: "pending" };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── #10: MANUAL TRIGGER — Admin Monthly Summary (fire-and-store pattern, same as #9)
  else if (action === "triggerAdminSummary") {
    const month  = sanitize(e.parameter.month,  20);
    const year   = sanitize(e.parameter.year,   10);
    const jobKey = sanitize(e.parameter.jobKey, 50) || ("job_" + Date.now());
    // [FIX] No 1-hour cooldown here — this action is the manual/admin "Send Now" test
    // button, gated by _verifySession already (a real admin must be logged in to fire
    // it). A 1-hour lockout on a test tool caused it to silently reject re-clicks, and
    // the old code never wrote a "pending" record for the throttled case — so the
    // frontend poll loop waited forever for a jobKey that was never stored. If you want
    // this un-throttled from anywhere, keep it this way; the automatic month-end trigger
    // (sendAdminMonthlySummary) is separate and unaffected.
    const withPdf = sanitize(e.parameter.withPdf, 2) !== "0"; // default true — pass withPdf=0 to skip PDF generation
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "ADMSUM_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify({ status: "pending" })
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    let jobResult;
    try {
      jobResult = _doSendAdminSummary(month || null, year || null, withPdf);
    } catch(err) {
      logAction("System", "ADMIN_SUMMARY_ERROR", "Month: " + (month||"auto") + " | Year: " + (year||"auto"), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      jobResult = { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "ADMSUM_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify(jobResult)
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    result = jobResult;
  }

  // ── #10b: POLL for admin summary result
  else if (action === "getAdminSummaryStatus") {
    const jobKey = sanitize(e.parameter.jobKey, 50);
    if (!jobKey) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Missing jobKey" };
    } else {
      try {
        const raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("ADMSUM_" + jobKey);
        if (!raw) {
          result = { status: "pending" };
        } else {
          result = JSON.parse(raw);
          if (result.status !== "pending") {
            try { PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty("ADMSUM_" + jobKey); } catch(e) {}
          }
        }
      } catch(e) {
        result = { status: "pending" };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── GOAL MANAGEMENT
  else if (action === "addGoal") {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GOALS);
    if (!sheet) { result = { status: "error", message: "GOALS sheet not found" }; }
    else {
      const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      const row = headers.map(h => {
        if (h === "GoalId")       return sanitize(e.parameter.GoalId, 50) || generateSheetId("GOAL");
        if (h === "GoalName")     return sanitize(e.parameter.GoalName, 200);
        if (h === "TargetAmount") return Number(e.parameter.TargetAmount||0);
        if (h === "CurrentAmount")return Number(e.parameter.CurrentAmount||0);
        if (h === "Status")       return sanitize(e.parameter.Status, 20) || "Disabled";
        if (h === "CreatedAt")    return formatDate();
        return "";
      });
      sheet.appendRow(row);
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Goal", sanitize(e.parameter.GoalName, 100) + " | Target: ₹" + (e.parameter.TargetAmount||""));
      result = { status: "success" };
    }
  }
  else if (action === "updateGoal") {
    const rows    = getSheetData(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const rid     = sanitize(e.parameter.GoalId, 50);
    const idx     = rows.findIndex(r => String(r.GoalId) === rid);
    if (idx === -1) { result = { status: "error", message: "Goal not found" }; }
    else {
      const sheetRow = idx + 2;
      headers.forEach((h,i) => {
        if (h === "GoalName")      sheet.getRange(sheetRow,i+1).setValue(sanitize(e.parameter.GoalName,200));
        if (h === "TargetAmount")  sheet.getRange(sheetRow,i+1).setValue(Number(e.parameter.TargetAmount||0));
        if (h === "CurrentAmount") sheet.getRange(sheetRow,i+1).setValue(Number(e.parameter.CurrentAmount||0));
        if (h === "Status")        sheet.getRange(sheetRow,i+1).setValue(sanitize(e.parameter.Status,20));
      });
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Goal", "GoalId: " + rid + " | Name: " + sanitize(e.parameter.GoalName||"",100));
      // M7 — check if goal just completed
      _checkGoalCompletion(rid);
      result = { status: "updated" };
    }
  }
  else if (action === "deleteGoal") {
    const rows  = getSheetData(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const rid   = sanitize(e.parameter.GoalId, 50);
    const idx   = rows.findIndex(r => String(r.GoalId) === rid);
    if (idx === -1) { result = { status: "error", message: "Goal not found" }; }
    else { sheet.deleteRow(idx + 2); logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete Goal", "GoalId: " + rid); result = { status: "deleted" }; }
  }

  // ── GALLERY
  else if (action === "getGallery") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GALLERY);
      if (!sheet) { result = []; }
      else {
        const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        if (data.length < 2) { result = []; }
        else {
          const headers = data[0];
          result = data.slice(1)
            .filter(r => String(r[headers.indexOf("Status")] || "Active") !== "Deleted")
            .map(r => ({
              // [FIX] Wrap every field in String() — Sheets auto-types cells, so a
              // caption/tag that looks numeric (e.g. "2024") or a date comes back
              // as a Number/Date object instead of text. Client code calls string
              // methods (toLowerCase, split, etc.) on these, which throws if they
              // aren't real strings — that was the "Error loading gallery" cause.
              PhotoId:  String(r[headers.indexOf("ImageId")]  || ""),
              Caption:  String(r[headers.indexOf("Title")]    || ""),
              PhotoURL: String(r[headers.indexOf("PhotoURL")] || ""),
              Priority: r[headers.indexOf("Priority")] || "",
              Status:   String(r[headers.indexOf("Status")]   || ""),
              AddedAt:  String(r[headers.indexOf("CreatedAt")]|| ""),
              Tags:     String(r[headers.indexOf("Tags")]     || "")
            }))
            .sort((a, b) => (Number(a.Priority)||999) - (Number(b.Priority)||999));
        }
      }
    } catch(err) { result = []; }
  }

  else if (action === "deleteGalleryPhoto") {
    const photoId = sanitize(e.parameter.PhotoId, 50);
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GALLERY);
      if (!sheet) { result = { status: "error", message: "GALLERY sheet not found" }; }
      else {
        const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers = data[0];
        const idCol   = headers.indexOf("ImageId");
        const urlCol  = headers.indexOf("PhotoURL");
        let found = false;
        for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
          if (String(data[i][idCol]) === photoId) {
            try {
              const url = String(data[i][urlCol] || "");
              // [FIX] Gallery photos are uploaded via _uploadToFolder(), which returns
              // "https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=...&sz=w400" — NOT the lh3.
              // googleusercontent.com/d/... format. Only the lh3 format was handled
              // here before, so fileId was never extracted and the Drive file was
              // never trashed, even though the sheet row was deleted. Added the
              // thumbnail?id= branch (same pattern already used in deleteUser).
              let fileId = "";
              if (url.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/")) {
                fileId = url.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
              } else if (url.includes("drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=")) {
                fileId = url.split("id=")[1].split("&")[0].trim();
              }
              if (fileId && fileId.length > 10) DriveApp.getFileById(fileId).setTrashed(true);
            } catch(driveErr) { /* non-fatal */ }
            sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
            logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName, 100) || "Admin", "deleteGalleryPhoto", "PhotoId: " + photoId);
            found = true; result = { status: "deleted" }; break;
          }
        }
        if (!found) result = { status: "error", message: "Photo not found" };
      }
    } catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  // ── GET ALL DATA
  else if (action === "getAllData") {
    var _sortBySortOrder = function(arr) {
      return arr.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
        return (Number(a.SortOrder) || 0) - (Number(b.SortOrder) || 0);
      });
    };
    result = {
      users:         getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS),
      types:         _sortBySortOrder(getSheetData(SHEETS.TYPES)),
      expenseTypes:  _sortBySortOrder(getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES)),
      occasions:     _sortBySortOrder(getSheetData(SHEETS.OCCASIONS)),
      contributions: getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS),
      expenses:      getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES),
      yearConfig:    getSheetData("YEAR_CONFIG"),
      goals:         getSheetData(SHEETS.GOALS)
    };
    // [DEFAULT-PWD] Strip password hashes for security, but flag whether the
    // requesting user still has the default "JaiShreeRam" password — the client
    // uses this flag to force a password change on first login without exposing hashes.
    const _defaultHash = hashPassword("JaiShreeRam");
    const _requesterIdStr = sanitize(e.parameter.userId || "", 30);
    result.users = result.users.map(u => {
      let s = Object.assign({}, u);
      if (String(u.UserId) === _requesterIdStr) {
        s.IsDefaultPwd = (String(u.Password || "").toLowerCase().trim() === _defaultHash);
      } else {
        s.IsDefaultPwd = false;
      }
      delete s.Password;
      return s;
    });
  }

  // ── AUDIT LOG — returns latest 1000 rows, newest first, with Reason column
  // Auth: covered by _WRITE_ACTIONS above
  else if (action === "getAuditLog") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.AUDIT);
      if (!sheet) { result = []; }
      else {
        const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        if (data.length < 2) { result = []; }
        else {
          // Use header-based column lookup — handles both old 6-col and new 9-col sheet layouts
          const hdr = data[0];
          const _ac = (n) => hdr.indexOf(n);
          result = data.slice(1).slice(-1000).reverse().map(r => {
            const rawTs = r[0];
            // Sheets can auto-convert a date-like string into a real Date cell,
            // which then comes back as a JS Date object here (and would
            // otherwise serialize as a raw ISO string to the client).
            const ts = (rawTs instanceof Date)
              ? Utilities.formatDate(rawTs, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MMM-yyyy HH:mm:ss")
              : (rawTs || "");
            return {
              Timestamp:  ts,
              UserAdmin:  r[1]                               || "",
              Action:     r[2]                               || "",
              Result:     _ac("Result")    !== -1 ? (r[_ac("Result")]    || "") : "",
              Details:    _ac("Details")   !== -1 ? (r[_ac("Details")]   || "") : (r[3] || ""),
              Reason:     _ac("Reason")    !== -1 ? (r[_ac("Reason")]    || "") : (r[4] || ""),
              Error:      _ac("Error")     !== -1 ? (r[_ac("Error")]     || "") : "",
              DeviceInfo: _ac("DeviceInfo")!== -1 ? (r[_ac("DeviceInfo")]|| "") : (r[5] || ""),
              Severity:   _ac("Severity")  !== -1 ? (r[_ac("Severity")]  || "") : ""
            };
          });
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { result = []; }
  }

  // ── FEEDBACK
  else if (action === "getFeedback") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("FEEDBACK");
      if (!sheet) { result = []; }
      else {
        const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        if (data.length < 2) { result = []; }
        else {
          // Return rows with RowIndex (1-based, header=row1 so data starts row2)
          // Columns: Timestamp(0), Name(1), Mobile(2), Address(3), Message(4), Status(5)
          result = data.slice(1).map((r, i) => ({
            RowIndex: i + 2,
            Timestamp: r[0] || "", Name: r[1] || "", Mobile: r[2] || "",
            Address: r[3] || "", Message: r[4] || "", Status: r[5] || "Pending"
          })).filter(r => r.Status !== "Deleted").reverse();
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { result = []; }
  }

  else if (action === "updateFeedbackStatus") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("FEEDBACK");
      if (!sheet) { result = { status: "error", message: "Sheet not found" }; }
      else {
        const rowIndex = parseInt(e.parameter.RowIndex);
        // FIX: validate RowIndex — must be an integer > 1 (row 1 is the header)
        if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > sheet.getLastRow()) {
          result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid row index." };
        } else {
          const newStatus = sanitize(e.parameter.Status, 20);
          // Ensure Status column (col 6) exists — extend header if needed
          const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
          if (headers.length < 6) sheet.getRange(1, 6).setValue("Status");
          sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 6).setValue(newStatus);
          logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Feedback Status", "RowIndex: " + rowIndex + " | NewStatus: " + newStatus, "", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
          result = { status: "updated" };
        }
      }
    } catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else if (action === "deleteFeedback") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("FEEDBACK");
      if (!sheet) { result = { status: "error", message: "Sheet not found" }; }
      else {
        const rowIndex = parseInt(e.parameter.RowIndex);
        // FIX: validate RowIndex — must be an integer > 1 (row 1 is the header)
        if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > sheet.getLastRow()) {
          result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid row index." };
        } else {
          // Mark as Deleted (soft delete) so row numbers stay stable
          const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
          if (headers.length < 6) sheet.getRange(1, 6).setValue("Status");
          sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 6).setValue("Deleted");
          logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete Feedback", "RowIndex: " + rowIndex, "Soft-deleted by admin", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SUCCESS" });
          result = { status: "deleted" };
        }
      }
    } catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else if (action === "submitFeedback") {
    try {
      let sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("FEEDBACK");
      if (!sheet) {
        sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().insertSheet("FEEDBACK");
        sheet.appendRow(["Timestamp","Name","Mobile","Address","Message","Status"]);
      }
      // Add Status header if missing
      const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
      if (lastCol < 6) sheet.getRange(1, 6).setValue("Status");
      sheet.appendRow([
        formatDate(),
        sanitize(e.parameter.Name, 100),
        sanitize(e.parameter.Mobile, 15),
        sanitize(e.parameter.Address, 200),
        sanitize(e.parameter.Message, 1000),
        "Pending"
      ]);
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.Name||"Guest",100), "Submit Feedback", "Mobile: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Mobile||"",15), "Public feedback submitted", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
      result = { status: "success" };
    } catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else if (action === "logAudit") {
    logAction(
      sanitize(e.parameter.adminName, 100),
      sanitize(e.parameter.action2,   100),
      sanitize(e.parameter.details,   500),
      sanitize(e.parameter.reason,    300)   // reason from client
    );
    result = { status: "ok" };
  }

  else if (action === "logout") {
    // logoutReason tells us exactly WHY session ended:
    //   "User clicked logout"              → manual by user
    //   "Admin clicked logout button"      → manual by admin
    //   "Session expired - 30 min inactivity" → auto timeout
    //   "Kicked - login from another device"  → new device login
    //   "Kicked - another tab opened"         → same browser, new tab
    //   "Session expired - missing or corrupted" → corrupt session
    logAction(
      sanitize(e.parameter.userName, 100) || "User",
      "Logout",
      "UserId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30),
      sanitize(e.parameter.logoutReason || "Session ended", 200),
      sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo   || "", 200)
    );
    result = { status: "ok" };
  }

    else if (action === "getChatbotConfig")  result = getChatbotConfig();
 
  else if (action === "saveChatbotConfig") result = saveChatbotConfig(e.parameter);

  // ── M1: MANUAL TRIGGER for monthly reminder (also runs via time-based trigger)
  else if (action === "triggerMonthlyReminder") {
    const month  = sanitize(e.parameter.month  || "", 20);
    const year   = sanitize(e.parameter.year   || "", 10);
    const jobKey = sanitize(e.parameter.jobKey || "", 50) || ("job_" + Date.now());
    // Mark as pending immediately so first poll knows job started
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "MREPORT_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify({ status: "pending" })
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    // Run the reminders job
    let jobResult;
    try {
      jobResult = sendMonthlyReminders(month || null, year || null, true);
    } catch(err) {
      logAction("System", "MONTHLY_REMINDER_TRIGGER_ERROR", "Month: " + month + " Year: " + year, err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      jobResult = { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
    // Store final result so poll endpoint can return it
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(
        "MREPORT_" + jobKey, JSON.stringify(jobResult)
      );
    } catch(e) {}
    result = jobResult;
  }
 
  else if (action === "sendBirthdayEmails") {
    const isTest    = (e.parameter.isTest === "1");
    const testUserId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId || "", 30) || null;
    try {
      result = sendBirthdayEmails(isTest, testUserId);
    } catch(err) {
      logAction("System", "BIRTHDAY_EMAIL_ERROR", "isTest: " + isTest, err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      result = { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
  }

  else if (action === "registerUser")      result = registerUser(e.parameter);
 
  else if (action === "approveUser")       result = approveUser(e.parameter);
 
  else if (action === "rejectUser")        result = rejectUser(e.parameter);
 
  else if (action === "getPendingUsers") {
    try {
      const all = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      result = all
        .filter(u => String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() === "pending")
        .map(u => { const s = Object.assign({}, u); delete s.Password; return s; });
    } catch(err) { result = []; }
  }
 
  else if (action === "getPendingCount") {
    try {
      const all = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      result = { count: all.filter(u => String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() === "pending").length };
    } catch(err) { result = { count: 0 }; }
  }

  else if (action === "getYearlySummary") { result = getYearlySummary(); }

  // ── H14: SYSTEM HEALTH CHECK

  else if (action === "getPublicStats") {
      result = getPublicStats();
  }
 
  else if (action === "getUsersByStatus") {
    const filterStatus = sanitize(e.parameter.status || "all", 20);
    try {
      let all = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS).map(u => { const s = Object.assign({}, u); delete s.Password; return s; });
      if (filterStatus !== "all") all = all.filter(u => String(u.Status || "Active").toLowerCase() === filterStatus.toLowerCase());
      result = all;
    } catch(err) { result = []; }
  }

  // ── ADD USER
  else if (action === "addUser") {
    let existingUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
    let mobile = sanitize(e.parameter.Mobile, 15);
    let email  = sanitize(e.parameter.Email || "", 200).toLowerCase();
    const role = sanitize(e.parameter.Role || "User", 20);

    // [VAL] Server-side mobile and email validation
    const mobileErr = _validateMobile(mobile);
    if (mobileErr) {
      result = { status: "error", message: mobileErr };
    }
    // Check duplicate mobile
    else if (existingUsers.some(u => String(u.Mobile) === mobile)) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Mobile number already registered." };
    }
    // Check duplicate email (only against non-rejected accounts)
    else if (email && existingUsers.some(u =>
      String(u.Email || "").toLowerCase() === email &&
      String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "rejected"
    )) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Email address already registered." };
    } else {
      const emailErr = _validateEmail(email);
      if (emailErr) {
        result = { status: "error", message: emailErr };
      } else {
        // [DEFAULT-PWD] Admin-added users always get the default password "JaiShreeRam".
        // The password is set server-side only — the frontend never sends a password for addUser.
        // The user is forced to change it on first login (detected client-side by hash comparison).
        const DEFAULT_PASSWORD = "JaiShreeRam";
        let hashedPwd = hashPassword(DEFAULT_PASSWORD);
        // [ID] Generate role-aware sequential UserId — never trust frontend-supplied ID
        const newUserId = _genUserId(role);
        // [FIX] Write ALL 18 columns in exact sheet order to prevent field misalignment.
        // Previously only 9 values were written, causing DOB to land in the Village column.
        // Column order: UserId,Name,Mobile,Role,Password,Email,Status,SessionToken,
        //               Village,Address,RegisteredAt,PhotoURL,MonthlyTarget,LastLogin,DOB,TokenExpiry,
        //               ContribStartDate,InactiveSince
        // NOTE: ContribStartDate + InactiveSince must exist as headers (columns 17 & 18)
        // in the USERS sheet — add them once manually if they aren't there yet.
        const _addDob = sanitize(e.parameter.DOB || "", 12);
        const _addContribStart = sanitize(e.parameter.ContribStartDate || "", 12);
        addRow(SHEETS.USERS, [
          newUserId,                                          // UserId
          sanitize(e.parameter.Name,   100),                 // Name
          mobile,                                            // Mobile
          role,                                              // Role
          hashedPwd,                                         // Password
          email,                                             // Email
          "Active",                                          // Status — admin adds directly as Active
          "",                                                // SessionToken
          "",                                                // Village
          "",                                                // Address
          formatDate(),                                      // RegisteredAt — stamped at creation
          "",                                                // PhotoURL
          0,                                                 // MonthlyTarget
          "",                                                // LastLogin
          _addDob,                                           // DOB
          "",                                                // TokenExpiry
          _addContribStart,                                  // ContribStartDate — optional, admin-set
          ""                                                 // InactiveSince — blank, user starts Active
        ]);
        logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add User", "UserId: " + newUserId + " | Mobile: " + mobile + " | Name: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Name||"",100) + " | Role: " + role);

        // Send welcome email — same style as approval email since admin is directly activating.
        // Best-effort: never fail the addUser response if email fails.
        const _addEmail = email;
        if (_addEmail && tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
          try {
            const _addUserObj = {
              Name:   sanitize(e.parameter.Name, 100),
              Mobile: mobile,
              Email:  _addEmail,
              UserId: newUserId,
              Role:   role
            };
            MailApp.sendEmail({
              to:       _addEmail,
              subject:  CFG.name + " — Your Account Has Been Created!",
              htmlBody: _buildAdminAddedEmail(_addUserObj)
            });
          } catch(mailErr) {
            logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "ADD_USER_EMAIL_ERROR",
              "UserId: " + newUserId + " | To: " + _addEmail, mailErr.message, "",
              { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
          }
        }

        result = { status: "success", userId: newUserId };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── FORGOT PASSWORD Step 1: look up by mobile, return masked email
  //  Security: generic error — never reveals whether mobile exists
  else if (action === "lookupMobileForReset") {
    const mobile = sanitize(e.parameter.mobile, 15);
    if (!mobile || !/^[6-9]\d{9}$/.test(mobile)) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Enter a valid 10-digit mobile number." };
    } else {
      const users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      const user  = users.find(u =>
        String(u.Mobile || "") === mobile &&
        ["active","pending"].indexOf(String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase()) !== -1
      );
      if (!user) {
        // Generic — do not reveal if mobile exists or not
        logAction(mobile, "MOBILE_RESET_LOOKUP", "Mobile: " + mobile, "No active account found", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "No active account found for this mobile number." };
      } else {
        // Mask email: m***@g***.com
        const em = String(user.Email || "");
        const at = em.indexOf("@");
        let masked = em;
        if (at > 1) {
          const local  = em.substring(0, at);
          const domain = em.substring(at + 1);
          const dDot   = domain.indexOf(".");
          const dMask  = (dDot > 1 ? domain.substring(0,1) + "***" + domain.substring(dDot) : domain);
          masked = local.substring(0,1) + "***@" + dMask;
        }
        logAction(mobile, "MOBILE_RESET_LOOKUP", "UserId: " + user.UserId + " | Mobile: " + mobile, "Masked email returned for password reset", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
        result = { status: "success", userId: user.UserId, maskedEmail: masked };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── FORGOT PASSWORD Step 2: send OTP to the server-known email (never from client)
  //  Security: userId from step 1 — client cannot specify which email to send to
  else if (action === "sendForgotPasswordOTP") {
    const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    if (!userId) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid request." };
    } else {
      const users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      const user  = users.find(u => String(u.UserId || "") === userId &&
        ["active","pending"].indexOf(String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase()) !== -1
      );
      if (!user || !user.Email) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Account not found." };
      } else if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Email limit reached for today. Please try again tomorrow." };
      } else {
        const otp = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000);
        CacheService.getScriptCache().put("fpotp_" + userId, String(otp), 600); // 10 min TTL
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to: user.Email,
          subject: CFG.name + " — Password Reset Code",
          htmlBody: `<div style="max-width:480px;margin:0 auto;font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;
              background:#fff;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
            <div style="background:#0F766E;padding:20px 28px;text-align:center;">
              <div style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;">${CFG.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div style="padding:26px 28px;">
              <p style="color:#475569;font-size:13.5px;margin:0 0 6px;">A password reset was requested for your account. Use this code:</p>
              <div style="text-align:center;color:#0F766E;font-size:42px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:8px;margin:18px 0;">${otp}</div>
              <p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12.5px;margin:0;">This code expires in 10 minutes. If you did not request this, please ignore this email.</p>
            </div>
            <div style="background:#f6f9f8;padding:12px 28px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
              <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">${CFG.name} | ${CFG.location}</div>
            </div>
          </div>`
        });
        logAction(userId, "FORGOT_PASSWORD_OTP_SENT", "UserId: " + userId, "Password reset OTP sent to registered email", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
        result = { status: "success" };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── LEGACY: keep sendEmailOTP for backward compatibility (old clients)
  else if (action === "sendEmailOTP") {
    result = { status: "error", message: "This flow has been updated. Please use the latest version of the app." };
  }

  // ── RESET PASSWORD
  else if (action === "resetPassword") {
    const cache      = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const userId     = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
    const savedOtp   = cache.get("fpotp_" + userId) || cache.get("otp_" + userId); // fpotp_ = new key, otp_ = legacy
    const userOtp    = sanitize(e.parameter.otp, 10);
    if (savedOtp && userOtp === savedOtp) {
      let sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
      let data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      let headers = data[0];
      let pwdCol  = headers.indexOf("Password"); // safe header lookup — not hardcoded col 5
      let found   = false;
      let newHashedPwd = sanitize(e.parameter.NewPassword, 128);
      if (pwdCol === -1) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Password column not found in USERS sheet." };
      } else {
        for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
          if (String(data[i][headers.indexOf("UserId")] || data[i][0]) === userId) {
            sheet.getRange(i + 1, pwdCol + 1).setValue(newHashedPwd);
            SpreadsheetApp.flush();
            cache.remove("fpotp_" + userId); cache.remove("otp_" + userId); // clear both keys
            found = true;
            logAction("System", "Password Reset", "UserId: " + userId);
            break;
          }
        }
        result = found ? { status: "success" } : { status: "error", message: "User not found." };
      }
    } else {
      logAction(userId || "Unknown", "RESET_PASSWORD_OTP_FAILED", "UserId: " + (userId||"Unknown"), savedOtp ? "Wrong OTP supplied" : "OTP expired or not found", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
      result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid or expired OTP." };
    }
  }

  else if (action === "changePassword") {
      result = _changePassword(e.parameter);
  }

  else if (action === "deleteUser") {
    let id = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
    // [UNDO-FIX] Read the full user row BEFORE deleting so we can return the
    // password hash to the frontend. getAllData strips Password for security,
    // so the undo snapshot never has it — we attach it here to the delete
    // response and the frontend stores it in _undoSaved for the restore call.
    const _allUsersRaw = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS); // has Password (not stripped here)
    const _delUser = _allUsersRaw.find(u => String(u.UserId) === id);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.USERS, id);
    if (result.status === "deleted") {
      // Return password hash so undo can restore it exactly
      if (_delUser && _delUser.Password) result.passwordHash = _delUser.Password;
      // Delete profile photo from Drive if one exists
      try {
        const _photoUrl = String(_delUser && _delUser.PhotoURL || e.parameter.PhotoURL || "").trim();
        if (_photoUrl) {
          let _photoFileId = "";
          if (_photoUrl.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/")) _photoFileId = _photoUrl.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
          else if (_photoUrl.includes("drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=")) _photoFileId = _photoUrl.split("id=")[1].split("&")[0].trim();
          if (_photoFileId && _photoFileId.length > 10) {
            DriveApp.getFileById(_photoFileId).setTrashed(true);
            logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Profile Photo Deleted", "UserId: " + id + " | DriveFileId: " + _photoFileId, "Deleted with user account", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
          }
        }
      } catch(_photoErr) { /* photo deletion is best-effort — do not block user delete */ }
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete User",
        "UserId: " + id + (_delUser ? " | Name: " + (_delUser.Name||"") + " | Mobile: " + (_delUser.Mobile||"") + " | Role: " + (_delUser.Role||"") : ""),
        "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SUCCESS" });
    }
  }

  // ── RESTORE USER (undo-delete) ────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Re-inserts a deleted user with their ORIGINAL UserId and ALL original data.
  // _genUserId() is NOT called. Only triggered by admin undo-delete flow.
  // Password: getAllData strips it for security, so deleteUser now returns the
  // hash in its response and the frontend passes it back here via e.parameter.Password.
  // All 16 USERS columns written in exact sheet order — no data lost.
  else if (action === "restoreUser") {
    const restoreId = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
    const restoreName = sanitize(e.parameter.Name, 100);
    if (!restoreId || !restoreName) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Missing UserId or Name for restore." };
    } else {
      const existingUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      if (existingUsers.some(u => String(u.UserId) === restoreId)) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "User already exists — restore aborted." };
      } else {
        // Password: use whatever was sent (should be the hash returned by deleteUser)
        // If somehow empty, write empty string — user can reset via forgot password.
        const pwd = sanitize(e.parameter.Password || "", 200);
        // Sheet column order must exactly match canonical header order (line 2495):
        // UserId,Name,Mobile,Role,Password,Email,Status,SessionToken,
        // Village,Address,RegisteredAt,PhotoURL,MonthlyTarget,LastLogin,DOB,TokenExpiry
        addRow(SHEETS.USERS, [
          restoreId,                                                     // UserId
          restoreName,                                                   // Name
          sanitize(e.parameter.Mobile       || "", 15),                 // Mobile
          sanitize(e.parameter.Role         || "User", 20),             // Role
          pwd,                                                           // Password (hash)
          sanitize(e.parameter.Email        || "", 200).toLowerCase(),  // Email
          sanitize(e.parameter.Status       || "Active", 20),           // Status
          "",                                                            // SessionToken — cleared
          sanitize(e.parameter.Village      || "", 100),                // Village
          sanitize(e.parameter.Address      || "", 300),                // Address
          sanitize(e.parameter.RegisteredAt || "", 30),                 // RegisteredAt
          sanitize(e.parameter.PhotoURL     || "", 500),                // PhotoURL
          // [FIX] Never use (val || 0) — "0" is falsy so a real 0 becomes 0 correctly
          // but an absent param (undefined) also needs 0. Use explicit check instead.
          (e.parameter.MonthlyTarget !== undefined && e.parameter.MonthlyTarget !== "")
            ? Number(e.parameter.MonthlyTarget) : 0,                    // MonthlyTarget
          sanitize(e.parameter.LastLogin    || "", 30),                 // LastLogin
          sanitize(e.parameter.DOB          || "", 12),                 // DOB
          ""                                                             // TokenExpiry — cleared
        ]);
        // [FIX-11] Force DOB cell to plain text after restore — same as addUser.
        // Prevents Google Sheets auto-converting "dd-MM-yyyy" strings to Date objects
        // which flip the format to mm-dd-yyyy on subsequent reads.
        try {
          const _restoreSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
          if (_restoreSheet) {
            const _restoreHdrs = _restoreSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, _restoreSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
            const _restoreDobCol = _restoreHdrs.indexOf("DOB");
            if (_restoreDobCol !== -1) {
              _restoreSheet.getRange(_restoreSheet.getLastRow(), _restoreDobCol + 1).setNumberFormat("@");
            }
          }
        } catch(_rDobErr) { /* non-fatal */ }
        logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Restore User",
          "UserId: " + restoreId + " | Name: " + restoreName,
          "Restored via undo-delete", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
        result = { status: "success", userId: restoreId };
      }
    }
  }
  else if (action === "updateUser")      { result = updateUser(e.parameter); }
  // ── CONTRIBUTION TYPES (with permanent SortOrder) ──────────────
  else if (action === "addType") {
    var nextSort = _getNextSortOrder(SHEETS.TYPES);
    addRow(SHEETS.TYPES, [generateSheetId("TYPE"), sanitize(e.parameter.TypeName, 100), nextSort]);
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Type", sanitize(e.parameter.TypeName||"",100));
    _bustSheetCache("c_types");
    result = { status: "success" };
  }
  else if (action === "deleteType") {
    let id = sanitize(e.parameter.TypeId, 30);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.TYPES, id);
    _bustSheetCache("c_types");
    if (result.status === "deleted") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete Type", "TypeId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.TypeId||id,30));
  }
  else if (action === "updateType") {
    result = updateSingle(SHEETS.TYPES, sanitize(e.parameter.TypeId,30), sanitize(e.parameter.TypeName,100));
    _bustSheetCache("c_types");
    if (result && result.status === "updated") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Type", "TypeId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.TypeId,30));
  }
  else if (action === "updateSortOrder") {
    // FIX: wrap JSON.parse in try-catch — malformed order param would crash doGet
    let _sortOrder = [];
    try { _sortOrder = JSON.parse(e.parameter.order || "[]"); } catch(ex) { _sortOrder = []; }
    result = _updateSortOrder(sanitize(e.parameter.sheet, 20), _sortOrder, sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100));
  }

  // ── OCCASIONS (with permanent SortOrder) ────────────────────────
  else if (action === "addOccasion") {
    var nextSort = _getNextSortOrder(SHEETS.OCCASIONS);
    addRow(SHEETS.OCCASIONS, [generateSheetId("OCC"), sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionName, 100), nextSort]);
    _bustSheetCache("c_occasions");
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Occasion", sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionName,100));
    result = { status: "success" };
  }
  else if (action === "deleteOccasion")  {
    const _delOccId = sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionId,30);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.OCCASIONS, _delOccId);
    _bustSheetCache("c_occasions");
    if (result.status === "deleted") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete Occasion", "OccasionId: " + _delOccId);
  }
  else if (action === "updateOccasion")  {
    result = updateSingle(SHEETS.OCCASIONS, sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionId,30), sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionName,100));
    _bustSheetCache("c_occasions");
    if (result && result.status === "updated") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Occasion", "OccasionId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionId,30));
  }

  // ── EXPENSE TYPES (with permanent SortOrder) ─────────────────────
  else if (action === "addExpenseType") {
    var nextSort = _getNextSortOrder(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES);
    addRow(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES, [generateSheetId("EXPT"), sanitize(e.parameter.Name, 100), nextSort]);
    _bustSheetCache("c_exptypes");
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Expense Type", sanitize(e.parameter.Name,100));
    result = { status: "success" };
  }
  else if (action === "deleteExpenseType") {
    const _delEtId = sanitize(e.parameter.ExpenseTypeId,30);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES, _delEtId);
    _bustSheetCache("c_exptypes");
    if (result.status === "deleted") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Delete Expense Type", "ExpenseTypeId: " + _delEtId);
  }
  else if (action === "updateExpenseType"){
    result=updateSingle(SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES,sanitize(e.parameter.ExpenseTypeId,30),sanitize(e.parameter.Name,100));
    _bustSheetCache("c_exptypes");
    if (result && result.status === "updated") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Expense Type", "ExpenseTypeId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.ExpenseTypeId,30));
  }

  // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  //  IMPROVEMENT #1 + #3 — ADD CONTRIBUTION
  //  [ID] Contribution row ID: CONT-00001 (never resets)
  //  [ID] Walk-in UserId: WALKIN_2025_00001 (year-wise, generated here)
  //  Receipt ID: MNR-2025-00001 (year-wise, uses selected Year)
  // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  else if (action === "addContribution") {
    // ── [GUARANTEE] Idempotency check — see _idempotencyCheckAndReserve() above.
    // If this exact request (same IdempotencyKey) already ran, replay its
    // result instead of inserting a second row.
    const idemKey = sanitize(e.parameter.IdempotencyKey, 100);
    if (idemKey) {
      const _idemPrior = _idempotencyCheckAndReserve(idemKey);
      if (_idemPrior === "__IN_PROGRESS__") {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Previous request for this entry is still processing. Please wait a moment.", errorCode: "duplicate_in_progress" };
        return ContentService
          .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify(result) + ")")
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
      }
      if (_idemPrior) {
        // Already completed on a prior attempt — hand back the ORIGINAL result verbatim.
        return ContentService
          .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + _idemPrior + ")")
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
      }
    }
    const suppliedReceiptId = sanitize(e.parameter.ReceiptID, 30);
    const year        = sanitize(e.parameter.Year, 10);
    // [FIX-9] If client supplies a ReceiptID, verify it doesn't already exist in CONTRIBUTIONS.
    // A duplicate receipt ID silently creates two records under the same ID.
    if (suppliedReceiptId) {
      const _existingContribs = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);
      if (_existingContribs.some(c => String(c.ReceiptID || "") === suppliedReceiptId)) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Receipt ID already exists: " + suppliedReceiptId + ". Please use a unique receipt ID." };
        return ContentService
          .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify(result) + ")")
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
      }
    }
    const receiptId   = suppliedReceiptId || generateReceiptId(year);
    const paymentMode = sanitize(e.parameter.PaymentMode, 30) || "UPI";
    // [ID] Walk-in signal: frontend sends UserId="WALKIN" → backend generates WALKIN_YYYY_NNNNN
    // [FIX-1] Use WalkInYear param (form's selected year) so backdated entries get correct year in UserId
    let userId = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
    if (userId === "WALKIN") {
      const walkInYear = sanitize(e.parameter.WalkInYear, 10) || String(new Date().getFullYear());
      userId = generateSheetIdForYear("WALKIN", walkInYear); // e.g. WALKIN_2025_00001
    }
    const amount      = Number(sanitize(e.parameter.Amount, 20)) || 0;
    const forMonth    = sanitize(e.parameter.ForMonth, 20);
    const typeId      = sanitize(e.parameter.TypeId, 30);
    const occasionId  = sanitize(e.parameter.OccasionId, 30);
    const note        = sanitize(e.parameter.Note, 500);
    const suppliedPaymentDate = sanitize(e.parameter.PaymentDate, 30);
    const paymentDate         = suppliedPaymentDate || formatDate();
    // [ID] Sequential contribution row ID: CONT-00001
    const contribId = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30) || generateSheetId("CONT");

    addRow(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS, [
      contribId,
      userId,
      amount,
      paymentDate,
      forMonth,
      year,
      typeId,
      occasionId,
      note,
      receiptId,
      paymentMode
    ]);
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Contribution", "Id: " + contribId + " | UserId: " + userId + " | Amount: ₹" + amount + " | Receipt: " + receiptId + " | Month: " + forMonth + " " + year + " | Mode: " + paymentMode);

    // #1 — Send receipt email (quota-guarded)
    // Case A: Walk-in entry with a directly provided email (WalkInEmail param)
    // Case B: Regular member contribution when auto_receipt toggle is ON
    let emailSent = false;
    let emailSkipped = false;
    try {
      const walkInEmail = sanitize(e.parameter.WalkInEmail || "", 200).trim();
      const isWalkIn    = userId.indexOf("WALKIN_") === 0;

      if (isWalkIn && walkInEmail) {
        // Walk-in donor provided an email — always send receipt regardless of auto_receipt toggle
        const types     = getSheetData(SHEETS.TYPES);
        const occasions = getSheetData(SHEETS.OCCASIONS);
        const typeName     = (types.find(t => String(t.TypeId) === typeId) || {}).TypeName || "Contribution";
        const occasionName = (occasions.find(o => String(o.OccasionId) === occasionId) || {}).OccasionName || "";
        // Extract donor name from Note field: "Walk-in: Ramesh Kumar | 9876543210"
        const noteStr  = sanitize(e.parameter.Note || "", 500);
        const nameMatch = noteStr.match(/Walk-in:\s*([^|]+)/);
        const donorName = nameMatch ? nameMatch[1].trim() : "Donor";
        // ✅ FIX: Do NOT call tryConsumeEmailQuota() here.
        // sendReceiptEmail() already calls it atomically inside.
        // Calling it here too was causing DOUBLE quota increment (+2 per email).
        emailSent = sendReceiptEmail(
          walkInEmail, donorName, receiptId,
          amount, forMonth, year,
          typeName, occasionName, note,
          formatDate(), paymentMode
        );
        if (!emailSent) {
          emailSkipped = true;
        }
      } else if (!isWalkIn) {
        // Regular member — send only if auto_receipt toggle is ON
        const emailSettings = getEmailSettings();
        if (emailSettings.auto_receipt) {
          const users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
          const donor = users.find(u => String(u.UserId) === userId);
          if (donor && donor.Email && String(donor.Email).trim() !== "") {
            const types     = getSheetData(SHEETS.TYPES);
            const occasions = getSheetData(SHEETS.OCCASIONS);
            const typeName     = (types.find(t => String(t.TypeId) === typeId) || {}).TypeName || "Contribution";
            const occasionName = (occasions.find(o => String(o.OccasionId) === occasionId) || {}).OccasionName || "";
            // ✅ FIX: Do NOT call tryConsumeEmailQuota() here.
            // sendReceiptEmail() already calls it atomically inside.
            // Calling it here too was causing DOUBLE quota increment (+2 per email).
            emailSent = sendReceiptEmail(
              donor.Email, donor.Name, receiptId,
              amount, forMonth, year,
              typeName, occasionName, note,
              formatDate(), paymentMode
            );
            if (!emailSent) {
              emailSkipped = true;
            }
          } else {
          }
        } else {
        }
      }
    } catch(emailErr) {
      // Non-fatal — contribution was already saved. Log so admins know email failed.
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "RECEIPT_EMAIL_ERROR", "ReceiptId: " + receiptId + " | UserId: " + userId, emailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:emailErr });
    }

    result = {
      status:        "success",
      receiptId:     receiptId,
      walkInUserId:  userId.indexOf("WALKIN_") === 0 ? userId : undefined, // [FIX-1] Return generated ID to client
      emailSent:     emailSent,
      emailSkipped:  emailSkipped
    };

    // ── [GUARANTEE] Save result under the idempotency key so any retry of
    // this exact request (same key) replays this result instead of
    // inserting a second row. Must happen AFTER the row is safely written.
    if (idemKey) _idempotencySave(idemKey, result);
  }

  // ── ADD EXPENSE — [ID] EXP-2025-00001 (year-wise reset)
  else if (action === "addExpense") {
    // ── [GUARANTEE] Idempotency check — same guard addContribution uses above.
    // If this exact request (same IdempotencyKey) already ran, replay its
    // result instead of inserting a second expense row.
    const expIdemKey = sanitize(e.parameter.IdempotencyKey, 100);
    if (expIdemKey) {
      const _expIdemPrior = _idempotencyCheckAndReserve(expIdemKey);
      if (_expIdemPrior === "__IN_PROGRESS__") {
