        result = { status: "error", message: "Previous request for this entry is still processing. Please wait a moment.", errorCode: "duplicate_in_progress" };
        return ContentService
          .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify(result) + ")")
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
      }
      if (_expIdemPrior) {
        // Already completed on a prior attempt — hand back the ORIGINAL result verbatim.
        return ContentService
          .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + _expIdemPrior + ")")
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
      }
    }

    const expYear = sanitize(e.parameter.Year, 10) || String(new Date().getFullYear());
    // [ID] Year-wise expense ID so each year's expenses count from 00001
    const expId = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30) || generateSheetId("EXP", true);
    addRow(SHEETS.EXPENSES, [
      expId,
      sanitize(e.parameter.Title,         200),
      Number(sanitize(e.parameter.Amount,  20)) || 0,
      formatDate(),
      expYear,
      sanitize(e.parameter.ExpenseTypeId,  30),
      sanitize(e.parameter.ForMonth,       20) || ""
    ]);
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Add Expense", "Id: " + expId + " | Title: " + e.parameter.Title + " | Amount: ₹" + e.parameter.Amount + " | Year: " + expYear);
    result = { status: "success", expId: expId };

    // ── [GUARANTEE] Save result under the idempotency key so any retry of
    // this exact request (same key) replays this result instead of
    // inserting a second row. Must happen AFTER the row is safely written.
    if (expIdemKey) _idempotencySave(expIdemKey, result);
  }

  else if (action === "deleteContribution") {
    let id    = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30);
    let admin = sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName || "Admin", 100);
    const _dc = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS).find(r => String(r.Id) === id);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS, id);
    if (result.status === "deleted") logAction(admin, "Delete Contribution", "Id: " + id + (_dc ? " | UserId: " + (_dc.UserId||"") + " | Amount: ₹" + (_dc.Amount||0) + " | Month: " + (_dc.ForMonth||"") + " " + (_dc.Year||"") + " | Receipt: " + (_dc.ReceiptID||"") : ""), "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SUCCESS" });
  }
  else if (action === "deleteExpense") {
    let id    = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30);
    let admin = sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName || "Admin", 100);
    const _de = getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES).find(r => String(r.Id) === id);
    result = deleteRow(SHEETS.EXPENSES, id);
    if (result.status === "deleted") logAction(admin, "Delete Expense", "Id: " + id + (_de ? " | Title: " + (_de.Title||"") + " | Amount: ₹" + (_de.Amount||0) + " | Month: " + (_de.ForMonth||"") + " " + (_de.Year||"") : ""), "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SUCCESS" });
  }
  else if (action === "updateContribution") {
    result = updateRow(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS, e.parameter);
    if (result.status === "updated") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Contribution", "Id: " + e.parameter.Id + " | Amount: ₹" + (e.parameter.Amount||"") + " | Month: " + (e.parameter.ForMonth||"") + " " + (e.parameter.Year||""));
  }
  else if (action === "updateExpense") {
    result = updateExpenseRow(SHEETS.EXPENSES, e.parameter);
    if (result.status === "updated") logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Update Expense", "Id: " + e.parameter.Id + " | Title: " + (e.parameter.Title||"") + " | Amount: ₹" + (e.parameter.Amount||""));
  }

  // ── ANNOUNCEMENTS & BROADCASTS (unchanged from original)
  else if (action === "getAnnouncement")        { result = _getAnnouncement(); }
  else if (action === "getAnnouncementHistory") { result = _getAnnouncementHistory(); }
  else if (action === "getBroadcasts")          { result = _getBroadcasts(); }
  else if (action === "saveAnnouncement")       { result = _saveAnnouncement(e); }
  else if (action === "clearAnnouncement")      { result = _clearAnnouncement(e); }
  else if (action === "saveBroadcast")          { result = _saveBroadcast(e); }
  else if (action === "deleteBroadcast")        { result = _deleteBroadcast(e); }

      else if (action === "removeExpenseReceipt" || action === "removeOneExpenseReceipt") {
      // removeOneExpenseReceipt: removes a single URL from the ReceiptURLs array
      try {
        const expId     = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30);
        const urlToRemove = sanitize(e.parameter.ReceiptURL || e.parameter.OldReceiptURL, 500);
        const adminName = sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName, 100) || "Admin";
        const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
        const data2   = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const hdrs    = data2[0];
        const rcptCol  = hdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURL");
        const urlsCol  = hdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURLs");
        for (let i = 1; i < data2.length; i++) {
          if (String(data2[i][0]) === expId) {
            // Parse existing array
            let urls = [];
            if (urlsCol !== -1 && data2[i][urlsCol]) {
              try { urls = JSON.parse(data2[i][urlsCol]); } catch(ex) {}
            }
            if (!Array.isArray(urls) || urls.length === 0) {
              // Legacy: single URL in ReceiptURL column
              if (rcptCol !== -1) urls = [String(data2[i][rcptCol] || "")].filter(Boolean);
            }
            // Trash the Drive file being removed
            if (urlToRemove && urlToRemove.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/")) {
              try {
                const fid = urlToRemove.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
                if (fid && fid.length > 10) DriveApp.getFileById(fid).setTrashed(true);
              } catch(driveErr) {}
            }
            // Remove the URL from array
            urls = urls.filter(function(u) { return u !== urlToRemove; });
            const newJson = JSON.stringify(urls);
            const firstUrl = urls[0] || "";
            if (urlsCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, urlsCol + 1).setValue(newJson);
            if (rcptCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, rcptCol + 1).setValue(firstUrl);
            SpreadsheetApp.flush();
            logAction(adminName, "removeOneExpenseReceipt", "ExpenseId: " + expId);
            result = { status: "success", receiptUrls: newJson, receiptUrl: firstUrl };
            break;
          }
        }
        if (!result || !result.status) result = { status: "error", message: "Expense not found." };
      } catch(err) {
        logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "REMOVE_RECEIPT_ERROR", "ExpenseId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Id||"",30), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
        result = { status: "error", message: err.message };
      }
    }

    else if (action === "removeAllExpenseReceipts") {
      try {
        const expId     = sanitize(e.parameter.Id, 30);
        const adminName = sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName, 100) || "Admin";
        const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
        const data2   = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const hdrs    = data2[0];
        const rcptCol  = hdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURL");
        const urlsCol  = hdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURLs");
        // Parse URLs to trash from client-sent list
        let urlsToTrash = [];
        try { urlsToTrash = JSON.parse(sanitize(e.parameter.OldReceiptURLs, 5000) || "[]"); } catch(ex) {}
        urlsToTrash.forEach(function(u) {
          if (u && u.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/")) {
            try {
              const fid = u.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
              if (fid && fid.length > 10) DriveApp.getFileById(fid).setTrashed(true);
            } catch(driveErr) {}
          }
        });
        for (let i = 1; i < data2.length; i++) {
          if (String(data2[i][0]) === expId) {
            if (urlsCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, urlsCol + 1).setValue("[]");
            if (rcptCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, rcptCol + 1).setValue("");
            SpreadsheetApp.flush();
            break;
          }
        }
        logAction(adminName, "removeAllExpenseReceipts", "ExpenseId: " + expId);
        result = { status: "success" };
      } catch(err) {
        logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "REMOVE_ALL_RECEIPTS_ERROR", "ExpenseId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Id||"",30), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
        result = { status: "error", message: err.message };
      }
    }

  // ── HEALTH CHECK
  else if (action === "getHealthCheck") {
    try {
      const ss     = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
      const props  = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
      const quota  = getEmailQuotaStatus();
      const checks = {};

      // Check all required sheets exist
      const requiredSheets = ["USERS","CONTRIBUTIONS","EXPENSES","GOALS","TYPES",
        "OCCASIONS","EXPENSE_TYPES","AUDIT_LOGS","SETTINGS","GALLERY",
        "ANNOUNCEMENT","BROADCAST","EVENTS","EVENT_EXPENSES","CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS"];
      requiredSheets.forEach(function(name) {
        checks["sheet_" + name] = !!ss.getSheetByName(name);
      });

      // Per-year receipt counters (new system — one key per year: RECEIPT_CNT_YYYY)
      const _hcCurYr = new Date().getFullYear();
      for (var _ry = _hcCurYr - 2; _ry <= _hcCurYr + 1; _ry++) {
        var _rval = parseInt(props.getProperty("RECEIPT_CNT_" + _ry) || "0", 10);
        if (_rval > 0) checks["receipt_count_" + _ry] = _rval;
      }
      // Legacy single counter — no longer incremented, kept for reference only
      checks["receipt_counter_legacy"] = parseInt(props.getProperty("RECEIPT_COUNTER") || "0", 10);
      

      // Email quota
      checks["email_used"]      = quota.used;
      checks["email_limit"]     = quota.limit;
      checks["email_remaining"] = quota.remaining;
      // ── Row counts for each sheet ──
      requiredSheets.forEach(function(name) {
        var s = ss.getSheetByName(name);
        checks["sheet_rows_" + name] = s ? Math.max(0, s.getLastRow() - 1) : 0;
      });

      // ── Column integrity check per sheet ──
      var expectedCols = {
        "USERS":                 ["UserId","Name","Mobile","Role","Password","Email","Status","SessionToken","Village","Address","RegisteredAt","PhotoURL","MonthlyTarget","LastLogin","DOB","TokenExpiry","ContribStartDate","InactiveSince","SessionTTL"],
        "CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS": ["ReqId","UserId","Amount","PaymentMode","ForMonth","Year","Note","UtrRef","Status","RequestedAt","SlipURL","RejectionNote"],
        "BROADCAST":             ["BcId","Type","Priority","Title","Message","Time","AdminName"],
        "CONTRIBUTIONS":         ["Id","UserId","Amount","PaymentDate","ForMonth","Year","TypeId","OccasionId","Note","ReceiptID","PaymentMode"],
        "EXPENSES":              ["Id","Title","Amount","PaymentDate","Year","ExpenseTypeId","ForMonth","ReceiptURL","ReceiptURLs"],
        "GOALS":                 ["GoalId","GoalName","TargetAmount","CurrentAmount","Status","CreatedAt"],
        "TYPES":                 ["TypeId","TypeName","SortOrder"],
        "OCCASIONS":             ["OccasionId","OccasionName","SortOrder"],
        "EXPENSE_TYPES":         ["ExpenseTypeId","Name","SortOrder"],
        "EVENTS":                ["EventId","EventName","Category","StartDate","EndDate","Budget","Status","Description","CreatedAt","AdminName"],
        "EVENT_EXPENSES":        ["Id","EventId","Title","Amount","PaymentDate","ExpenseTypeId","ForMonth","Note","AdminName"],
        "GALLERY":               ["ImageId","Title","PhotoURL","Priority","Status","CreatedAt","Tags"],
        "SETTINGS":              ["Key","Value","UpdatedAt"],
        "FEEDBACK":              ["Timestamp","Name","Mobile","Address","Message","Status"],
        "CHATBOT_CONFIG":        ["Key","Value","UpdatedAt"],
        "AUDIT_LOGS":            ["Timestamp","Actor","Action","Result","Details","Reason","Error","DeviceInfo","Severity"],
        "ANNOUNCEMENT":          ["AnnId","Message","Badge","Icon","Color","Status","AdminName","CreatedAt"],
        "YEAR_CONFIG":           ["Year","OpeningBalance"]
      };

      Object.keys(expectedCols).forEach(function(name) {
        var s = ss.getSheetByName(name);
        if (!s) { checks["sheet_col_" + name] = "Sheet missing"; return; }
        var lastCol = s.getLastColumn();
        if (lastCol === 0) { checks["sheet_col_" + name] = "Sheet is empty"; return; }
        var actual   = s.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0].map(function(h){ return String(h).trim(); });
        var expected = expectedCols[name];
        var missing  = expected.filter(function(c){ return actual.indexOf(c) === -1; });
        var extra    = actual.filter(function(c){ return c !== "" && expected.indexOf(c) === -1; });
        if (missing.length === 0 && extra.length === 0) {
          checks["sheet_col_" + name] = true;
        } else {
          var msg = [];
          if (missing.length > 0) msg.push("Missing: " + missing.join(", "));
          if (extra.length > 0)   msg.push("Unknown: " + extra.join(", "));
          checks["sheet_col_" + name] = msg.join(" | ");
        }
      });

      // Backup — find latest backup in Mandir_Backups folder
      let lastBackup = "Never";
      try {
        const folderIter = DriveApp.getRootFolder().getFoldersByName("Mandir_Backups");
        if (folderIter.hasNext()) {
          const backupFolder = folderIter.next();
          const files = backupFolder.getFiles();
          let latest = null;
          while (files.hasNext()) {
            const f = files.next();
            if (!latest || f.getDateCreated() > latest.getDateCreated()) latest = f;
          }
          if (latest) lastBackup = Utilities.formatDate(latest.getDateCreated(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm");
        }
      } catch(be) {}
      checks["last_backup"] = lastBackup;

      // CFG version
      checks["version"] = CFG.version || "—";

      result = { status: "ok", checks: checks };
    } catch(err) {
      result = { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
  }

  // ── TRAFFIC STATS
  else if (action === "getTrafficStats") {
    result = getTrafficStats();
  }

  // ── RESET TRAFFIC STATS (manual reset from admin panel)
  else if (action === "resetTrafficStats") {
    result = resetTrafficStats();
  }

  // ── MONTHLY CONTRIBUTION REMINDER (trigger on 25th via Time-based trigger)
  else if (action === "sendMonthlyReminders") {
    result = sendMonthlyReminders(e.parameter.month || null, e.parameter.year || null, false);
  }

  // ── M16: Send OTP to verify NEW mobile number before changing
  else if (action === "sendMobileChangeOTP") {
    const userId    = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    const newMobile = sanitize(e.parameter.newMobile, 15);
    if (!newMobile || !/^[6-9]\d{9}$/.test(newMobile)) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid mobile number format." };
    } else {
      // Check if new mobile already taken
      const users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      const taken = users.find(u => String(u.Mobile||"") === newMobile && String(u.UserId||"") !== userId);
      if (taken) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "This mobile number is already registered to another account." };
      } else if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Email limit reached. Please try again tomorrow." };
      } else {
        const user = users.find(u => String(u.UserId||"") === userId);
        if (!user || !user.Email) {
          result = { status: "error", message: "Your account email is not set. Cannot send OTP." };
        } else {
          const otp = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000);
          CacheService.getScriptCache().put("mobile_otp_" + userId, JSON.stringify({otp: String(otp), newMobile: newMobile}), 600);
          MailApp.sendEmail({
            to: String(user.Email).trim(),
            subject: CFG.name + " — Mobile Number Change OTP",
            htmlBody: `<div style="max-width:480px;margin:0 auto;font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;
              background:#fff;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
              <div style="background:#0F766E;padding:20px 28px;text-align:center;">
                <div style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;">Mobile Number Change</div>
              </div>
              <div style="padding:26px 28px;">
                <p style="color:#475569;font-size:13.5px;margin:0 0 6px;">You requested to change your registered mobile to: <strong style="color:#1e293b;">${newMobile}</strong></p>
                <div style="text-align:center;color:#0F766E;font-size:42px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:8px;margin:18px 0;">${otp}</div>
                <p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12.5px;margin:0;">This code expires in 10 minutes. Do not share it.</p>
              </div>
              <div style="background:#f6f9f8;padding:12px 28px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
                <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">${CFG.name} | ${CFG.location}</div>
              </div>
            </div>`
          });
          logAction(userId, "MOBILE_CHANGE_OTP_SENT", "UserId: " + userId + " | NewMobile: " + newMobile.substring(0,4) + "***", "Mobile change OTP sent to registered email", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
          result = { status: "success", message: "OTP sent to your registered email." };
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // ── M16: Verify OTP and update mobile number
  else if (action === "verifyMobileChangeOTP") {
    const userId    = sanitize(e.parameter.userId, 30);
    const userOtp   = sanitize(e.parameter.otp, 10);
    const cache     = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const raw       = cache.get("mobile_otp_" + userId);
    if (!raw) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "OTP expired or not found. Please request a new OTP." };
    } else {
      const saved = JSON.parse(raw);
      if (saved.otp !== userOtp) {
        logAction(userId, "MOBILE_CHANGE_OTP_FAILED", "UserId: " + userId, "Wrong OTP supplied for mobile change", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Incorrect OTP. Please try again." };
      } else {
        // OTP valid — update mobile
        cache.remove("mobile_otp_" + userId);
        const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
        const allData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers = allData[0];
        const mobileCol = headers.indexOf("Mobile");
        if (mobileCol === -1) { result = { status: "error", message: "Mobile column not found." }; }
        else {
          let found = false;
          for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
            if (String(allData[i][headers.indexOf("UserId")]||allData[i][0]) === userId) {
              sheet.getRange(i+1, mobileCol+1).setValue(saved.newMobile);
              SpreadsheetApp.flush();
              logAction(userId, "Mobile Number Changed", "UserId: " + userId + " | New: " + saved.newMobile);
              found = true; break;
            }
          }
          result = found ? {status:"success"} : {status:"error",message:"User not found."};
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // ── M4: User submits contribution request (payment proof)
  else if (action === "submitContributionRequest") {
    try {
      const userId  = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
      const amount  = sanitize(e.parameter.Amount, 20);
      const mode    = sanitize(e.parameter.PaymentMode || "UPI", 30);
      const note    = sanitize(e.parameter.Note || "", 500);
      const month   = sanitize(e.parameter.ForMonth || "", 20);
      const year    = sanitize(e.parameter.Year || String(new Date().getFullYear()), 10);
      const utrRef  = sanitize(e.parameter.UtrRef || "", 50);
      const slipUrl = sanitize(e.parameter.SlipURL || "", 500);
      if (!userId || !amount || !month) {
        result = { status:"error", message:"UserId, Amount and Month are required." };
      } else {
        const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
        let reqSheet = ss.getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
        // ── Actual sheet column order (matches live sheet):
        //    A=ReqId  B=UserId  C=Amount  D=PaymentMode  E=ForMonth  F=Year
        //    G=Note   H=UtrRef  I=Status  J=RequestedAt  K=SlipURL   L=RejectionNote
        if (!reqSheet) {
          reqSheet = ss.insertSheet("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
          reqSheet.appendRow(["ReqId","UserId","Amount","PaymentMode","ForMonth","Year","Note","UtrRef","Status","RequestedAt","SlipURL","RejectionNote"]);
          reqSheet.getRange(1,1,1,12).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#334155").setFontColor("#ffffff");
          reqSheet.setFrozenRows(1);
        } else {
          // Ensure SlipURL and RejectionNote columns exist (upgrade existing sheet)
          const hdrs = reqSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, reqSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
          if (!hdrs.includes("SlipURL")) reqSheet.getRange(1, hdrs.length+1).setValue("SlipURL");
          if (!hdrs.includes("RejectionNote")) reqSheet.getRange(1, hdrs.length+1).setValue("RejectionNote");
        }
        const newId = generateSheetId("REQ");
        // Insert in exact sheet column order: ReqId,UserId,Amount,PaymentMode,ForMonth,Year,Note,UtrRef,Status,RequestedAt,SlipURL,RejectionNote
        reqSheet.appendRow([newId, userId, Number(amount)||0, mode, month, year, note, utrRef, "Pending",
          Utilities.formatDate(new Date(),"GMT+5:30","dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss"), slipUrl, ""]);
        logAction(userId, "Contribution Request Submitted", "UserId: " + userId + " | Amount: ₹" + amount + " | Month: " + month + " | Mode: " + mode);
        result = { status:"success", reqId: newId };
      }
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.UserId||"User",30), "CONTRIBUTION_REQUEST_ERROR", "Amount: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Amount||"",20) + " | Month: " + sanitize(e.parameter.ForMonth||"",20), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      result = { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }

  // ── User: edit their own PENDING contribution request
  else if (action === "editContributionRequest") {
    try {
      const reqId   = sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId, 30);
      const userId  = sanitize(e.parameter.UserId, 30);
      const amount  = sanitize(e.parameter.Amount, 20);
      const mode    = sanitize(e.parameter.PaymentMode || "UPI", 30);
      const note    = sanitize(e.parameter.Note || "", 500);
      const month   = sanitize(e.parameter.ForMonth || "", 20);
      const utrRef  = sanitize(e.parameter.UtrRef || "", 50);
      const slipUrl = sanitize(e.parameter.SlipURL || "", 500);
      if (!reqId || !userId || !amount || !month) {
        result = { status:"error", message:"ReqId, UserId, Amount and Month are required." };
      } else {
        const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
        if (!sheet) { result = { status:"error", message:"Sheet not found." }; }
        else {
          const data2 = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
          const hdrs  = data2[0];
          let found = false;
          for (let i = 1; i < data2.length; i++) {
            const rowReqId  = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("ReqId")]  || data2[i][0] || "");
            const rowUserId = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("UserId")] || "");
            const rowStatus = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Status")] || "Pending");
            if (rowReqId === reqId && rowUserId === userId && rowStatus === "Pending") {
              const updates = { Amount: Number(amount)||0, PaymentMode: mode, ForMonth: month, UtrRef: utrRef, Note: note };
              if (slipUrl) updates.SlipURL = slipUrl;
              // Batch all updates into a single setValues() call — avoids 5-6 separate Sheets API round-trips
              const newRow = data2[i].slice();
              for (const [col, val] of Object.entries(updates)) {
                const ci = hdrs.indexOf(col);
                if (ci !== -1) newRow[ci] = val;
              }
              sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);
              SpreadsheetApp.flush();
              logAction(userId, "EditContributionRequest", "ReqId:"+reqId+" Month:"+month+" Amount:"+amount);
              result = { status:"success" };
              found = true;
              break;
            }
          }
          if (!found) result = { status:"error", message:"Pending request not found or not authorized." };
        }
      }
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.UserId||"User",30), "EDIT_CONTRIB_REQUEST_ERROR", "ReqId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId||"",30), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      result = { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }

  // ── User: get their own contribution requests
  else if (action === "getUserContributionRequests") {
    try {
      const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId || e.parameter.UserId || "", 30);
      const sheet  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
      if (!sheet || !userId) { result = []; }
      else {
        const data2 = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        if (data2.length < 2) { result = []; }
        else {
          const hdrs = data2[0];
          result = data2.slice(1).map(r => {
            let o = {}; hdrs.forEach((h,i) => { o[h] = r[i]; }); return o;
          }).filter(r => String(r.UserId || r.userId || "") === userId)
            .reverse();
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { result = []; }
  }

  // ── Admin: get pending contribution requests
  else if (action === "getContributionRequests") {
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
      if (!sheet) { result = []; }
      else {
        const data2 = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        if (data2.length < 2) { result = []; }
        else {
          const hdrs = data2[0];
          // [FIX-12] Return only Pending requests for admin action.
          // Previously returned Pending + Approved (excluded only Rejected).
          // Approved requests would accumulate in the admin view indefinitely
          // until the user manually deleted them.
          result = data2.slice(1).map(r => {
            let o = {}; hdrs.forEach((h,i) => { o[h] = r[i]; }); return o;
          }).filter(r => String(r.Status || "Pending") === "Pending").reverse();
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { result = []; }
  }

  // ── Admin: approve/reject contribution request
  else if (action === "resolveContributionRequest") {
    try {
      const reqId    = sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId, 30);
      const status   = sanitize(e.parameter.Status, 20); // Approved or Rejected
      const admin    = sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName || "Admin", 100);
      const rejNote  = sanitize(e.parameter.RejectionNote || "", 300);
      // Whitelist Status values — prevent arbitrary strings being written to sheet
      const VALID_STATUSES = ["Approved", "Rejected"];
      if (!VALID_STATUSES.includes(status)) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Invalid status value. Must be Approved or Rejected." };
      } else {
      const sheet    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
      if (!sheet) { result = {status:"error",message:"Sheet not found"}; }
      else {
        // Use LockService to prevent dual-admin race condition creating duplicate contributions
        const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
        lock.waitLock(8000);
        try {
        const data2 = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const hdrs  = data2[0];
        const statusCol    = hdrs.indexOf("Status");
        const rejNoteCol   = hdrs.indexOf("RejectionNote");
        for (let i = 1; i < data2.length; i++) {
          if (String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("ReqId")]||data2[i][0]) === reqId) {
            // Check current status inside the lock — prevent duplicate approvals
            const currentStatus = String(data2[i][statusCol] || "Pending");
            if (currentStatus !== "Pending") {
              result = { status: "already_resolved", message: "This request was already resolved by another admin." };
              break;
            }
            sheet.getRange(i+1, statusCol+1).setValue(status);
            if (rejNoteCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i+1, rejNoteCol+1).setValue(rejNote);
            SpreadsheetApp.flush();
            const _rUserId = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("UserId")]  || "");
            const _rMonth  = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("ForMonth")]|| "");
            const _rYear   = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Year")]    || "");
            const _rAmt    = Number(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Amount")]  || 0);
            const _rMode   = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("PaymentMode")]|| "");
            logAction(admin, "ResolveContributionRequest", "ReqId: " + reqId + " | Status: " + status + " | UserId: " + _rUserId + " | Amount: ₹" + _rAmt + " | Month: " + _rMonth + " " + _rYear + " | Mode: " + _rMode + (rejNote ? " | Reason: " + rejNote : ""), "", "", { severity: status === "Rejected" ? "WARN" : "INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
            // Send rejection email to user
            if (status === "Rejected") {
              try {
                const userId   = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("UserId")] || "");
                const forMonth = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("ForMonth")] || "");
                const year     = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Year")] || "");
                const amount   = Number(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Amount")] || 0);
                const allUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
                const donor    = allUsers.find(u => String(u.UserId) === userId);
                const toEmail  = donor ? String(donor.Email || "").trim() : "";
                if (toEmail && tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
                  MailApp.sendEmail({
                    to: toEmail,
                    subject: CFG.name + " — Payment Request Update",
                    htmlBody: _buildContribRejectionEmail(donor, amount, forMonth, year, rejNote)
                  });
                }
              } catch(mailErr) {
                logAction("System", "REJECTION_EMAIL_ERROR", "ReqId: " + reqId + " | UserId: " + String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("UserId")]||""), mailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
              }
            } // end if (status === "Rejected")

            // [FIX-1] When Approved: auto-create the CONTRIBUTIONS row server-side.
            // Previously only the request status was set to "Approved" and the
            // frontend was responsible for calling addContribution separately.
            // If that second call failed, the request showed Approved but no
            // contribution record existed — permanent data loss.
            // Now the server creates the contribution atomically inside the same lock.
            if (status === "Approved") {
              try {
                const _reqNote   = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("Note")]        || "");
                const _reqUtrRef = String(data2[i][hdrs.indexOf("UtrRef")]      || "");
                // Combine UtrRef into note if present so it's visible on the contribution
                const _contribNote = _reqUtrRef
                  ? (_reqNote ? _reqNote + " | UTR: " + _reqUtrRef : "UTR: " + _reqUtrRef)
                  : _reqNote;
                const _newReceiptId  = generateReceiptId(_rYear);
                const _newContribId  = generateSheetId("CONT");
                addRow(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS, [
                  _newContribId,   // Id
                  _rUserId,        // UserId
                  _rAmt,           // Amount
                  formatDate(),    // PaymentDate
                  _rMonth,         // ForMonth
                  _rYear,          // Year
                  "",              // TypeId — not captured in request flow
                  "",              // OccasionId — not captured in request flow
                  _contribNote,    // Note
                  _newReceiptId,   // ReceiptID
                  _rMode           // PaymentMode
                ]);
                logAction(admin, "AutoContribution_OnApproval",
                  "ReqId: " + reqId + " | ContribId: " + _newContribId + " | ReceiptId: " + _newReceiptId + " | UserId: " + _rUserId + " | Amount: ₹" + _rAmt,
                  "Auto-created from approved contribution request", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
                // Return generated IDs to frontend so it can skip its own addContribution call
                result = { status: "success", autoContribId: _newContribId, autoReceiptId: _newReceiptId };
              } catch(_autoContribErr) {
                // Non-fatal — request is already Approved in the sheet. Log clearly.
                logAction(admin, "AUTO_CONTRIB_ON_APPROVAL_ERROR",
                  "ReqId: " + reqId + " | UserId: " + _rUserId + " — contribution row could not be auto-created",
                  _autoContribErr.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:_autoContribErr });
                result = { status: "success" }; // still success — request was approved
              }
            } else {
              result = { status: "success" };
            }
            break;
          } // end for loop
        }
        // Use explicit found flag instead of checking result.status
        if (!result || (result.status !== "success" && result.status !== "already_resolved")) result = {status:"error",message:"Request not found"};
        } finally { lock.releaseLock(); }
      }
      } // end VALID_STATUSES check
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100), "RESOLVE_CONTRIB_REQUEST_ERROR", "ReqId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId||"",30) + " | Status: " + sanitize(e.parameter.Status||"",20), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      result = {status:"error",message:err.message};
    }
  }

  // ── User: delete their own APPROVED or REJECTED contribution request
  else if (action === "deleteContributionRequest") {
    try {
      const reqId  = sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId, 30);
      const userId = sanitize(e.parameter.userId || e.parameter.UserId || "", 30);
      if (!reqId || !userId) { result = { status:"error", message:"ReqId and userId required." }; }
      else {
        const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName("CONTRIBUTION_REQUESTS");
        if (!sheet) { result = { status:"error", message:"Sheet not found." }; }
        else {
          const data2 = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
          const hdrs  = data2[0];
          const idCol     = hdrs.indexOf("ReqId");
          const userCol   = hdrs.indexOf("UserId");
          const statusCol = hdrs.indexOf("Status");
          let found = false;
          for (let i = 1; i < data2.length; i++) {
            const rowReqId  = String(data2[i][idCol]   || data2[i][0] || "");
            const rowUserId = String(data2[i][userCol]  || "");
            const rowStatus = String(data2[i][statusCol]|| "Pending");
            // Only allow deleting Approved or Rejected (not Pending)
            if (rowReqId === reqId && rowUserId === userId && rowStatus !== "Pending") {
              sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
              SpreadsheetApp.flush();
              logAction(userId, "DeleteContributionRequest", "ReqId: " + reqId + " Status: " + rowStatus);
              result = { status:"deleted" }; found = true; break;
            }
          }
          if (!found) result = { status:"error", message:"Request not found or not eligible for deletion." };
        }
      }
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.userId||e.parameter.UserId||"User",30), "DELETE_CONTRIB_REQUEST_ERROR", "ReqId: " + sanitize(e.parameter.ReqId||"",30), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      result = { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }

  // ── Y1: Send OTP for registration email verification
  else if (action === "sendRegistrationOTP") {
    const email = sanitize(e.parameter.email, 200);
    if (!email) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Email is required." };
    } else {
      // Pre-check: is this email already registered in an active/pending/inactive account?
      const allUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
      const existingEmail = allUsers.find(u =>
        String(u.Email || "").toLowerCase() === email.toLowerCase() &&
        String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "rejected"
      );
      if (existingEmail) {
        const es = String(existingEmail.Status || "").toLowerCase();
        if (es === "active") {
          result = { status: "error", message: "This email is already registered. Please login directly or use Forgot Password.", errorCode: "email_active" };
        } else if (es === "pending") {
          result = { status: "error", message: "A registration with this email is already pending approval. Please wait for admin review.", errorCode: "email_pending" };
        } else {
          result = { status: "error", message: "This email address is already in use.", errorCode: "email_exists" };
        }
      } else if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
        result = { status: "error", message: "Email limit reached for today. Please try again tomorrow." };
      } else {
        const otp = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000);
        // [FIX-3] Include a short hash of the full email (not just first 30 chars)
        // to prevent key collisions between similar emails like user+test@gmail.com
        // and user-test@gmail.com which both normalise to "user_test_gmail_com".
        const _emailFull = email.toLowerCase();
        let _eHash = 0;
        for (let _ei = 0; _ei < _emailFull.length; _ei++) {
          _eHash = ((_eHash << 5) - _eHash + _emailFull.charCodeAt(_ei)) | 0;
        }
        const otpKey = "regOtp_" + _emailFull.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g,"_").substring(0,24) + "_" + (_eHash >>> 0).toString(36).substring(0,6);
        CacheService.getScriptCache().put(otpKey, String(otp), 600); // 10 min
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to: email,
          subject: CFG.name + " — Email Verification Code",
          htmlBody: `<div style="max-width:480px;margin:0 auto;font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;
              background:#fff;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
            <div style="background:#0F766E;padding:20px 28px;text-align:center;">
              <div style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;">${CFG.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div style="padding:26px 28px;">
              <p style="color:#475569;font-size:13.5px;margin:0 0 6px;">You are registering a new account. Please verify your email with this code:</p>
              <div style="text-align:center;color:#0F766E;font-size:42px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:8px;margin:18px 0;">${otp}</div>
              <p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12.5px;margin:0;">This code expires in 10 minutes. Do not share it with anyone.</p>
            </div>
            <div style="background:#f6f9f8;padding:12px 28px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
              <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">${CFG.name} | ${CFG.address}</div>
            </div>
          </div>`
        });
        result = { status: "success", otpKey: otpKey };
        logAction("System", "REGISTRATION_OTP_SENT", "Email: " + email.substring(0,3) + "***", "Email verification OTP sent", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
      }
    }
  }

  // ── Y1: Verify registration OTP
  else if (action === "verifyRegistrationOTP") {
    const otpKey  = sanitize(e.parameter.otpKey, 80);
    const userOtp = sanitize(e.parameter.otp, 10);
    if (!otpKey || !userOtp) {
      result = { status: "error", message: "Missing OTP key or code." };
    } else {
      const saved = CacheService.getScriptCache().get(otpKey);
      if (!saved) {
        logAction("Unknown", "REGISTRATION_OTP_FAILED", "OtpKey: " + otpKey.substring(0,20) + "***", "OTP expired or not found", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "OTP expired or not found. Please request a new code." };
      } else if (saved !== userOtp) {
        logAction("Unknown", "REGISTRATION_OTP_FAILED", "OtpKey: " + otpKey.substring(0,20) + "***", "Wrong OTP supplied", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
        result = { status: "error", message: "Incorrect code. Please try again." };
      } else {
        // [FIX-2] Do NOT remove the OTP here. registerUser() verifies AND consumes
        // it atomically (cache.remove inside registerUser). If we remove it here,
        // the subsequent registerUser call gets "otp_expired" and registration fails.
        // This action is now a pure validate-only step — no side effects.
        result = { status: "success" };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── PHOTO PROXY: fetch Drive photo server-side as base64 (solves CORS block in browser)
  // ── PHOTO PROXY: fetch Drive photo server-side as base64 (solves CORS block in browser)
  // Auth: covered by _WRITE_ACTIONS above
  else if (action === "getPhotoBase64") {
    const fileId = sanitize(e.parameter.fileId, 200);
    result = getPhotoBase64(fileId);
  }

  // Returns the logo image (as base64) from CFG.folderLogo for the admin preview card.
  // Uses the same _getLogoUrl() logic so the preview exactly matches what emails will show.
  else if (action === "getEmailLogoPreview") {
    const logoUrl = _getLogoUrl();
    if (!logoUrl) {
      result = { status: "none", message: "No image found in CFG.folderLogo — Om symbol will be used." };
    } else {
      // Extract the file ID from the lh3 URL and proxy it through getPhotoBase64
      const m = logoUrl.match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{10,})/);
      result = m ? getPhotoBase64(m[1]) : { status: "error", message: "Could not parse logo file ID." };
    }
  }

  else if (action === "getTodayBirthdays") {
    try { result = _getTodayBirthdays(e.parameter.userId); }
    catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else if (action === "sendBirthdayWish") {
    try { result = _sendBirthdayWish(e.parameter); }
    catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else if (action === "getMyBirthdayWishes") {
    try { result = _getMyBirthdayWishes(e.parameter.userId); }
    catch(err) { result = { status: "error", message: err.message }; }
  }

  else {
    logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.userId||e.parameter.UserId||"Unknown",30), "INVALID_ACTION", "Action: " + action, "", sanitize(e.parameter.deviceInfo||"",200), { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
    result = { error: "Invalid action: " + action };
  }

  return ContentService
    .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify(result) + ")")
    .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);

} // end doGet — NO outer try-catch by design: Apps Script handles uncaught exceptions
  // at the platform level. Each action branch has its own try-catch above.
  // If you see "Script error" in client, check AUDIT_LOGS for the action name.

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HELPERS
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function _loginCacheKey(mobile) {
  // FIX BUG-1: Previous key used last-4 digits + length, causing collisions between
  // mobiles sharing the same last 4 digits (e.g. 9999999999 and 1239999999 → same key).
  // Now we XOR-scramble the full 10-digit mobile so the raw number isn't in the key
  // but each unique mobile maps to a unique cache key.
  const m = String(mobile).replace(/\D/g, ""); // digits only
  let h = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < m.length; i++) { h = ((h << 5) - h + m.charCodeAt(i)) | 0; }
  return "lfail_" + (h >>> 0).toString(36); // unsigned 32-bit → base-36 string
}
 
function _checkLoginRate(mobile) {
  if (!mobile) return { blocked: false };
  try {
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const key   = _loginCacheKey(mobile);
    const raw   = cache.get(key);
    if (!raw) return { blocked: false };
 
    const rec = JSON.parse(raw);
    if (!rec || !rec.count) return { blocked: false };
 
    // Block after 10 server-side attempts within 15 minutes
    if (rec.count >= 10) {
      return {
        blocked: true,
        message: "Too many login attempts. Please wait 15 minutes before trying again."
      };
    }
    return { blocked: false };
  } catch(e) {
    return { blocked: false }; // on cache error, never block legitimate users
  }
}
 
function _recordLoginFail(mobile) {
  if (!mobile) return;
  try {
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const key   = _loginCacheKey(mobile);
    const raw   = cache.get(key);
    let rec     = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : { count: 0 };
    rec.count   = (rec.count || 0) + 1;
    // TTL: 15 minutes (900 seconds) — resets window on each failure
    cache.put(key, JSON.stringify(rec), 900);
  } catch(e) { /* silent — never crash login on cache error */ }
}
 
function _clearLoginFail(mobile) {
  if (!mobile) return;
  try {
    CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(_loginCacheKey(mobile));
  } catch(e) {}
}

// ── Server-side sheet cache helper (10-min TTL via CacheService)
// Used for master data that rarely changes: Types, Occasions, ExpenseTypes.
// Cache key is short (c_types etc.) to stay under CacheService 250-char key limit.
// On any write that modifies these sheets, call _bustSheetCache(key) to invalidate.
function _cachedSheet(sheetName, cacheKey, ttlSeconds) {
  const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
  const hit   = cache.get(cacheKey);
  if (hit) {
    try { return JSON.parse(hit); } catch(e) { /* corrupt cache — fall through */ }
  }
  const fresh = getSheetData(sheetName);
  try { cache.put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(fresh), ttlSeconds); } catch(e) { /* silent */ }
  return fresh;
}
 
// ── Bust a specific server-side cache key after a write
// Call this inside addType, deleteType, addOccasion etc. after the write completes.
function _bustSheetCache(cacheKey) {
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(cacheKey); } catch(e) {}
}

function getYearlySummary() {
  try {
    const contributions = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);
    const expenses      = getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
    const yearConfigRaw = getSheetData("YEAR_CONFIG");
 
    // ── Collect all years present in contributions or expenses
    const yearSet = new Set();
    contributions.forEach(c => {
      const y = parseInt(c.Year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y) && y > 2000) yearSet.add(y);
    });
    expenses.forEach(e => {
      const y = parseInt(e.Year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y) && y > 2000) yearSet.add(y);
    });
 
    // Also include any years defined in YEAR_CONFIG even if no transactions yet
    yearConfigRaw.forEach(row => {
      const y = parseInt(row.Year || row.year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y) && y > 2000) yearSet.add(y);
    });
 
    // Sort years ascending
    const years = Array.from(yearSet).sort((a, b) => a - b);
 
    // ── Build a lookup for opening balances from YEAR_CONFIG
    // Supports column names: OpeningBalance, Opening_Balance, opening_balance, Balance, balance
    const openingMap = {};
    yearConfigRaw.forEach(row => {
      const y = parseInt(row.Year || row.year, 10);
      if (isNaN(y)) return;
      const ob = Number(
        row.OpeningBalance  || row.Opening_Balance  ||
        row.opening_balance || row.Balance          ||
        row.balance         || 0
      );
      openingMap[y] = isNaN(ob) ? 0 : ob;
    });
 
    // PERF: Pre-aggregate contributions and expenses into Maps keyed by year.
    // This is O(n) instead of O(n * numYears) — avoids re-scanning all rows per year.
    const contribByYear = {};
    contributions.forEach(c => {
      const y = parseInt(c.Year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y)) contribByYear[y] = (contribByYear[y] || 0) + Number(c.Amount || 0);
    });
    const expenseByYear = {};
    expenses.forEach(e => {
      const y = parseInt(e.Year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y)) expenseByYear[y] = (expenseByYear[y] || 0) + Number(e.Amount || 0);
    });

    // [RPT] Pre-aggregate enhanced stats per year: receipt count, expense count, unique members
    const receiptCountByYear = {};
    const expenseCountByYear = {};
    const memberSetByYear    = {};
    contributions.forEach(c => {
      const y = parseInt(c.Year, 10);
      if (isNaN(y)) return;
      receiptCountByYear[y] = (receiptCountByYear[y] || 0) + 1;
      if (!memberSetByYear[y]) memberSetByYear[y] = new Set();
      if (c.UserId && !String(c.UserId).startsWith("WALKIN")) {
        memberSetByYear[y].add(String(c.UserId));
      }
    });
    expenses.forEach(e => {
      const y = parseInt(e.Year, 10);
      if (!isNaN(y)) expenseCountByYear[y] = (expenseCountByYear[y] || 0) + 1;
    });

    // ── Build summary rows with carry-forward chain
    const rows = [];
    let carryForward = 0; // running carry-forward from previous year
 
    years.forEach(year => {
      // Opening balance = YEAR_CONFIG value OR carry-forward from last year
      // YEAR_CONFIG takes priority (admin may have set an explicit opening)
      const configOpening = openingMap[year] || 0;
      // Use explicit config opening if set, else use carry-forward
      const openingBalance = configOpening > 0 ? configOpening : carryForward;
 
      // Use pre-aggregated maps — O(1) lookup per year
      const totalCollection = contribByYear[year] || 0;
      const totalExpense    = expenseByYear[year]  || 0;
 
      // Closing balance = opening + collection - expense
      const closingBalance = openingBalance + totalCollection - totalExpense;
 
      // This year's closing becomes next year's carry-forward
      carryForward = closingBalance;
 
      // [RPT] Enhanced stats for this year
      const rc  = receiptCountByYear[year] || 0;
      const ec  = expenseCountByYear[year] || 0;
      const mc  = memberSetByYear[year] ? memberSetByYear[year].size : 0;
      const avg = rc > 0 ? Math.round(totalCollection / rc) : 0;

      rows.push({
        year:            year,
        openingBalance:  openingBalance,
        totalCollection: totalCollection,
        totalExpense:    totalExpense,
        closingBalance:  closingBalance,
        carryForward:    closingBalance,  // same value — explicit for UI clarity
        receiptCount:    rc,              // how many contribution entries this year
        expenseCount:    ec,              // how many expense entries this year
        memberCount:     mc,              // unique members who contributed (excl. walk-ins)
        avgContribution: avg              // average per receipt this year
      });
    });
 
    return { status: "ok", rows: rows };
 
  } catch(err) {
    return { status: "error", message: err.message, rows: [] };
  }
}

function updateSingle(sheetName, id, value) {
  let sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
  let data  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][0]) === String(id)) { sheet.getRange(i+1,2).setValue(value); return {status:"updated"}; }
  }
  return { status: "not found" };
}

function updateUser(p) {
  // M3 GUARD: Deactivating a user (Status=Inactive) only changes the USERS sheet.
  // CONTRIBUTIONS, EXPENSES and all financial records are NEVER touched here.
  // This is by design — inactive members' historical records must remain visible
  // and counted in all admin reports.

  // [VAL] Server-side mobile + email validation
  if (p.Mobile) {
    const mErr = _validateMobile(sanitize(p.Mobile, 15));
    if (mErr) return { status: "error", message: mErr };
  }
  if (p.Email) {
    const eErr = _validateEmail(sanitize(p.Email, 200));
    if (eErr) return { status: "error", message: eErr };
  }

  // [FIX-6] Duplicate mobile/email guard — prevent admin accidentally assigning
  // another user's mobile or email to this user, which would break login for both.
  const _userId = sanitize(p.UserId, 30);
  const _allUsersForCheck = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  if (p.Mobile) {
    const _mobileConflict = _allUsersForCheck.find(u =>
      String(u.Mobile || "") === sanitize(p.Mobile, 15) &&
      String(u.UserId || "") !== _userId
    );
    if (_mobileConflict) return { status: "error", message: "This mobile number is already registered to another account." };
  }
  if (p.Email && String(p.Email).trim() !== "") {
    const _emailConflict = _allUsersForCheck.find(u =>
      String(u.Email || "").toLowerCase() === sanitize(p.Email, 200).toLowerCase() &&
      String(u.UserId || "") !== _userId &&
      String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "rejected"
    );
    if (_emailConflict) return { status: "error", message: "This email address is already registered to another account." };
  }

  let sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
  let data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  let headers = data[0];
  let userId  = _userId;
  let found   = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][0]) === userId) {
      // PERF: Build a full row array and write it in ONE setValues() call
      // instead of one sheet.getRange().setValue() per column.
      // This reduces Sheets API round-trips from ~10 calls to 1.
      const existingPwd = data[i][headers.indexOf("Password")];
      let newPwd = existingPwd;
      if (p.Password && sanitize(p.Password, 128).length > 0) {
        let pwd = sanitize(p.Password, 128);
        newPwd = pwd.length === 64 ? pwd : hashPassword(pwd);
      }
      // Clone existing row so columns not listed here are unchanged
      const newRow = data[i].slice();
      function _setCol(headerName, value) {
        const col = headers.indexOf(headerName);
        if (col !== -1 && value !== undefined) newRow[col] = value;
      }
      const _newStatus = sanitize(p.Status, 20) || "Active";
      const _oldStatus = String(data[i][headers.indexOf("Status")] || "Active");
      _setCol("Name",          sanitize(p.Name,    100));
      _setCol("Mobile",        sanitize(p.Mobile,  15));
      _setCol("Role",          sanitize(p.Role,    20));
      _setCol("Password",      newPwd);
      _setCol("Email",         sanitize(p.Email,   200));
      _setCol("Status",        _newStatus);
      _setCol("PhotoURL",      sanitize(p.PhotoURL, 500) || "");
      if (p.Village       !== undefined) _setCol("Village",       sanitize(p.Village, 100));
      if (p.Address       !== undefined) _setCol("Address",       sanitize(p.Address, 300));
      if (p.MonthlyTarget !== undefined) _setCol("MonthlyTarget", Number(p.MonthlyTarget||0));
      if (p.DOB           !== undefined) _setCol("DOB",           sanitize(p.DOB || "", 12));
      // [TRACKER] Contribution Start Date — optional, admin-set. Used by the Tracker
      // to know from which month a late-joining member's pending should start counting.
      if (p.ContribStartDate !== undefined) _setCol("ContribStartDate", sanitize(p.ContribStartDate || "", 12));
      // [TRACKER] InactiveSince — auto-managed, not directly editable from the form.
      // Active → Inactive: stamp today's date so Tracker freezes pending from here.
      // Inactive → Active: clear it, member is back to normal pending tracking.
      if (headers.indexOf("InactiveSince") !== -1) {
        if (_oldStatus.toLowerCase() !== "inactive" && _newStatus.toLowerCase() === "inactive") {
          _setCol("InactiveSince", Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy"));
        } else if (_oldStatus.toLowerCase() === "inactive" && _newStatus.toLowerCase() !== "inactive") {
          _setCol("InactiveSince", "");
        }
      }
      // Single batched write — 1 API call instead of ~10
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);
      // Force DOB cell to plain text — prevents Sheets auto-converting "03-02-1998" to a Date object
      const _dobCol = headers.indexOf("DOB");
      if (_dobCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, _dobCol + 1).setNumberFormat("@");
      // Same plain-text guard for the two new Tracker date columns
      const _csdCol = headers.indexOf("ContribStartDate");
      if (_csdCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, _csdCol + 1).setNumberFormat("@");
      const _isCol = headers.indexOf("InactiveSince");
      if (_isCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, _isCol + 1).setNumberFormat("@");
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      found = true; break;
    }
  }
  if (found) { logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"System","Update User","UserId: "+userId+" | Name: "+sanitize(p.Name||"",100)+" | Role: "+sanitize(p.Role||"",20)+" | Status: "+sanitize(p.Status||"",20),"Profile updated"); return {status:"updated"}; }
  return { status: "not found" };
}

function addRow(name, row) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  sheet.appendRow(row);
  bustSheetCache(name); // invalidate cached read — row was just added
  // Force PaymentDate column to plain text so Sheets never auto-parses "dd-MM-yyyy"
  // as a date. Without this, "11-04-2026" is read as MM-DD → November 4,
  // corrupting every sort and display downstream.
  if (name === "CONTRIBUTIONS" || name === "EXPENSES" || name === "EVENT_EXPENSES") {
    const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const pdCol = headers.indexOf("PaymentDate");
    if (pdCol >= 0) {
      const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
      sheet.getRange(lastRow, pdCol + 1).setNumberFormat("@"); // @ = plain text
    }
  }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ONE-TIME REPAIR: Fix corrupted PaymentDate cells in CONTRIBUTIONS
// Run this ONCE from Apps Script editor: repairPaymentDates()
// It converts any Date-object cells back to "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss" IST plain text.
// Safe to run multiple times — skips cells already in plain text format.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function repairPaymentDates() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheetNames = ["CONTRIBUTIONS", "EXPENSES", "EVENT_EXPENSES"];
  var totalFixed = 0;

  sheetNames.forEach(function(name) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) return;
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return;
    const headers = data[0];
    const pdCol = headers.indexOf("PaymentDate");
    if (pdCol < 0) return;

    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const cell = sheet.getRange(i + 1, pdCol + 1);
      const val  = data[i][pdCol];
      if (val instanceof Date) {
        // Convert Date object to IST plain text string
        const fixed = Utilities.formatDate(val, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss");
        cell.setNumberFormat("@");   // plain text first
        cell.setValue(fixed);         // then write string
        totalFixed++;
        Logger.log("Fixed row " + (i+1) + ": " + val + " -> " + fixed); // keep: maintenance tool, runs manually
      } else if (String(val).trim() !== "") {
        // Already a string — just ensure cell format is plain text to prevent future re-parsing
        cell.setNumberFormat("@");
      }
    }
  });

  Logger.log("repairPaymentDates complete. Fixed " + totalFixed + " cells.");
  logAction("System", "repairPaymentDates", "Fixed " + totalFixed + " Date cells in CONTRIBUTIONS/EXPENSES sheets", "", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
  return "Done. Fixed " + totalFixed + " Date cells. Check Logs for details.";
}

function deleteRow(name, id) {
  let sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  let data  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][0]) === String(id)) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i+1);
      bustSheetCache(name); // [FIX-4] Invalidate in-request cache after delete so any
                            // subsequent same-request read (e.g. audit log) sees fresh data.
      return {status:"deleted"};
    }
  }
  return { status: "not found" };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PERMANENT SORT ORDER HELPERS
//  _getNextSortOrder — returns max(SortOrder)+1 for a sheet
//                      so newly added items go to the bottom.
//  _updateSortOrder  — receives [{id, sort}] array, writes each
//                      SortOrder value back to col 3 of the sheet.
//                      Called by the ↑ ↓ buttons in admin panel.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _getNextSortOrder(sheetName) {
  var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!sheet) return 1;
  var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return 1;
  var headers = data[0];
  var sortCol = headers.indexOf("SortOrder");
  if (sortCol === -1) return data.length; // no column yet — use row count as fallback
  var max = 0;
  for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    var v = Number(data[i][sortCol] || 0);
    if (v > max) max = v;
  }
  return max + 1;
}

function _updateSortOrder(sheetName, orderArr, adminName) {
  // orderArr: [{id: "...", sort: 1}, {id: "...", sort: 2}, ...]
  // Writes the SortOrder value into column 3 (index 2) for each matching row.
  if (!sheetName || !Array.isArray(orderArr) || orderArr.length === 0) {
    return { status: "error", message: "Invalid parameters" };
  }
  var sheetMap = { types: SHEETS.TYPES, occasions: SHEETS.OCCASIONS, expenseTypes: SHEETS.EXPENSE_TYPES };
  var target = sheetMap[sheetName] || sheetName;
  var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(target);
  if (!sheet) return { status: "error", message: "Sheet not found: " + target };

  var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var headers = data[0];
  var idCol   = 0; // ID is always col 0 (TypeId / OccasionId / ExpenseTypeId)

  // Find or create SortOrder column
  var sortCol = headers.indexOf("SortOrder");
  if (sortCol === -1) {
    // Column missing — add header to row 1
    sortCol = headers.length;
    sheet.getRange(1, sortCol + 1).setValue("SortOrder");
  }

  // Build a lookup map id → sort value for O(1) access
  var sortMap = {};
  orderArr.forEach(function(item) { sortMap[String(item.id)] = Number(item.sort); });

  // Write each SortOrder value in one pass
  var updated = 0;
  for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    var rowId = String(data[i][idCol] || "");
    if (sortMap.hasOwnProperty(rowId)) {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, sortCol + 1).setValue(sortMap[rowId]);
      updated++;
    }
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  // Bust the relevant cache
  var cacheKeyMap = { TYPES: "c_types", OCCASIONS: "c_occasions", EXPENSE_TYPES: "c_exptypes" };
  if (cacheKeyMap[target]) _bustSheetCache(cacheKeyMap[target]);

  logAction(sanitize(adminName||"Admin",100), "Update Sort Order", sheetName + " — " + updated + " rows updated");
  return { status: "success", updated: updated };
}

function updateRow(name, body) {
  let sheet  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  let values = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = values[0];
  let rowIndex = values.map(r=>String(r[0])).indexOf(String(sanitize(body.Id,30)));
  if (rowIndex !== -1) {
    let row = rowIndex + 1;
    // Header-based updates — safe regardless of column order
    function _setColRow(h, val) {
      const c = headers.indexOf(h);
      if (c !== -1 && val !== undefined) sheet.getRange(row, c+1).setValue(val);
    }
    _setColRow("Amount",      sanitize(body.Amount,    20));
    _setColRow("ForMonth",    sanitize(body.ForMonth,  20));
    if (body.Year) _setColRow("Year", sanitize(body.Year, 10));
    _setColRow("TypeId",      sanitize(body.TypeId,    30));
    if (body.OccasionId !== undefined) _setColRow("OccasionId", sanitize(body.OccasionId, 30));
    if (body.Note       !== undefined) _setColRow("Note",       sanitize(body.Note,       500));
    if (body.PaymentMode)              _setColRow("PaymentMode",sanitize(body.PaymentMode, 30));
    return { status: "updated" };
  }
  return { status: "not found" };
}

function updateExpenseRow(name, body) {
  let sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(name);
  let data  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0]; // read headers once, not per row
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][0]) === String(sanitize(body.Id,30))) {
      // PERF: Clone the existing row and apply all updates to it,
      // then write the whole row back in ONE setValues() call.
      // Previously 5-6 separate getRange().setValue() calls were made.
      const newRow = data[i].slice();
      function _setExpCol(headerName, value) {
        const c = headers.indexOf(headerName);
        if (c !== -1 && value !== undefined) newRow[c] = value;
      }
      _setExpCol("Title",         sanitize(body.Title,         200));
      _setExpCol("Amount",        sanitize(body.Amount,         20));
      _setExpCol("Year",          sanitize(body.Year,           10));
      _setExpCol("ExpenseTypeId", sanitize(body.ExpenseTypeId,  30));
      _setExpCol("ForMonth",      sanitize(body.ForMonth,       20));
      if (body.ReceiptURL !== undefined)
        _setExpCol("ReceiptURL",  sanitize(body.ReceiptURL||"", 500));
      // FIX #5: Single batched write — 1 API call instead of 5-6
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);
      return { status: "updated" };
    }
  }
  return { status: "not found" };
}

// ── Announcement helpers (extracted for clarity)
function _getAnnouncement() {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT);
    if (!sheet) return {};
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return {};
    const headers = data[0];
    const active = data.slice(1).reverse().find(r => {
      const si = headers.indexOf("Status");
      return si===-1 || String(r[si]||"Active").toLowerCase()==="active";
    });
    if (!active) return {};
    return {
      Id:      active[headers.indexOf("AnnId")]    ||"",
      Message: active[headers.indexOf("Message")]  ||"",
      Badge:   active[headers.indexOf("Badge")]    ||"",
      Icon:    active[headers.indexOf("Icon")]     ||"🔔",
      Color:   active[headers.indexOf("Color")]    ||"purple",
      Status:  active[headers.indexOf("Status")]   ||"Active",
      CreatedAt:active[headers.indexOf("CreatedAt")]||""
    };
  } catch(e) { return {}; }
}

function _getAnnouncementHistory() {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT);
    if (!sheet) return [];
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return [];
    const headers = data[0];
    return data.slice(1).reverse().map(r => ({
      AnnId:    r[headers.indexOf("AnnId")]    ||"",
      Message:  r[headers.indexOf("Message")]  ||"",
      Badge:    r[headers.indexOf("Badge")]     ||"",
      Icon:     r[headers.indexOf("Icon")]      ||"🔔",
      Color:    r[headers.indexOf("Color")]     ||"purple",
      Status:   r[headers.indexOf("Status")]    ||"Active",
      AdminName:r[headers.indexOf("AdminName")] ||"Admin",
      CreatedAt:r[headers.indexOf("CreatedAt")] ||""
    }));
  } catch(e) { return []; }
}

function _getBroadcasts() {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.BROADCAST);
    if (!sheet) return [];
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return [];
    const headers = data[0];
    return data.slice(1).reverse().slice(0,20).map(r => {
      const rawTime = r[headers.indexOf("Time")];
      // Sheets auto-converts date-like strings into real Date cells, so this
      // can come back as a JS Date object (which would otherwise serialize
      // as a raw ISO string like "2026-07-21T21:34:07.000Z" to the client).
      // Format it into something readable either way.
      const time = (rawTime instanceof Date)
        ? Utilities.formatDate(rawTime, "GMT+5:30", "dd MMM yyyy, hh:mm a")
        : (rawTime || "");
      return {
        BcId:    r[headers.indexOf("BcId")]    ||"",
        Type:    r[headers.indexOf("Type")]    ||"",
        Priority:r[headers.indexOf("Priority")]||"normal",
        Title:   r[headers.indexOf("Title")]   ||"",
        Message: r[headers.indexOf("Message")] ||"",
        Time:    time,
        AdminName: r[headers.indexOf("AdminName")] ||""
      };
    });
  } catch(e) { return []; }
}

function _saveAnnouncement(e) {
  try {
    const msg = sanitize(e.parameter.Message, 500);
    if (!msg) return { status:"error", message:"Missing Message." };
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let annSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT);
    if (!annSheet) { annSheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT); annSheet.appendRow(["AnnId","Message","Badge","Icon","Color","Status","AdminName","CreatedAt"]); }
    const hdrRow = annSheet.getRange(1,1,1,annSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    if (hdrRow.indexOf("Color")===-1) annSheet.getRange(1, hdrRow.length+1).setValue("Color");
    const annData = annSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const annHdrs = annData[0];
    const stCol = annHdrs.indexOf("Status")+1;
    for (let i=1;i<annData.length;i++) {
      if (String(annData[i][annHdrs.indexOf("Status")]||"Active").toLowerCase()==="active") annSheet.getRange(i+1,stCol).setValue("Past");
    }
    const newId = generateSheetId("ANN");
    const freshHdrs = annSheet.getRange(1,1,1,annSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    annSheet.appendRow(freshHdrs.map(h=>{
      if(h==="AnnId")    return newId;
      if(h==="Message")  return msg;
      if(h==="Badge")    return sanitize(e.parameter.Badge||"",50);
      if(h==="Icon")     return sanitize(e.parameter.Icon||"🔔",10);
      if(h==="Color")    return sanitize(e.parameter.Color||"purple",20);
      if(h==="Status")   return "Active";
      if(h==="AdminName")return sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100);
      if(h==="CreatedAt")return formatDate();
      return "";
    }));
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin","saveAnnouncement","Id: "+newId);
    return { status:"success", annId:newId };
  } catch(err) { return { status:"error", message:err.message }; }
}

function _clearAnnouncement(e) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const annSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.ANNOUNCEMENT);
    if (annSheet) {
      const annData = annSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const annHdrs = annData[0];
      const stCol = annHdrs.indexOf("Status")+1;
      for (let i=1;i<annData.length;i++) {
        if (String(annData[i][annHdrs.indexOf("Status")]||"").toLowerCase()==="active") annSheet.getRange(i+1,stCol).setValue("Past");
      }
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    }
    logAction(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin","clearAnnouncement","Banner removed");
    return { status:"success" };
  } catch(err) { return { status:"error", message:err.message }; }
}

function _saveBroadcast(e) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let bcSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.BROADCAST);
    if (!bcSheet) { bcSheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.BROADCAST); bcSheet.appendRow(["BcId","Type","Priority","Title","Message","Time","AdminName"]); }
    const newBcId = generateSheetId("BCAST");
    bcSheet.appendRow([
      newBcId,
      sanitize(e.parameter.type     ||"announcement",30),
      sanitize(e.parameter.priority ||"normal",20),
      sanitize(e.parameter.title    ||"",200),
      sanitize(e.parameter.message  ||"",2000),
      sanitize(e.parameter.time     ||formatDate(),50),
      sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin",100)
    ]);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction(e.parameter.AdminName||"Admin","saveBroadcast","Id: "+newBcId);
    return { status:"success", bcId:newBcId };
  } catch(err) { return { status:"error", message:err.message }; }
}

// Deletes a single broadcast row by BcId — used by the admin "delete" button
// in Broadcast History. Once removed here, it also stops showing in the
// member dashboard/bell (both read from this same sheet via _getBroadcasts).
function _deleteBroadcast(e) {
  try {
    const bcId = sanitize(e.parameter.BcId, 50);
    if (!bcId) return { status:"error", message:"Missing BcId" };
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.BROADCAST);
    if (!sheet) return { status:"error", message:"BROADCAST sheet not found" };
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    const idCol = headers.indexOf("BcId");
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][idCol]) === bcId) {
        sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
        SpreadsheetApp.flush();
        logAction(sanitize(e.parameter.AdminName,100) || "Admin", "deleteBroadcast", "BcId: " + bcId);
        return { status:"success" };
      }
    }
    return { status:"error", message:"Broadcast not found" };
  } catch(err) { return { status:"error", message:err.message }; }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  BIRTHDAY WISH BELL — helpers
//  Fixed-reply "wish" notifications between active members.
//  Sheet: WISHES — WishId | FromUserId | FromName | ToUserId | ToName |
//                  Message | Timestamp | Year
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── Parse a DOB cell (Date object OR "dd-MM-yyyy"/"yyyy-MM-dd" string)
//    into {day, month} using IST — same rule sendBirthdayEmails() already
//    uses, kept separate here so neither function risks the other.
function _getDobDayMonth(dob) {
  try {
    if (dob instanceof Date) {
      var istStr = Utilities.formatDate(dob, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy");
      var p = istStr.split("-");
      return { day: Number(p[0]), month: Number(p[1]) };
    }
    var s = String(dob || "").trim();
    if (/^\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}$/.test(s)) {
      var p2 = s.split("-"); return { day: Number(p2[0]), month: Number(p2[1]) };
    }
    if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(s)) {
      var p3 = s.split("-"); return { day: Number(p3[2]), month: Number(p3[1]) };
    }
    return null;
  } catch (e) { return null; }
}

// ── Today's day/month/year, fixed to IST regardless of requester's timezone
function _todayIST() {
  var now = new Date();
  return {
    day:   Number(Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+5:30", "d")),
    month: Number(Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+5:30", "M")),
    year:  Number(Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy"))
  };
}

// ── getTodayBirthdays: for the requesting user, returns
//    { isMyBirthdayToday, others: [{UserId,Name,PhotoURL,alreadyWished}] }
//    "others" excludes the requester, inactive accounts, and anyone who has
//    opted out via ShowBirthday === false (column optional — defaults to shown).
function _getTodayBirthdays(requestUserId) {
  var users = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  var today = _todayIST();
  var isMine = false;
  var others = [];

  // Build "already wished this year" set for this requester
  var wished = {};
  try {
    var w = _readSheetRaw(SHEETS.WISHES);
    var fCol = w.headers.indexOf("FromUserId");
    var tCol = w.headers.indexOf("ToUserId");
    var yCol = w.headers.indexOf("Year");
    w.rows.forEach(function (r) {
      if (String(r[fCol]) === String(requestUserId) && String(r[yCol]) === String(today.year)) {
        wished[String(r[tCol])] = true;
      }
    });
  } catch (e) { /* WISHES sheet doesn't exist yet — nothing wished */ }

  users.forEach(function (u) {
    if (String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "active") return;
    if (u.ShowBirthday === false) return; // privacy opt-out (column optional)
    var dm = _getDobDayMonth(u.DOB);
    if (!dm || dm.day !== today.day || dm.month !== today.month) return;

    if (String(u.UserId) === String(requestUserId)) {
      isMine = true;
    } else {
      others.push({
        UserId: u.UserId,
        Name: u.Name,
        PhotoURL: u.PhotoURL || "",
        alreadyWished: !!wished[String(u.UserId)]
      });
    }
  });

  return { status: "success", isMyBirthdayToday: isMine, others: others };
}

// ── sendBirthdayWish: records one fixed-reply wish, one per sender per
//    recipient per year. Returns {status:"success"} / {status:"already_sent"}.
function _sendBirthdayWish(p) {
  var fromUserId = sanitize(p.userId, 30);
  var toUserId   = sanitize(p.ToUserId, 30);
  var message    = sanitize(p.Message, 200);

  if (!fromUserId || !toUserId || !message) {
    return { status: "error", message: "Missing required fields." };
  }
  if (fromUserId === toUserId) {
    return { status: "error", message: "You can't wish yourself." };
  }

  var today = _todayIST();
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.WISHES);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.WISHES);
    sheet.appendRow(["WishId", "FromUserId", "FromName", "ToUserId", "ToName", "Message", "Timestamp", "Year"]);
  }

  // Duplicate guard — one wish per sender per recipient per year
  var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var headers = data[0];
  var fCol = headers.indexOf("FromUserId");
  var tCol = headers.indexOf("ToUserId");
  var yCol = headers.indexOf("Year");
  for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][fCol]) === fromUserId && String(data[i][tCol]) === toUserId && String(data[i][yCol]) === String(today.year)) {
      return { status: "already_sent" };
    }
  }

  var fromRow = _findUserRow(fromUserId);
  var toRow   = _findUserRow(toUserId);
  var fromName = fromRow ? fromRow.allData[fromRow.rowIndex][fromRow.headers.indexOf("Name")] : "";
  var toName   = toRow   ? toRow.allData[toRow.rowIndex][toRow.headers.indexOf("Name")]     : "";

  var wishId = generateSheetId("WISH");
  sheet.appendRow([wishId, fromUserId, fromName, toUserId, toName, message, formatDate(), today.year]);
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  logAction(fromName || fromUserId, "SEND_BIRTHDAY_WISH", "To: " + (toName || toUserId) + " | Msg: " + message, "", "", { severity: "INFO", result: "SUCCESS" });

  return { status: "success", wishId: wishId };
}

// ── getMyBirthdayWishes: wishes received by this user this year, newest first
function _getMyBirthdayWishes(userId) {
  var today = _todayIST();
  var out = [];
  try {
    var w = _readSheetRaw(SHEETS.WISHES);
    var idCol = w.headers.indexOf("WishId");
    var tCol  = w.headers.indexOf("ToUserId");
    var yCol  = w.headers.indexOf("Year");
    var fnCol = w.headers.indexOf("FromName");
    var mCol  = w.headers.indexOf("Message");
    var tsCol = w.headers.indexOf("Timestamp");
    w.rows.forEach(function (r) {
      if (String(r[tCol]) === String(userId) && String(r[yCol]) === String(today.year)) {
        out.push({ WishId: r[idCol], FromName: r[fnCol], Message: r[mCol], Timestamp: r[tsCol] });
      }
    });
  } catch (e) { /* WISHES sheet doesn't exist yet */ }
  out.reverse();
  return { status: "success", wishes: out, count: out.length };
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  POST HANDLER (photo upload — unchanged)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function doPost(e) {
  let result = {};
  try {
    const data = JSON.parse(e.postData.contents);
