    // [FIX-TOKEN] Handle clearSessionToken BEFORE auth check — this action clears
    // the token itself so it must not require a valid token to run.
    // Called by admin.js logout() via postData (reliable JSON POST path).
    if (data.action === "clearSessionToken") {
      const userId = sanitize(data.userId || data.UserId || "", 30);
      if (userId) {
        try {
          const sheet    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
          const allData  = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
          const headers  = allData[0];
          const tokenCol  = headers.indexOf("SessionToken");
          const expiryCol = headers.indexOf("TokenExpiry");
          const nameCol   = headers.indexOf("Name");
          for (let i = 1; i < allData.length; i++) {
            const rowUserId = String(allData[i][0] || "").trim();
            const rowName   = nameCol !== -1 ? String(allData[i][nameCol] || "").trim() : "";
            if ((rowUserId && rowUserId === userId) || (rowName && rowName === userId)) {
              if (tokenCol  !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, tokenCol  + 1).setValue("");
              if (expiryCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i + 1, expiryCol + 1).setValue("");
              SpreadsheetApp.flush(); break;
            }
          }
        } catch(clrErr) { /* non-fatal */ }
        logAction(userId, "SESSION_TOKEN_CLEARED", "UserId: " + userId, sanitize(data.reason||"Logout",200), "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
      }
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ status: "ok" })).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }

    // FIX SEC-9: Verify session token on all doPost actions — photo uploads modify Drive and user data
    const _postUserId = sanitize(data.UserId || data.userId || "", 30);
    const _postToken  = sanitize(data.sessionToken || data.token || "", 64);
    if (!_postUserId || !_postToken) {
      logAction(_postUserId || "Unknown", "REJECTED_NO_TOKEN", "doPost action: " + (data.action||"unknown") + " — missing userId or sessionToken", "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"BLOCKED" });
      return ContentService
        .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ status: "error", message: "Authentication required." }))
        .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
    if (!_verifySession({ userId: _postUserId, sessionToken: _postToken }, data.action || "doPost")) {
      return ContentService
        .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ status: "error", message: "Session expired. Please login again." }))
        .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }

    if (data.action === "uploadAndSaveProfile") {
      if (!data.base64 || !data.fileName) return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({status:"error",message:"Missing data."})).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
      // Try to delete old photo — handle both lh3 and thumbnail URL formats
      if (data.oldPhotoURL) {
        try {
          let oldId = "";
          const oldUrl = String(data.oldPhotoURL);
          if (oldUrl.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/")) oldId = oldUrl.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
          else if (oldUrl.includes("drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=")) oldId = oldUrl.split("id=")[1].split("&")[0].trim();
          if (oldId && oldId.length > 10) {
            DriveApp.getFileById(oldId).setTrashed(true);
            logAction(data.AdminName||"User", "Old Profile Photo Deleted", "UserId: " + data.UserId + " | DriveFileId: " + oldId, "Replaced on profile update", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
          }
        } catch(ex){}
      }
      const photoUrl = uploadProfilePhoto(data.base64, sanitize(data.fileName,100));
      const userUpdateRes = updateUser({ UserId:data.UserId, Name:data.Name, Mobile:data.Mobile||"", Role:data.Role, Password:"", Email:data.Email||"", Status:data.Status||"Active", PhotoURL:photoUrl, AdminName:data.AdminName||"User", Village:data.Village||"", Address:data.Address||"" });
      logAction(data.AdminName||"User","Upload Photo","UserId: "+data.UserId);
      result = { status:"success", photoUrl:photoUrl };
    } else if (data.action === "uploadPaymentSlip") {
      if (!data.base64 || !data.fileName) return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({status:"error",message:"Missing data."})).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
      // Delete old slip from Drive if provided
      if (data.oldSlipURL) {
        try {
          const oldUrl = String(data.oldSlipURL);
          let oldId = "";
          if (oldUrl.includes("drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=")) oldId = oldUrl.split("id=")[1].split("&")[0].trim();
          else if (oldUrl.includes("lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/"))  oldId = oldUrl.split("/d/")[1].split("?")[0].trim();
          if (oldId && oldId.length > 10) {
            DriveApp.getFileById(oldId).setTrashed(true);
            logAction(sanitize(data.UserId,30)||"User", "Old Payment Slip Deleted", "UserId: " + data.UserId + " | DriveFileId: " + oldId, "Replaced on slip re-upload", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
          }
        } catch(ex) { /* non-fatal — continue with upload */ }
      }
      const slipUrl = uploadPaymentSlipPhoto(data.base64, sanitize(data.fileName,100));
      logAction(sanitize(data.UserId,30)||"User","Upload Payment Slip","UserId: "+data.UserId);
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({status:"success",slipUrl:slipUrl})).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    } else if (data.action === "uploadExpenseReceipt") {
      if (!data.base64 || !data.fileName || !data.expenseId) {
        return ContentService.createTextOutput(
          JSON.stringify({status:"error",message:"Missing fields."})
        ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
      }
      const receiptUrl = uploadExpenseReceiptPhoto(data.base64, sanitize(data.fileName, 100));
      // Parse existing URLs array (sent from client) and append new URL
      let existingUrls = [];
      try { existingUrls = JSON.parse(data.existingURLs || "[]"); } catch(ex) {}
      if (!Array.isArray(existingUrls)) existingUrls = [];
      existingUrls.push(receiptUrl);
      const newUrlsJson = JSON.stringify(existingUrls);
      // Save to EXPENSES sheet — update both ReceiptURLs (array) and ReceiptURL (legacy first item)
      const expSheet  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
      const expData   = expSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const expHdrs   = expData[0];
      // Ensure ReceiptURLs column exists (add if missing)
      let urlsCol = expHdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURLs");
      if (urlsCol === -1) {
        urlsCol = expHdrs.length;
        expSheet.getRange(1, urlsCol + 1).setValue("ReceiptURLs");
      }
      const rcptCol = expHdrs.indexOf("ReceiptURL");
      for (let i = 1; i < expData.length; i++) {
        if (String(expData[i][0]) === String(sanitize(data.expenseId, 30))) {
          expSheet.getRange(i + 1, urlsCol + 1).setValue(newUrlsJson);
          if (rcptCol !== -1) expSheet.getRange(i + 1, rcptCol + 1).setValue(existingUrls[0] || receiptUrl);
          SpreadsheetApp.flush();
          break;
        }
      }
      logAction(sanitize(data.AdminName,100)||"Admin", "uploadExpenseReceipt", "ExpenseId: " + data.expenseId);
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(
        JSON.stringify({status:"success", receiptUrl: existingUrls[0] || receiptUrl, receiptUrls: newUrlsJson})
      ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
 
    } else if (data.action === "uploadGalleryPhoto") {
      if (!data.base64 || !data.fileName) return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({status:"error",message:"Missing base64 or fileName."})).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
      const photoUrl = uploadGalleryPhotoFile(data.base64, sanitize(data.fileName,100));
      const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
      let galSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.GALLERY);
      if (!galSheet) {
        galSheet=ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.GALLERY);
        galSheet.appendRow(["ImageId","Title","PhotoURL","Priority","Status","CreatedAt","Tags"]);
      } else {
        // Ensure Tags column exists (upgrade existing sheet)
        const existHdrs = galSheet.getRange(1,1,1,galSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
        if (!existHdrs.includes("Tags")) {
          galSheet.getRange(1, existHdrs.length+1).setValue("Tags");
        }
      }
      const headers = galSheet.getRange(1,1,1,galSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      const newId = generateSheetId("GAL");
      galSheet.appendRow(headers.map(h=>{
        if(h==="ImageId")  return newId;
        if(h==="Title")    return sanitize(data.caption||data.Caption||"",200);
        if(h==="PhotoURL") return photoUrl;
        if(h==="Priority") return Number(data.priority||999);
        if(h==="Status")   return "Active";
        if(h==="CreatedAt")return formatDate();
        if(h==="Tags")     return sanitize(data.tags||data.Tags||"",300);
        return "";
      }));
      logAction(sanitize(data.AdminName,100)||"Admin","uploadGalleryPhoto","Id: "+newId);
      result = { status:"success", photoUrl:photoUrl, photoId:newId };
    } else { result = { status:"error", message:"Unknown action." }; }
  } catch(err) {
    logAction(sanitize((JSON.parse(e.postData.contents||"{}").AdminName||JSON.parse(e.postData.contents||"{}").userId||"Unknown"),100), "DOPOST_UNHANDLED_ERROR", "Action: " + (JSON.parse(e.postData.contents||"{}").action||"unknown"), err.message, "", { severity:"CRITICAL", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
    result = { status:"error", message:err.message };
  }
  return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(result)).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

// ── Core upload helper — uploads base64 to a specific Drive folder by ID
function _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, folderId) {
  // FIX BUG-2: Whitelist MIME types — reject non-image uploads to prevent
  // arbitrary file types (JS, HTML, PDF, etc.) being stored in Drive folders
  const contentType = base64Data.substring(5, base64Data.indexOf(';'));
  const ALLOWED_TYPES = ["image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/webp", "image/gif", "image/heic", "image/heif"];
  if (!ALLOWED_TYPES.includes(contentType.toLowerCase())) {
    throw new Error("Invalid file type. Only images (JPEG, PNG, WEBP, GIF) are allowed.");
  }
  const folder      = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const bytes       = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data.split(',')[1]);
  const blob        = Utilities.newBlob(bytes, contentType, fileName);
  const file        = folder.createFile(blob);
  file.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
  return "https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=" + file.getId() + "&sz=w400";
}

// ── Upload profile photo → ProfilePhotos folder
function uploadProfilePhoto(base64Data, fileName) {
  return _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, CFG.folderProfile);
}

// ── Upload expense receipt → ExpenseReceipts folder
function uploadExpenseReceiptPhoto(base64Data, fileName) {
  return _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, CFG.folderExpense);
}

// ── Upload payment slip → PaymentSlips folder (separate from expense receipts)
function uploadPaymentSlipPhoto(base64Data, fileName) {
  return _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, CFG.folderSlip);
}

// ── Upload gallery photo → GalleryPhotos folder
function uploadGalleryPhotoFile(base64Data, fileName) {
  return _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, CFG.folderGallery);
}

// ── Legacy wrapper — kept for any code that still calls uploadUserPhoto directly.
// Routes to folderMain (original folder) for backward compatibility.
// New doPost handlers below use the 3 specific functions.
function uploadUserPhoto(base64Data, fileName) {
  return _uploadToFolder(base64Data, fileName, CFG.folderMain);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  H14 — SYSTEM HEALTH CHECK
//  Returns green/red status for every critical system component.
//  Called by admin health check page.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  M1 — MONTHLY REMINDER TO UNPAID MEMBERS (run on 25th via trigger)
//  Also callable manually from admin via triggerMonthlyReminder action.
//  Only runs if monthly_reminder toggle is ON in email settings.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MONTHLY CONTRIBUTION REMINDER — SINGLE FUNCTION (merged)
//
//  WHO gets the email:
//    ✅ Active members only (Status = "Active")
//    ✅ Non-admin only (Role ≠ "admin")
//    ✅ Must have an email address on record
//    ✅ Must NOT have any contribution recorded for the current month + year
//    ❌ Already-paid members are SKIPPED — no reminder sent
//    ❌ Inactive / suspended members are SKIPPED
//    ❌ Walk-in entries (no UserId in USERS sheet) are SKIPPED
//
//  CALLED FROM:
//    1. Apps Script Time-based trigger (fires automatically, e.g. 25th of month)
//       → Apps Script passes its event object as first arg — safeMonth guard rejects it
//       → month/year auto-resolved from current date
//    2. Admin panel "Send Reminder" button (action = triggerMonthlyReminder)
//       → passes month + year + bypassToggle=true (ignores ON/OFF toggle)
//    3. Web API (action = sendMonthlyReminders)
//       → passes month + year from request params
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function sendMonthlyReminders(overrideMonth, overrideYear, bypassToggle) {
  try {
    const settings = getEmailSettings();
    // Toggle bypassed when bypassToggle=true (manual admin trigger from panel)
    if (!bypassToggle && !settings.monthly_report) {
      logAction("System", "monthlyReminder", "Skipped — monthly_report toggle is OFF");
      return { status: "ok", sent: 0, skipped: 0, message: "Monthly emails disabled in settings." };
    }

    // Guard: Apps Script Time-based trigger passes its event object {triggerUid, year, month...}
    // as overrideMonth. That object is truthy so without this guard it would be used as the month
    // value → "[object Object]" in email subject AND hasPaid always false → everyone gets email.
    // Only accept overrideMonth/overrideYear when they are actual strings or numbers.
    var safeMonth = (typeof overrideMonth === "string" && overrideMonth.trim()) ? overrideMonth.trim() : null;
    var safeYear  = (typeof overrideYear  === "string" && overrideYear.trim())  ? overrideYear.trim()
                  : (typeof overrideYear  === "number")                         ? String(overrideYear)
                  : null;

    const MONTHS = ["January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"];
    const now    = new Date();
    const month  = safeMonth || MONTHS[now.getMonth()];
    const year   = safeYear  || String(now.getFullYear());

    // Normalize ForMonth: Google Sheets can return a Date object when the cell is
    // date-formatted. String(Date) → "Mon May 01 2026..." which never equals "May"
    // → hasPaid always false → every member gets reminder even if they already paid.
    function _normalizeForMonth(val) {
      if (val instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(val, "GMT+5:30", "MMMM");
      return String(val || "").trim();
    }

    const users         = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
    const contributions = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);

    // Only members who are: active + non-admin + have email + have NOT paid this month
    const unpaid = users.filter(function(u) {
      if (String(u.Role   || "").toLowerCase() === "admin")        return false;
      if (String(u.Status || "Active").toLowerCase() !== "active") return false;
      if (!String(u.Email || "").trim())                           return false;
      const paid = contributions.some(function(c) {
        return String(c.UserId)             === String(u.UserId) &&
               _normalizeForMonth(c.ForMonth) === month &&
               String(c.Year)               === year;
      });
      return !paid; // only include members who have NOT paid
    });

    let sent = 0, skipped = 0;
    unpaid.forEach(function(member) {
      if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) { skipped++; return; }
      try {
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to:       String(member.Email).trim(),
          subject:  CFG.name + " — Contribution Reminder for " + month + " " + year,
          htmlBody: _buildMonthlyReminderEmail(member, month, year)
        });
        sent++;
        Utilities.sleep(200);
      } catch(mailErr) {
        logAction("System", "REMINDER_EMAIL_SEND_ERROR", "To: " + member.Email + " | Name: " + (member.Name||""), mailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
        skipped++;
      }
    });

    logAction("System", "MonthlyReminder", month + " " + year + " — sent:" + sent + ", skipped:" + skipped + ", unpaid:" + unpaid.length);
    return { status: "ok", sent: sent, skipped: skipped, unpaidCount: unpaid.length };
  } catch(err) {
    logAction("System", "MONTHLY_REMINDER_FAILED", "Month: " + (month||"") + " Year: " + (year||""), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
    return { status: "error", message: err.message };
  }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  M7 — GOAL COMPLETION NOTIFICATION
//  Call this inside updateGoal or addContribution when CurrentAmount
//  reaches or exceeds TargetAmount. Marks goal "Completed" and emails admin.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _checkGoalCompletion(goalId) {
  try {
    const goals   = getSheetData(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const goal    = goals.find(function(g) { return String(g.GoalId) === String(goalId); });
    if (!goal) return;

    const current = Number(goal.CurrentAmount || goal.Current || 0);
    const target  = Number(goal.TargetAmount  || goal.Target  || 0);
    const status  = String(goal.Status || "").toLowerCase();

    // Only fire if just reached/exceeded target and not already completed
    if (target > 0 && current >= target && status !== "completed") {
      // Mark goal as Completed in sheet
      const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.GOALS);
      const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const headers = data[0];
      const statusCol = headers.indexOf("Status");
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][headers.indexOf("GoalId")]) === String(goalId)) {
          if (statusCol !== -1) sheet.getRange(i+1, statusCol+1).setValue("Completed");
          SpreadsheetApp.flush();
          break;
        }
      }

      // Email all admins
      const admins = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS).filter(function(u) {
        return String(u.Role || "").toLowerCase() === "admin" &&
               String(u.Email || "").trim() !== "";
      });
      const goalName   = goal.GoalName || goal.Name || "Goal";
      const amountFmt  = CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(current).toLocaleString("en-IN");
      const targetFmt  = CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(target).toLocaleString("en-IN");
      admins.forEach(function(admin) {
        if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) return;
        try {
          MailApp.sendEmail({
            to:       String(admin.Email).trim(),
            subject:  "🎉 " + CFG.name + " — Goal Fully Funded: " + goalName,
            htmlBody: `<div style="max-width:520px;margin:0 auto;font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;
              background:#fff;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
              <div style="background:#0F766E;padding:26px 28px;text-align:center;">
                <div style="font-size:30px;margin-bottom:4px;">🎉</div>
                <div style="color:#fff;font-size:17px;font-weight:700;">Goal Fully Funded!</div>
              </div>
              <div style="padding:24px 28px;">
                <p style="color:#1e293b;font-size:14px;margin:0 0 8px;">Dear ${admin.Name},</p>
                <p style="font-size:13.5px;color:#475569;margin:0 0 14px;">The fundraising goal <strong>"${goalName}"</strong> has been fully funded.</p>
                <table style="width:100%;font-size:13px;border-collapse:collapse;margin:0 0 14px;">
                  <tr><td style="padding:8px 0;color:#64748b;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;">Target</td><td style="padding:8px 0;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:#1e293b;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;">${targetFmt}</td></tr>
                  <tr><td style="padding:8px 0;color:#64748b;">Collected</td><td style="padding:8px 0;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:#16a34a;">${amountFmt}</td></tr>
                </table>
                <p style="color:#475569;font-size:12.5px;margin:0;">The goal has been automatically marked as Completed in the system.</p>
              </div>
              <div style="background:#f6f9f8;padding:12px 28px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #e7ebe9;">
                <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">${CFG.name} | ${CFG.location}</div>
              </div>
            </div>`
          });
        } catch(mailErr) {}
      });

      logAction("System", "GoalCompleted", "GoalId: " + goalId + " | " + goalName + " | " + amountFmt);
    }
  } catch(err) { /* non-fatal — never crash main operation */ }
}

// ── Mid-month reminder email (used by sendMonthlyReminders — fires ~25th, still time to pay)
function _buildMonthlyReminderEmail(member, month, year) {
  var firstName = (member.Name || "Friend").split(" ")[0];
  const body = `
  ${_emHeadSimple("Gentle Reminder")}

  <tr><td style="padding:26px 32px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 14px;">Dear ${firstName} जी,</p>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13.5px;line-height:1.85;margin:0 0 16px;">
      Hope you and your family are doing well 🙏। यह एक friendly reminder है कि आपका contribution
      <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${month} ${year}</strong> के लिए अभी तक record नहीं हुआ है।
    </p>

    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-left:3px solid ${_EM.brand};padding:14px 18px;margin:0 0 18px;">
      <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:4px;">
        ${month} ${year} — Contribution Due
      </div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.7;">
        अभी महीना खत्म होने में समय है, तो कृपया जल्द ही अपना contribution complete कर दें। अगर already
        pay कर दिया है, तो household admin से coordinate करके इसे record करवा दें।
      </div>
    </div>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0 0 18px;">
      यह contribution हमारे घर के मासिक खर्चों को manage करने के लिए है, and every family member's timely
      share helps us run things smoothly — आपकी भागीदारी हमेशा गिनी जाती है। 🌸
    </p>

    <p style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;font-style:italic;text-align:center;">
      धन्यवाद — Thank you for being part of our home. 🙏
    </p>
  </td></tr>

  ${_emFooterSimple("This is a private reminder sent only to you.")}`;
  return _emShell(520, body);
}

// ── CHATBOT CONFIG ────────────────────────────────────────────
 
function getChatbotConfig() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("CHATBOT_CONFIG");
    if (!sheet) return _defaultChatbotConfig();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return _defaultChatbotConfig();
    const config = Object.assign({}, _defaultChatbotConfig());
    data.slice(1).forEach(r => {
      if (r[0]) {
        // FIX: Google Sheets stores empty numeric cells as the number 0, not "".
        // String(0) = "0" which is truthy — caused chatbot to show "Account: 0",
        // "IFSC: 0" etc. Treat value 0 (number) as empty string, same as null/undefined.
        const rawVal = r[1];
        const key    = String(r[0]).trim();
        // Numeric 0 in Sheets = empty cell for most fields (fixes "Account: 0" etc.)
        // EXCEPT "enabled": 0 intentionally means disabled — must survive as "0".
        const strVal = (rawVal === undefined || rawVal === null || (rawVal === 0 && key !== "enabled"))
                       ? "" : String(rawVal).trim();
        config[key] = strVal;
      }
    });
    return config;
  } catch(e) { return _defaultChatbotConfig(); }
}
 
function _defaultChatbotConfig() {
  return {
    enabled:         "1",
    welcome_en:      "${CFG.tagline}! How can I help you today?",
    welcome_hi:      "${CFG.tagline}! आज मैं आपकी कैसे मदद कर सकता हूँ?",
    timings_en:      "Temple is open daily:\nMorning: 5:00 AM – 12:00 PM\nEvening: 4:00 PM – 9:00 PM",
    timings_hi:      "मंदिर प्रतिदिन खुला रहता है:\nसुबह: 5:00 AM – 12:00 PM\nशाम: 4:00 PM – 9:00 PM",
    location_en:     "${CFG.name}, ${CFG.address}.",
    location_hi:     "श्री हनुमान मंदिर, पालिया, सुल्तानपुर, उत्तर प्रदेश।",
    donate_en:       "You can donate in person at the temple or via bank transfer / UPI. Please see Bank Details or UPI/QR option for more.",
    donate_hi:       "आप मंदिर में आकर या बैंक ट्रांसफर / UPI के माध्यम से दान कर सकते हैं।",
    bank_name:       "",
    bank_account:    "",
    bank_ifsc:       "",
    bank_branch:     "",
    upi_id:          "",
    contact_phone:   "",
    contact_email:   "",
    contact_whatsapp:"",
    custom_q1_en:    "",
    custom_q1_hi:    "",
    custom_a1_en:    "",
    custom_a1_hi:    "",
    custom_q2_en:    "",
    custom_q2_hi:    "",
    custom_a2_en:    "",
    custom_a2_hi:    ""
  };
}
 
function saveChatbotConfig(params) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("CHATBOT_CONFIG");
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet("CHATBOT_CONFIG");
      sheet.appendRow(["Key", "Value", "UpdatedAt"]);
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3).setFontWeight("bold")
           .setBackground("#334155").setFontColor("#ffffff");
      sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    }
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const allowedKeys = [
      "enabled","welcome_en","welcome_hi","timings_en","timings_hi",
      "location_en","location_hi","donate_en","donate_hi",
      "bank_name","bank_account","bank_ifsc","bank_branch",
      "upi_id","contact_phone","contact_email","contact_whatsapp",
      "custom_q1_en","custom_q1_hi","custom_a1_en","custom_a1_hi",
      "custom_q2_en","custom_q2_hi","custom_a2_en","custom_a2_hi"
    ];
    const ts = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy HH:mm:ss");
    const savedKeys = [];
    allowedKeys.forEach(key => {
      if (params[key] === undefined || params[key] === null) return;
      const val = sanitize(String(params[key]), 1000);
      let found = false;
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === key) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, 2).setValue(val);
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, 3).setValue(ts);
          found = true; break;
        }
      }
      if (!found) sheet.appendRow([key, val, ts]);
      savedKeys.push(key);
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction(sanitize(params.AdminName||"Admin",100), "Save Chatbot Config", "Updated: " + savedKeys.join(", "));
    return { status: "success" };
  } catch(e) { return { status: "error", message: e.message }; }
}
 
 
// ── USER REGISTRATION WITH ADMIN APPROVAL ────────────────────
 
function registerUser(params) {
  try {
    const ss     = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet  = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
    if (!sheet) return { status: "error", message: "System error. Please try again." };

    const name    = sanitize(params.Name    || "", 100);
    const mobile  = sanitize(params.Mobile  || "", 15);
    const email   = sanitize(params.Email   || "", 200);
    const pwd     = sanitize(params.Password || "", 200); // SHA-256 hashed on client
    const village = sanitize(params.Village || "", 100);
    const address = sanitize(params.Address || "", 300);

    if (!name || !mobile || !email || !pwd) {
      return { status: "error", message: "Name, Mobile, Email and Password are required." };
    }

    // [VAL] Server-side mobile + email validation
    const mobileErr = _validateMobile(mobile);
    if (mobileErr) return { status: "error", message: mobileErr };
    const emailErr = _validateEmail(email);
    if (emailErr) return { status: "error", message: emailErr };

    // ── ATOMIC OTP VERIFICATION (new flow: OTP sent before form, verified here)
    //  If otpKey + otp are provided, verify and consume them now — one round trip.
    //  If not provided (legacy path or direct API), skip OTP check.
    const otpKey  = sanitize(params.otpKey || "", 80);
    const userOtp = sanitize(params.otp    || "", 10);
    if (otpKey && userOtp) {
      const cache    = CacheService.getScriptCache();
      const savedOtp = cache.get(otpKey);
      if (!savedOtp) {
        return { status: "error", message: "OTP expired or not found. Please request a new verification code.", errorCode: "otp_expired" };
      }
      if (savedOtp !== userOtp) {
        return { status: "error", message: "Incorrect verification code. Please try again.", errorCode: "otp_invalid" };
      }
      // Consume immediately — single use
      cache.remove(otpKey);
    }
 
    const existingUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
 
    // Check duplicate mobile
    const dupMobile = existingUsers.find(u => String(u.Mobile || "") === mobile);
    if (dupMobile) {
      const ds = String(dupMobile.Status || "").toLowerCase();
      if (ds === "pending")  return { status: "error", message: "A registration with this mobile is already pending approval." };
      if (ds === "active")   return { status: "error", message: "This mobile number is already registered. Please login directly." };
      if (ds === "rejected") return { status: "error", message: "This registration was previously rejected. Please contact the temple admin." };
      return { status: "error", message: "Mobile number already in use." };
    }
 
    // Check duplicate email (exclude rejected AND inactive — inactive users should be able to re-register)
    const dupEmail = existingUsers.find(u =>
      String(u.Email || "").toLowerCase() === email.toLowerCase() &&
      String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "rejected" &&
      String(u.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "inactive"
    );
    if (dupEmail) return { status: "error", message: "This email address is already registered." };
 
    // Ensure required columns exist — add gracefully if missing
    let headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const requiredCols = ["Village", "Address", "RegisteredAt", "DOB"];
    requiredCols.forEach(col => {
      if (headers.indexOf(col) === -1) {
        sheet.getRange(1, sheet.getLastColumn() + 1).setValue(col);
      }
    });
    // Refresh headers after possible additions
    headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
 
    // [ID] Always "User" role on self-registration → USER-NNNNN
    const newId = _genUserId("User");
    const dob = sanitize(params.DOB || "", 12);

    // ── Optional profile photo — 80x80 JPEG base64 sent directly in JSONP call.
    // Resized client-side before sending so base64 (~3-5KB) fits in GET URL.
    // fetch POST is blocked by CORS on Apps Script — JSONP is the only option.
    // Non-fatal: registration continues without photo if upload fails.
    let regPhotoURL = "";
    const photoB64  = params.PhotoB64 || "";
    const photoName = sanitize(params.FileName || "", 120);
    if (photoB64 && photoName) {
      try {
        regPhotoURL = _uploadToFolder(photoB64, photoName, CFG.folderProfile);
        logAction("System", "REG_PHOTO_UPLOADED", "Mobile: " + mobile + " | File: " + photoName, "", "", { severity:"INFO", result:"SUCCESS" });
      } catch(photoErr) {
        logAction("System", "REG_PHOTO_ERROR", "Mobile: " + mobile, photoErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
      }
    }

    const row = headers.map(h => {
      if (h === "UserId")       return newId;
      if (h === "Name")         return name;
      if (h === "Mobile")       return mobile;
      if (h === "Role")         return "User";
      if (h === "Password")     return pwd;
      if (h === "Email")        return email;
      if (h === "Status")       return "Pending";
      if (h === "SessionToken") return "";
      if (h === "Village")      return village;
      if (h === "Address")      return address;
      if (h === "RegisteredAt") return formatDate();
      if (h === "DOB")          return dob;
      if (h === "PhotoURL")     return regPhotoURL;
      return "";
    });
    sheet.appendRow(row);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction("System", "New Registration (Pending)", "Name: " + name + " | Mobile: " + mobile);
 
    // Send confirmation email to the registrant (best-effort)
    try {
      if (email && tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to: email,
          subject: CFG.name + " — Registration Received",
          htmlBody: `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"/></head>
<body style="margin:0;padding:0;background:${_EM.bg};font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;">
<table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:${_EM.bg};padding:36px 0;">
<tr><td align="center">
<table width="540" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="max-width:540px;width:92%;background:${_EM.card};border-radius:${_EM.radius};overflow:hidden;box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(15,23,42,0.06),0 8px 24px rgba(15,23,42,0.06);">
  ${_emHeader("REGISTRATION RECEIVED")}
  <tr><td style="padding:24px 28px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14.5px;font-weight:700;margin:0 0 8px;">${CFG.tagline}, ${name}!</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.7;margin:0 0 16px;">Thank you for registering with <strong>${CFG.name}</strong>. Your request has been received and is pending review by the household admin.</p>
    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-radius:10px;padding:16px 20px;margin:0 0 16px;">
      <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:12.5px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;">Your Registration Details</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:5px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Name:</strong> ${name}</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:5px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Mobile (Login ID):</strong> ${mobile}</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Email:</strong> ${email}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;">You will receive another email once the admin approves your account. Your <strong>mobile number</strong> will be your Login ID.</p>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter()}
</table></td></tr></table></body></html>`
        });
      }
    } catch(regMailErr) {
      logAction("System", "REGISTRATION_EMAIL_ERROR", "Mobile: " + mobile + " | Name: " + name, regMailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:regMailErr });
    }
 
    // Notify all admin users (best-effort, non-blocking)
    try {
      const admins = existingUsers.filter(u =>
        String(u.Role || "").toLowerCase() === "admin" &&
        String(u.Email || "").trim() !== "" &&
        String(u.Status || "Active").toLowerCase() === "active"
      );
      admins.forEach(admin => {
        try {
          MailApp.sendEmail({
            to: String(admin.Email).trim(),
            subject: CFG.name + " — New Registration Request from " + name,
            htmlBody: `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"/></head>
<body style="margin:0;padding:0;background:${_EM.bg};font-family:-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Arial,sans-serif;">
<table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:${_EM.bg};padding:36px 0;">
<tr><td align="center">
<table width="540" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="max-width:540px;width:92%;background:${_EM.card};border-radius:${_EM.radius};overflow:hidden;box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(15,23,42,0.06),0 8px 24px rgba(15,23,42,0.06);">
  ${_emHeader("NEW REGISTRATION REQUEST")}
  <tr><td style="padding:24px 28px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 6px;">Hello <strong>${admin.Name}</strong>,</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin:0 0 12px;">A new user has submitted a registration request:</p>
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
      ${_emailRow("Name", name)}
      ${_emailRow("Mobile", mobile)}
      ${_emailRow("Email", email)}
      ${_emailRow("Village", village || "—")}
    </table>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12px;margin:16px 0 0;">Please login to the admin panel → Users tab → Pending to approve or reject.</p>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter()}
</table></td></tr></table></body></html>`
          });
        } catch(mailErr) {
          logAction("System", "ADMIN_NOTIFY_EMAIL_ERROR", "Admin: " + (admin.Name||admin.Email||"") + " | NewUser: " + name, mailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
        }
      });
    } catch(e2) {
      logAction("System", "ADMIN_NOTIFY_LOOP_ERROR", "NewUser: " + name + " | Mobile: " + mobile, e2.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:e2 });
    }
 
    return { status: "success" };
  } catch(e) {
    logAction("System", "REGISTER_USER_ERROR", "Mobile: " + sanitize(params.Mobile||"",15) + " | Name: " + sanitize(params.Name||"",100), e.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}
 
function approveUser(params) {
  try {
    const userId    = sanitize(params.UserId    || "", 30);
    const adminName = sanitize(params.AdminName || "Admin", 100);
    if (!userId) return { status: "error", message: "UserId required." };
 
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
    if (!sheet) return { status: "error", message: "Users sheet not found." };
 
    const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    const statusIdx = headers.indexOf("Status");
    if (statusIdx === -1) return { status: "error", message: "Status column not found." };
 
    let userRow = -1;
    let userObj = {};
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][headers.indexOf("UserId")] || "") === userId) {
        userRow = i + 1;
        headers.forEach((h, j) => { userObj[h] = data[i][j]; });
        break;
      }
    }
    if (userRow === -1) return { status: "error", message: "User not found." };
    if (String(userObj.Status || "").toLowerCase() !== "pending") {
      return { status: "error", message: "User is not in Pending status." };
    }
 
    sheet.getRange(userRow, statusIdx + 1).setValue("Active");
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction(adminName, "Approve User", "UserId: " + userId + " | Name: " + userObj.Name + " | Mobile: " + userObj.Mobile);
 
    // Send approval email
    const toEmail = String(userObj.Email || "").trim();
    if (toEmail && tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
      try {
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to: toEmail,
          subject: CFG.name + " — Your Registration Has Been Approved!",
          htmlBody: _buildApprovalEmail(userObj)
        });
      } catch(mailErr) {
        logAction(adminName, "APPROVAL_EMAIL_ERROR", "UserId: " + userId + " | To: " + toEmail, mailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
      }
    }
 
    return { status: "success", emailSent: !!(toEmail) };
  } catch(e) {
    logAction("System", "APPROVE_USER_ERROR", "UserId: " + sanitize(params.UserId||"",30), e.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}
 
function rejectUser(params) {
  try {
    const userId    = sanitize(params.UserId    || "", 30);
    const reason    = sanitize(params.Reason    || "", 500);
    const adminName = sanitize(params.AdminName || "Admin", 100);
    if (!userId) return { status: "error", message: "UserId required." };
 
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
    if (!sheet) return { status: "error", message: "Users sheet not found." };
 
    const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
 
    let userRow = -1;
    let userObj = {};
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][headers.indexOf("UserId")] || "") === userId) {
        userRow = i + 1;
        headers.forEach((h, j) => { userObj[h] = data[i][j]; });
        break;
      }
    }
    if (userRow === -1) return { status: "error", message: "User not found." };

    // Send rejection email BEFORE deleting row (need user data)
    const toEmail = String(userObj.Email || "").trim();
    if (toEmail && tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
      try {
        MailApp.sendEmail({
          to: toEmail,
          subject: CFG.name + " — Regarding Your Registration Request",
          htmlBody: _buildRejectionEmail(userObj, reason)
        });
      } catch(mailErr) {
        logAction(adminName, "REJECTION_EMAIL_ERROR", "UserId: " + userId + " | To: " + toEmail, mailErr.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:mailErr });
      }
    }

    // DELETE the row from sheet
    sheet.deleteRow(userRow);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    logAction(adminName, "Reject & Delete User", "UserId: " + userId + " | Name: " + userObj.Name + (reason ? " | Reason: " + reason : ""));
 
    return { status: "success" };
  } catch(e) {
    logAction("System", "REJECT_USER_ERROR", "UserId: " + sanitize(params.UserId||"",30), e.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:e });
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}
 
// ── Shared onboarding content block — inserted into both the approval email
//    and the admin-added email, so every new user (whichever flow created
//    them) sees the same explanation of what the app offers and why.
//    Keep this as the single place to edit the wording — do not duplicate
//    the bullet lists inline in each email builder.
function _emWelcomeInfoBlock() {
  return `
    <div style="font-weight:700;color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">Yeh app hai kya</div>
    <ul style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.9;margin:0 0 20px;padding-left:18px;">
      <li>Ghar ke saare contributions ka digital record hai</li>
      <li>Kisne kitna diya, kab diya — sab track hota hai</li>
      <li>Kisi se poochna nahi padega, khud check kar sakta hai kabhi bhi</li>
    </ul>

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">Yaha kya kar sakta hai</div>
    <ul style="color:#334155;font-size:12.5px;line-height:2;margin:0 0 20px;padding-left:18px;">
      <li>Apna contribution history dekh sakta hai, kahi bhi aur kabhi bhi</li>
      <li>Naya payment submit kar sakta hai, nhi toh group me receipt send kar sakta hai</li>
      <li>Current year ka receipt download kar sakta hai</li>
      <li>Complete receipt (ab tak ka pura statement) download kar sakta hai</li>
      <li>Goals ka live progress track kar sakta hai</li>
      <li>Events aur announcements dekh sakta hai</li>
    </ul>

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">Reminder ka system (every month)</div>
    <div style="border-left:3px solid ${_EM.brand};background:${_EM.panel};padding:4px 16px;margin:0 0 20px;">
      <ul style="color:#334155;font-size:12.5px;line-height:2;margin:10px 0;padding-left:16px;">
        <li><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">25 tareek</strong> — reminder mail, agar contribution abhi tak submit nahi huwa ho</li>
        <li><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">30 tareek</strong> — contribution ho chuka ho toh complete summary mail</li>
        <li><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">30 tareek</strong> — nahi huwa ho toh last/final reminder mail</li>
      </ul>
    </div>

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:${_EM.ink};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">Safety</div>
    <ul style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.9;margin:0 0 4px;padding-left:18px;">
      <li>Har mail hamesha isi official Gmail ID se aayega — kisi aur address se aaye toh verify/ignore kare</li>
      <li>Password sirf usko hi pata hai — admin sahit koi bhi ise dekh nahi sakta, encrypted form me store hota hai</li>
    </ul>`;
}

function _buildApprovalEmail(user) {
  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("✓ REGISTRATION APPROVED", "#22c55e")}
  <tr><td style="padding:26px 32px 8px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 14px;">Namaste <strong style="color:${_EM.brand};">${user.Name}</strong> ji,</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0 0 18px;">Aapki registration request approve ho gaya hai. Ab aap login kar sakta hai.</p>
    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-radius:10px;padding:16px 20px;margin:0 0 20px;">
      <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:12.5px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;">Login Details</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:6px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Login ID (Mobile):</strong> ${user.Mobile}</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Password:</strong> Aapne registration ke time jo set kiya tha</div>
    </div>
    ${_emWelcomeInfoBlock()}
  </td></tr>
  ${_emButton("Open App", CFG.websiteUrl)}
  ${_emFooter("Koi sawaal ho toh app ke Feedback / Contact section se seedha message kar sakta hai.")}`;
  return _emShell(560, body);
}
 
// Welcome email sent when an admin manually adds a user (account Active from day one).
// Same design language as _buildApprovalEmail — green badge, login details box.
function _buildAdminAddedEmail(user) {
  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("✓ ACCOUNT CREATED", "#22c55e")}
  <tr><td style="padding:26px 32px 8px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 14px;">Namaste <strong style="color:${_EM.brand};">${user.Name}</strong> ji,</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0 0 18px;">Aapka account admin ne bana diya hai — abhi se active hai, neeche diye gaye details se login kar sakta hai.</p>
    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-radius:10px;padding:16px 20px;margin:0 0 20px;">
      <div style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:12.5px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;">Login Details</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:6px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Login ID (Mobile):</strong> ${user.Mobile}</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;margin-bottom:6px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Member ID:</strong> ${user.UserId}</div>
      <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;"><strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Password:</strong> <span style="background:#eef2f2;border:1px solid #d6e2e0;border-radius:6px;padding:2px 10px;font-family:monospace;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.5px;color:${_EM.brand};">JaiShreeRam</span></div>
      <div style="background:#fffbeb;border-radius:8px;padding:10px 14px;margin-top:12px;">
        <div style="color:#854d0e;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px;">⚠ First login par yeh zaroor kare</div>
        <div style="color:#78500e;font-size:12px;line-height:1.7;">Yeh ek temporary password hai. Pehli baar login karne ke baad turant naya password set karna hoga — us naye password ko kisi ke saath share na kare.</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    ${_emWelcomeInfoBlock()}
  </td></tr>
  ${_emButton("Open App", CFG.websiteUrl)}
  ${_emFooter("Koi sawaal ho toh app ke Feedback / Contact section se seedha message kar sakta hai.")}`;
  return _emShell(560, body);
}

function _buildRejectionEmail(user, reason) {
  const reasonBlock = reason
    ? `<div style="background:#fef2f2;border-left:3px solid #ef4444;border-radius:10px;padding:14px 18px;margin:16px 0;">
         <div style="color:#991b1b;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:6px;">Reason:</div>
         <div style="color:#7f1d1d;font-size:13px;line-height:1.6;">${reason}</div>
       </div>`
    : `<div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-radius:10px;padding:14px 18px;margin:16px 0;">
         <div style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;">If you have questions, please contact the household admin directly.</div>
       </div>`;
  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("REGISTRATION UPDATE", "rgba(255,255,255,0.18)", "#B45309")}
  <tr><td style="padding:26px 32px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 12px;">Dear <strong>${user.Name}</strong>,</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0 0 4px;">
      Thank you for your interest in registering with <strong>${CFG.name}</strong>.
      After review, we are unable to approve your registration request at this time.
    </p>
    ${reasonBlock}
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;">
      For assistance, please contact us at:<br/>
      <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">Phone:</strong> ${CFG.address}
    </p>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter()}`;
  return _emShell(560, body);
}


// ── Contribution request rejection notification email
function _buildContribRejectionEmail(user, amount, forMonth, year, reason) {
  const name      = user ? (user.Name || "Member") : "Member";
  const amtFmt    = CFG.currencyText + " " + Number(amount).toLocaleString("en-IN");
  const reasonHtml = reason
    ? `<div style="background:#fef2f2;border-left:3px solid #ef4444;border-radius:10px;padding:14px 16px;margin:14px 0;">
         <div style="color:#991b1b;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:6px;">Reason from Admin:</div>
         <div style="color:#7f1d1d;font-size:13px;line-height:1.6;">${reason}</div>
       </div>`
    : `<div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-radius:10px;padding:12px 16px;margin:14px 0;color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;">
         No specific reason provided. Please contact the household admin for details.
       </div>`;
  const body = `
  ${_emHeader("PAYMENT REQUEST UPDATE", "rgba(255,255,255,0.18)", "#B45309")}
  <tr><td style="padding:24px 32px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 10px;">Dear <strong>${name}</strong>,</p>
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.7;margin:0 0 4px;">
      Your payment request of <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${amtFmt}</strong> for <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${forMonth} ${year}</strong>
      has been reviewed and could not be approved at this time.
    </p>
    ${reasonHtml}
    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;">
      If you have questions or would like to resubmit with correct details, please contact the household admin.
    </p>
  </td></tr>
  ${_emFooter()}`;
  return _emShell(560, body);
}

// ── Public stats — safe aggregated data only, no personal info
function getPublicStats() {
  try {
    const contributions = getSheetData(SHEETS.CONTRIBUTIONS);
    const expenses      = getSheetData(SHEETS.EXPENSES);
    const users         = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
    const goals         = getSheetData(SHEETS.GOALS);
    const yearConfigRaw = getSheetData("YEAR_CONFIG");
 
    const curYear = new Date().getFullYear();
 
    // ── This year totals
    const thisYearCollection = contributions
      .filter(c => parseInt(c.Year,10) === curYear)
      .reduce((s,c) => s + Number(c.Amount||0), 0);
 
    const thisYearExpense = expenses
      .filter(e => parseInt(e.Year,10) === curYear)
      .reduce((s,e) => s + Number(e.Amount||0), 0);
 
    // ── Active member count (no Admin, no Inactive)
    const memberCount = users.filter(u =>
      String(u.Role||"").toLowerCase() !== "admin" &&
      String(u.Status||"Active").toLowerCase() === "active"
    ).length;
 
    // ── Year summary rows (reuse getYearlySummary logic)
    const summary = getYearlySummary();
    const yearRows = summary.rows || [];
 
    // ── Current balance = last year's closing balance
    const balance = yearRows.length > 0
      ? yearRows[yearRows.length - 1].closingBalance
      : 0;
 
    // ── Goals — return only Name, Target, Current, Status (no IDs)
    const safeGoals = goals.map(g => ({
      Name:    g.Name    || g.GoalName || "",
      Target:  Number(g.Target  || g.TargetAmount  || 0),
      Current: Number(g.Current || g.CurrentAmount || 0),
      Status:  g.Status || "Enabled"
    }));
 
    const updatedAt = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd-MMM-yyyy hh:mm a");
 
    return {
      status:             "ok",
      thisYearCollection: thisYearCollection,
      thisYearExpense:    thisYearExpense,
      balance:            balance,
      memberCount:        memberCount,
      yearRows:           yearRows,
      goals:              safeGoals,
      updatedAt:          updatedAt
    };
 
  } catch(err) {
    return { status: "error", message: err.message };
  }
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PHOTO PROXY — fetch Drive file server-side, return as base64
//  Called by client via action=getPhotoBase64&fileId=...
//  Solves CORS block: browser cannot read Drive thumbnails into canvas,
//  but Apps Script can fetch the file directly using DriveApp.
//  Result is cached in client (_photoB64Cache) so 1 call per session.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getPhotoBase64(fileId) {
  if (!fileId || fileId.length < 10) {
    return { status: "error", message: "Invalid fileId." };
  }
  try {
    const file  = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
    const blob  = file.getBlob();
    const b64   = Utilities.base64Encode(blob.getBytes());
    const mime  = blob.getContentType() || "image/jpeg";
    return { status: "success", base64: "data:" + mime + ";base64," + b64 };
  } catch (e) {
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}

function _changePassword(p) {  // FIX #3: Moved to global scope (was accidentally indented)
    try {
      const userId     = sanitize(p.UserId,      30);
      const oldHashRaw = sanitize(p.OldPassword, 128);
      const newHashRaw = sanitize(p.NewPassword, 128);
 
      if (!userId || !oldHashRaw || !newHashRaw) {
        return { status: "error", message: "Missing required fields." };
      }
      // Both must be 64-char SHA-256 hashes (client always sends hashed values)
      if (oldHashRaw.length !== 64 || newHashRaw.length !== 64) {
        return { status: "error", message: "Invalid password format." };
      }
      // Cannot set same password
      if (oldHashRaw === newHashRaw) {
        return { status: "error", message: "New password must be different." };
      }
 
      const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
      const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const headers = data[0];
      const pwdCol  = headers.indexOf("Password");
      const idCol   = 0; // UserId is always first column
 
      if (pwdCol === -1) return { status: "error", message: "Password column not found." };
 
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][idCol]) === userId) {
          const storedHash = String(data[i][pwdCol] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
          // Verify old password matches stored hash
          if (storedHash !== oldHashRaw.toLowerCase()) {
            logAction(userId, "CHANGE_PASSWORD_WRONG_CURRENT", "UserId: " + userId, "Supplied current password did not match", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE" });
            return { status: "error", message: "Current password is incorrect." };
          }
          // Write new password hash
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, pwdCol + 1).setValue(newHashRaw.toLowerCase());
          SpreadsheetApp.flush();
          logAction(userId, "Change Password", "UserId: " + userId, "User changed their own password");
          return { status: "success" };
        }
      }
      return { status: "error", message: "User not found." };
    } catch(err) {
      logAction("System", "CHANGE_PASSWORD_ERROR", "UserId: " + sanitize((p||{}).UserId||"",30), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      return { status: "error", message: err.message };
    }
  }
function _addEvent(p) {  // FIX #3: Moved to global scope (was accidentally indented)
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EVENTS);
      if (!sheet) return { status:"error", message:"EVENTS sheet not found." };
      const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      const row = headers.map(function(h) {
        if (h === "EventId")     return sanitize(p.EventId, 50) || generateSheetId("EVT");
        if (h === "EventName")   return sanitize(p.EventName, 200);
        if (h === "Category")    return sanitize(p.Category, 50);
        if (h === "StartDate")   return sanitize(p.StartDate, 20);
        if (h === "EndDate")     return sanitize(p.EndDate, 20);
        if (h === "Budget")      return Number(p.Budget || 0);
        if (h === "Status")      return sanitize(p.Status, 30) || "Upcoming";
        if (h === "Description") return sanitize(p.Description, 500);
        if (h === "CreatedAt")   return formatDate();
        if (h === "AdminName")   return sanitize(p.AdminName, 100);
        return "";
      });
      sheet.appendRow(row);
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"Admin", "addEvent", sanitize(p.EventName,100));
      return { status:"success" };
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"System", "ADD_EVENT_ERROR", "EventName: " + sanitize(p.EventName||"",100), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      return { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }
 
function _updateEvent(p) {
    try {
      const sheet   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EVENTS);
      const data    = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const headers = data[0];
      const eventId = sanitize(p.EventId, 50);
      // FIX #2: Declare rowIndex with let before the loop so the helper
      // function closes over the correct value. Previously var rowIndex
      // was declared inside the loop body, causing hoisting issues where
      // the helper would read undefined on the first access.
      let rowIndex = -1;
      // Helper: write a value to the column matching the given header name
      function setECol(h, v) {
        const c = headers.indexOf(h);
        if (c !== -1 && rowIndex !== -1) sheet.getRange(rowIndex+1, c+1).setValue(v);
      }
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][headers.indexOf("EventId")]) === eventId) {
          rowIndex = i;
          setECol("EventName",   sanitize(p.EventName,200));
          setECol("Category",    sanitize(p.Category,50));
          setECol("Status",      sanitize(p.Status,30));
          setECol("StartDate",   sanitize(p.StartDate,20));
          setECol("EndDate",     sanitize(p.EndDate,20));
          setECol("Budget",      Number(p.Budget||0));
          setECol("Description", sanitize(p.Description,500));
          SpreadsheetApp.flush();
          logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"Admin","updateEvent",eventId);
          return { status:"updated" };
        }
      }
      return { status:"not found" };
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"System", "UPDATE_EVENT_ERROR", "EventId: " + sanitize(p.EventId||"",50), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      return { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }
 
function _deleteEvent(p) {  // FIX #3: Moved to global scope (was accidentally indented)
    try {
      const eventId  = sanitize(p.EventId, 50);
      const adminName = sanitize(p.AdminName,100) || "Admin";
      // Delete event row
      const evSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EVENTS);
      const evData  = evSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const evHdrs  = evData[0];
      for (let i = evData.length-1; i >= 1; i--) {
        if (String(evData[i][evHdrs.indexOf("EventId")]) === eventId) {
          evSheet.deleteRow(i+1); break;
        }
      }
      // Delete all linked event expenses
      const exSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EVENT_EXPENSES);
      let _deletedExpCount = 0;
      if (exSheet) {
        const exData = exSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const exHdrs = exData[0];
        const eidCol = exHdrs.indexOf("EventId");
        for (let i = exData.length-1; i >= 1; i--) {
          if (String(exData[i][eidCol]) === eventId) { exSheet.deleteRow(i+1); _deletedExpCount++; }
        }
      }
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      logAction(adminName, "deleteEvent", "EventId: " + eventId + " | LinkedExpensesDeleted: " + _deletedExpCount, "", "", { severity:"WARN", result:"SUCCESS" });
      return { status:"deleted" };
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"System", "DELETE_EVENT_ERROR", "EventId: " + sanitize(p.EventId||"",50), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      return { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }
 
function _addEventExpense(p) {  // FIX #3: Moved to global scope (was accidentally indented)
    try {
      const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEETS.EVENT_EXPENSES);
      if (!sheet) return { status:"error", message:"EVENT_EXPENSES sheet not found." };
      const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      const row = headers.map(function(h) {
        if (h === "Id")           return sanitize(p.Id, 50) || generateSheetId("EEXP");
        if (h === "EventId")      return sanitize(p.EventId, 50);
        if (h === "Title")        return sanitize(p.Title, 200);
        if (h === "Amount")       return Number(p.Amount || 0);
        if (h === "PaymentDate")  return formatDate();
        if (h === "ExpenseTypeId")return sanitize(p.ExpenseTypeId, 30);
        if (h === "ForMonth")     return sanitize(p.ForMonth, 20);
        if (h === "Note")         return sanitize(p.Note, 300);
        if (h === "AdminName")    return sanitize(p.AdminName, 100);
        return "";
      });
      sheet.appendRow(row);
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"Admin","addEventExpense",
        "EventId:"+sanitize(p.EventId,50)+" Title:"+sanitize(p.Title,100));
      return { status:"success" };
    } catch(err) {
      logAction(sanitize(p.AdminName,100)||"System", "ADD_EVENT_EXPENSE_ERROR", "EventId: " + sanitize(p.EventId||"",50) + " | Title: " + sanitize(p.Title||"",100), err.message, "", { severity:"ERROR", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
      return { status:"error", message:err.message };
    }
  }

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  BIRTHDAY EMAIL SYSTEM
//  sendBirthdayEmails(isTest, testUserId)
//    - Called daily at 8AM via Time-based trigger (set up manually in Apps Script)
//    - isTest=true + testUserId: sends to that specific user regardless of DOB
//    - isTest=true + no testUserId: sends to ALL users whose birthday is today
//    - isTest=false: respects birthday_email toggle, only sends on actual birthday
//  Uses tryConsumeEmailQuota() — counter increments on every send automatically.
//  Toggle key: birthday_email in SETTINGS sheet (1=ON, 0=OFF).
//  Daily trigger: Apps Script > Triggers > sendBirthdayEmails > Time-based > Day timer > 8AM
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function sendBirthdayEmails(isTest, testUserId) {
  const settings = getEmailSettings();

  // Respect toggle unless it's a manual test
  if (!isTest && !settings.birthday_email) {
    logAction("System", "birthdayEmail", "Skipped — birthday_email toggle is OFF");
    return { status: "skipped", message: "Birthday email toggle is OFF. Enable it in Email Settings." };
  }

  const allUsers = getSheetData(SHEETS.USERS);
  // Use IST (GMT+5:30) consistent with all other date ops in this codebase
  const _now    = new Date();
  const todayDD = Number(Utilities.formatDate(_now, "GMT+5:30", "d"));  // 1-31
  const todayMM = Number(Utilities.formatDate(_now, "GMT+5:30", "M"));  // 1-12

  let sent = 0, skipped = 0, noEmail = 0, errors = [];

  const candidates = allUsers.filter(function(u) {
    if (!u.DOB)                                                     return false;
    if (String(u.Status || "Active").toLowerCase() !== "active")   return false;
    if (String(u.Role   || "").toLowerCase()       === "admin")    return false;
    if (!u.Email || !String(u.Email).trim())                        return false;

    // ✅ FIX: Test mode with specific user — only that user
    if (isTest && testUserId) {
      return String(u.UserId) === String(testUserId);
    }

    // ✅ FIX: Non-test mode (daily trigger) — pre-filter by today's birthday here
    //         so the forEach loop skips everyone else without consuming quota or logging
    if (!isTest) {
      try {
        var dd, mm;
        if (u.DOB instanceof Date) {
          var istStr = Utilities.formatDate(u.DOB, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy");
          var p = istStr.split("-");
          dd = Number(p[0]); mm = Number(p[1]);
        } else {
          var dob = String(u.DOB || "").trim();
          if (/^\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[0]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
          else if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[2]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
          else return false;
        }
        return dd === todayDD && mm === todayMM;
      } catch(e) { return false; }
    }

    // isTest=true, no testUserId — still only send to today's birthday members
    try {
      var dd, mm;
      if (u.DOB instanceof Date) {
        var istStr = Utilities.formatDate(u.DOB, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy");
        var p = istStr.split("-"); dd = Number(p[0]); mm = Number(p[1]);
      } else {
        var dob = String(u.DOB || "").trim();
        if      (/^\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[0]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
        else if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[2]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
        else return false;
      }
      return dd === todayDD && mm === todayMM;
    } catch(e) { return false; }
  });

  candidates.forEach(function(u) {
    try {
      // Parse DOB — handles both Date objects (from Sheets date cells) and strings
      var dd, mm;
      if (u.DOB instanceof Date) {
        // ✅ FIX: Date object from Sheets — use IST local values, NOT getUTCDate()
        // Sheets returns midnight IST; getUTCDate() would give the previous day (timezone bug)
        var istStr = Utilities.formatDate(u.DOB, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MM-yyyy");
        var p = istStr.split("-");
        dd = Number(p[0]); mm = Number(p[1]);
      } else {
        var dob = String(u.DOB || "").trim();
        if      (/^\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[0]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
        else if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(dob)) { var p=dob.split("-"); dd=Number(p[2]); mm=Number(p[1]); }
        else { skipped++; return; } // unrecognised string format
      }

      // Non-test: only send on actual birthday
      if (!isTest && (dd !== todayDD || mm !== todayMM)) { skipped++; return; }

      // Quota guard — also increments counter atomically
      if (!tryConsumeEmailQuota()) {
        errors.push(u.Name + " — email quota exhausted for today");
        return;
      }

      MailApp.sendEmail({
        to:       String(u.Email).trim(),
        subject:  "🎂 " + CFG.name + " — जन्मदिन मुबारक हो, " + (u.Name||"").split(" ")[0] + " जी! 🎉",
        htmlBody: _buildBirthdayEmail(u)
      });

      logAction("System", "birthdayEmail",
        "Sent to " + u.Name + " <" + u.Email + ">" + (isTest ? " [TEST]" : ""));
      sent++;

    } catch(err) {
      errors.push((u.Name||u.UserId) + ": " + err.message);
      logAction("System", "BIRTHDAY_EMAIL_SEND_ERROR", "UserId: " + (u.UserId||"") + " | Name: " + (u.Name||"") + " | To: " + (u.Email||""), err.message, "", { severity:"WARN", result:"FAILURE", error:err });
    }
  });

  var summary = "sent:" + sent + ", skipped:" + skipped + (errors.length ? ", errors:" + errors.join("; ") : "");
  logAction("System", "birthdayEmailBatch", summary + (isTest ? " [TEST]" : ""));

  return {
    status:  errors.length > 0 && sent === 0 ? "error" : "success",
    sent:    sent,
    skipped: skipped,
    errors:  errors,
    message: isTest
      ? (sent > 0
          ? "✅ Test birthday email sent to " + sent + " member(s) successfully."
          : "⚠️ No matching member found — check user has Email + DOB saved.")
      : (sent > 0
          ? "🎂 " + sent + " birthday email(s) sent today."
          : "No birthdays today — no emails sent.")
  };
}

// ── Beautiful home-themed birthday HTML email ──────
function _buildBirthdayEmail(member) {
  var firstName = (member.Name || "Friend").split(" ")[0];
  var today     = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "dd MMMM yyyy");

  const body = `
  ${_emHeadSimple("Happy Birthday 🎂")}

  <tr><td style="padding:28px 32px;">
    <p style="color:${_EM.ink};font-size:14px;margin:0 0 14px;">Dear ${firstName} जी,</p>

    <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13.5px;line-height:1.85;margin:0 0 16px;">
      Wishing you a very Happy Birthday! 🎉 आपका यह दिन खुशियों, अच्छी सेहत और अपनों के साथ प्यार भरे
      पलों से भरा रहे।
    </p>

    <div style="background:${_EM.panel};border-left:3px solid ${_EM.brand};padding:16px 18px;margin:0 0 18px;">
      <p style="color:${_EM.sub};font-size:13px;line-height:1.8;margin:0;">
        On behalf of <strong style="color:${_EM.ink};">${CFG.name}</strong>, हम आपकी दीर्घायु,
        स्वास्थ्य और खुशहाली की कामना करते हैं। May the year ahead bring you much joy and success. 🌸
      </p>
    </div>

    <p style="color:${_EM.brand};font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.7;margin:0;font-style:italic;text-align:center;">
      जन्मदिन मुबारक हो — ${CFG.tagline} 🙏
    </p>
  </td></tr>

  ${_emFooterSimple("Sent to " + member.Email + " on " + today)}`;
  return _emShell(520, body);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  TRAFFIC COUNTER
//  Keys: TC_HOUR_2026-04-21T14  → count for that UTC+5:30 hour
//        TC_DAY_2026-04-21      → count for that IST day
//        TC_TOTAL               → all-time total
//        TC_PEAK_HOUR           → highest single-hour count ever
//        TC_PEAK_DAY            → highest single-day count ever
//        TC_ACTIONS             → JSON map of action → count
//
//  DAILY LIMIT: Change TC_DAILY_LIMIT to match your account:
//    20000  = Free Google account
//    100000 = Google Workspace account
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var TC_DAILY_LIMIT = 20000; // ← CHANGE THIS if you have Google Workspace (use 100000)

function _trackRequest(action) {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var now   = new Date();
    var ist   = new Date(now.getTime() + 5.5 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

    var dayKey  = "TC_DAY_"  + Utilities.formatDate(ist, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd");
    var hourKey = "TC_HOUR_" + Utilities.formatDate(ist, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH");

    // ── BATCHED: 1 read + 1 write = 2 PS calls/request (40,000/day at 20k requests)
    //    Safely under the 50,000/day PropertiesService quota for free accounts.
    //    Old code used 7 individual calls — would have failed after ~7,100 requests/day.
    var all = props.getProperties();

    var dayCount  = Number(all[dayKey]         || 0) + 1;
    var hourCount = Number(all[hourKey]        || 0) + 1;
    var total     = Number(all["TC_TOTAL"]     || 0) + 1;
    var peakHour  = Number(all["TC_PEAK_HOUR"] || 0);
    var peakDay   = Number(all["TC_PEAK_DAY"]  || 0);

    var updates = {};
    updates[dayKey]     = String(dayCount);
    updates[hourKey]    = String(hourCount);
    updates["TC_TOTAL"] = String(total);
    if (hourCount > peakHour) updates["TC_PEAK_HOUR"] = String(hourCount);
    if (dayCount  > peakDay)  updates["TC_PEAK_DAY"]  = String(dayCount);

    if (action) {
      try {
        var actMap = JSON.parse(all["TC_ACTIONS"] || "{}");
        actMap[action] = (actMap[action] || 0) + 1;
        updates["TC_ACTIONS"] = JSON.stringify(actMap);
      } catch(e) {}
    }

    props.setProperties(updates); // single write call
  } catch(e) { /* never crash the main request */ }
}

function getTrafficStats() {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var all   = props.getProperties();
    var now   = new Date();
    var ist   = new Date(now.getTime() + 5.5 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

    var hours = [];
    for (var h = 23; h >= 0; h--) {
      var t    = new Date(ist.getTime() - h * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      var key  = "TC_HOUR_" + Utilities.formatDate(t, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH");
      var label = Utilities.formatDate(t, "GMT+5:30", "HH:00");
      hours.push({ hour: label, count: Number(all[key] || 0) });
    }

    var days = [];
    for (var d = 13; d >= 0; d--) {
      var t2   = new Date(ist.getTime() - d * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      var key2 = "TC_DAY_" + Utilities.formatDate(t2, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd");
      var lbl2 = Utilities.formatDate(t2, "GMT+5:30", "dd MMM");
      days.push({ date: lbl2, count: Number(all[key2] || 0) });
    }

    var todayKey = "TC_DAY_"  + Utilities.formatDate(ist, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd");
    var thisHourKey = "TC_HOUR_" + Utilities.formatDate(ist, "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH");

    var actMap = {};
    try { actMap = JSON.parse(all["TC_ACTIONS"] || "{}"); } catch(e) {}
    var actions = Object.keys(actMap)
      .map(function(k) { return { action: k, count: actMap[k] }; })
      .sort(function(a, b) { return b.count - a.count; })
      .slice(0, 15);

    var todayCount = Number(all[todayKey] || 0);
    var dailyLimit = TC_DAILY_LIMIT;
    var usedPct    = Math.round(todayCount / dailyLimit * 100);

    // ── Email quota (reuse existing getEmailQuotaStatus)
    var emailQuota  = { used: 0, limit: 100, remaining: 100 };
    try { emailQuota = getEmailQuotaStatus(); } catch(e) {}
    var emailPct = Math.min(100, Math.round(emailQuota.used / Math.max(1, emailQuota.limit) * 100));

    return {
      status:       "ok",
      total:        Number(all["TC_TOTAL"]     || 0),
      today:        todayCount,
      thisHour:     Number(all[thisHourKey]    || 0),
      peakHour:     Number(all["TC_PEAK_HOUR"] || 0),
      peakDay:      Number(all["TC_PEAK_DAY"]  || 0),
      dailyLimit:   dailyLimit,
      usedPct:      usedPct,
      emailUsed:    emailQuota.used,
      emailLimit:   emailQuota.limit,
      emailPct:     emailPct,
      last24Hours:  hours,
      last14Days:   days,
      topActions:   actions,
      generatedAt:  Utilities.formatDate(ist, "GMT+5:30", "dd-MMM-yyyy HH:mm:ss") + " IST"
    };
  } catch(err) {
    return { status: "error", message: err.message };
  }
}

// ── Manual reset — clears all TC_ keys except TC_DAILY_LIMIT config
function resetTrafficStats() {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var all   = props.getProperties();
    var deleted = 0;
    Object.keys(all).forEach(function(k) {
      if (k.indexOf("TC_") === 0) {
        props.deleteProperty(k);
        deleted++;
      }
    });
    return { status: "ok", message: "Traffic stats reset. " + deleted + " keys cleared.", deleted: deleted };
  } catch(err) {
    return { status: "error", message: err.message };
  }
}

// ── Auto-clean old hour keys — run weekly via Time-based trigger (Sunday)
//    Prevents PropertiesService filling up after months of use
function cleanTrafficKeys() {
  try {
    var props  = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var all    = props.getProperties();
    var cutoff = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    Object.keys(all).forEach(function(k) {
      if (k.indexOf("TC_HOUR_") === 0) {
        var dateStr = k.replace("TC_HOUR_", "").split("T")[0];
        if (new Date(dateStr) < cutoff) props.deleteProperty(k);
      }
    });
  } catch(e) {}
}
